
-----title
鲁山 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='169b719112054c6aa38b4f270a41b548_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("169b719112054c6aa38b4f270a41b548");'><span id='169b719112054c6aa38b4f270a41b548_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=719&endYear=745')">719-745年</a>，1-27岁</div><div id='169b719112054c6aa38b4f270a41b548' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=719&endYear=719')">719年</a>　是年生于家乡鲁山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=720&endYear=734')">720-734年</a>　乡居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　乡居，始折节向学，事从兄德秀。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=745')">736-745年</a>　乡居读书向学。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b541aab0b7fb4618809447e4e04718b5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b541aab0b7fb4618809447e4e04718b5");'><span id='b541aab0b7fb4618809447e4e04718b5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>，29岁</div><div id='b541aab0b7fb4618809447e4e04718b5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　应试长安，下第，东归山余。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8f6e5d02536d4c4ba003b0ec5d6e380e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8f6e5d02536d4c4ba003b0ec5d6e380e");'><span id='8f6e5d02536d4c4ba003b0ec5d6e380e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=750&endYear=752')">750-752年</a>，32-34岁</div><div id='8f6e5d02536d4c4ba003b0ec5d6e380e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=750&endYear=750')">750年</a>　习静商余山，有说楚赋三篇。作品：《说楚何荒王赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（苏源明官河南令或即天宝九载，时元结方习静商余。苏对《说楚赋》有“子居今而作真淳之语，难哉”的感叹。）</span>《说楚何惑王赋》《说楚何惛王赋》<div id='poem_1367491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>说楚何荒王赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（上）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（750年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367491")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367491'>梁宠王召君史问曰。史之记事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367491_comment'></div>无有遗乎。对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367491_comment'></div>有之。臣楚人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367491_comment'></div>请说楚人之遗事。昔闻臣何荒王使钓翁相水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367491_comment'></div>相置浮宫之所。相用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>罛钓</span>之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367491_comment'></div>翁曰。臣相水多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367491_comment'></div>不能悉说。请说湘江之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367491_comment'></div>有砻有泷。其至险也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367491_comment'></div>实回山如斗。㩻壁若合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367491_comment'></div>阳崖阴壑。景气常杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367491_comment'></div>崩流激声。空响相答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367491_comment'></div>则有峮𡸙峻束。喷濆触沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367491_comment'></div>冲回瀪漩。圮崖开谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367491_comment'></div>故众声相喧。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>积气</span>相昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367491_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>鼘阗</span>深沈。出入千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367491_comment'></div>常如凝阴。是以鱼经其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367491_comment'></div>皆鬣秃鳞脱。眄腮嚅煦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367491_comment'></div>忽为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>渊流</span>。瀛瀛油油。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367491_comment'></div>蕴淳无声。岛屿若浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367491_comment'></div>则有厌波涛湍险之苦者。必于其閒养鳞让鬣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367491_comment'></div>休游施舒。如此之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367491_comment'></div>皆曰鱼都。君王审之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367491_comment'></div>无易此乎。荒王眺叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367491_comment'></div>钓翁皂父。其思隘欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367491_comment'></div>乃欲置吾于湘水一曲。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>钓罗</span>病鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367491_comment'></div>吾自相水洞庭可矣。于是命造<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>罛钓</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367491_comment'></div>于是命造浮宫。令<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>罛钓</span>所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367491_comment'></div>渊无藏龙。令浮宫所状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367491_comment'></div>与仙府比同。宫有天䑢龙殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367491_comment'></div>当居史端。实孁巫鬼祝女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367491_comment'></div>司宫侍何荒王。而公族国卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367491_comment'></div>莫得至焉。宫有艎台揭拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367491_comment'></div>类拟天都。薰珍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>钿涂</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367491_comment'></div>缨佩垂纡。金珠玉炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367491_comment'></div>萧漻清泠。苾馥芬敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367491_comment'></div>臣何荒王于此台上。与妊女嫭姝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367491_comment'></div>双歌闲徐。娭然自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367491_comment'></div>宫有艂堂𦨽房。䑦馆艨廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367491_comment'></div>载戏儿奴妓官。谐奴内臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367491_comment'></div>宫姥优倡。及玩器不名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367491_comment'></div>戙维宫傍。宫有联⿰<span class='inlineComment2'>（舟需）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367491_comment'></div>负土以为𦫃囿。囿多夭草媚木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367491_comment'></div>淫禽丑兽。宫有海之阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367491_comment'></div>仡倔解悬。左曰瑞风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367491_comment'></div>右曰祥烟。宫有四门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367491_comment'></div>青气白云。丹景元寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367491_comment'></div>然后始为鹢城。匝宫屯备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367491_comment'></div>交战禁御。𡹚罗攒峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367491_comment'></div>其馀骇鲸之艆。飞龙之舫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367491_comment'></div>凫艋鹤𦩿。罗宫上下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367491_comment'></div>千里相望。浮宫可御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367491_comment'></div>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/102/Comments/0")'>罛钓</span>无成。臣何荒王乃浮浮宫于都龙之漩泠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367491_comment'></div>出洞庭之南渶。将观蛮师夷人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367491_comment'></div>与渔者试<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>罛钓</span>于沅湘会浘。臣何荒王始见积鱼之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367491_comment'></div>而喜色未起。及见罘犹畜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367491_comment'></div>委钓未施。已潆洄渊洑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367491_comment'></div>周袤千里。罛中之鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367491_comment'></div>皆触蹙锻骇。投跳委垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367491_comment'></div>可以荐车。臣何荒王辇于其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367491_comment'></div>而心始喜。是日置鱼监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367491_comment'></div>拜网尉。钓尹司纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367491_comment'></div>各有等次。又有类龙学鳇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367491_comment'></div>肘钓䏶剑。鹏腾鹗跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367491_comment'></div>潜深错𢱢。得怪鱼状龙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367491_comment'></div>皆差授官爵。宠王闻之喜曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367491_comment'></div>吾国无有长流激湍。平湘大渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367491_comment'></div>而不知有此乐也。始知城池宫馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367491_comment'></div>为拘我之邸。山泽鹰犬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367491_comment'></div>为劳我之方。当诵记所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367491_comment'></div>归学而主。君史证曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367491_comment'></div>不然。须臣言已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367491_comment'></div>或可听焉。臣闻浮宫之成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367491_comment'></div>臣何荒王令群臣。有后为浮司不为浮茅者族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367491_comment'></div>百姓能率为浮家共为浮乡者复。男子能湍游上下者为王宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367491_comment'></div>女子能渊居移日者为王嫔。未及一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367491_comment'></div>遂变楚俗。川原有楚室之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367491_comment'></div>江湖有骈舟之曲。家见湍上之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367491_comment'></div>户闻临渊之哭。时野有叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367491_comment'></div>呜呼。有国者非喜爱亡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367491_comment'></div>有家者非喜爱亡家。当取其亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367491_comment'></div>如喜爱者耶。今君上喜爱浮宫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_80_1367491", 1367491, "Clauses/161/Comments/0")'>罛钓</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367491_comment'></div>令臣下喜爱浮司浮乡。吾恐君臣各迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367491_comment'></div>而家国共亡。此实楚正士叹臣何荒王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367491_comment'></div>臣愿君王惊惧为心。指此为箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367491_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_84_1367491_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>说楚何惑王赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（中）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（750年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367492")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367492'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367492'>宠王聥然。复问君史曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367492_comment'></div>更有记乎。曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367492_comment'></div>有之。甚妖怪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367492_comment'></div>何故不说。宠王曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367492_comment'></div>当必为吾说之。对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367492_comment'></div>臣闻天鄙有山。山有玉鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367492_comment'></div>实有天𩵀。扣之歌舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367492_comment'></div>声媚金石。韵便宫羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367492_comment'></div>宠王曰。生休矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367492_comment'></div>吾将购之。君史证曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367492_comment'></div>不可。臣所不欲说者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367492_comment'></div>惧君王好之。君诚不忘欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367492_comment'></div>臣请备说。其可好乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367492_comment'></div>昔臣何惑王用阍嬖之谋。肆极荒淫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367492_comment'></div>更经年岁。凿险填深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367492_comment'></div>转馈通千里。万金五译。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367492_comment'></div>臣妾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1367492", 1367492, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>借喻</span>其心。然后云获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367492_comment'></div>非孁女抚鼓。而天𩵀不舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367492_comment'></div>非孁女引和。而天𩵀不歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367492_comment'></div>天𩵀舞。一容化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367492_comment'></div>一分眄。一祥襜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367492_comment'></div>一宛袂。臣何惑王见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367492_comment'></div>舒舒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1367492", 1367492, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>曳曳</span>。若多醇酎而不知所制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367492_comment'></div>天𩵀歌。一化颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367492_comment'></div>一主顾。一更声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367492_comment'></div>一换气。臣何惑王听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367492_comment'></div>娭娭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1367492", 1367492, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>懿懿</span>。若已酎昏而不知所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367492_comment'></div>天𩵀歌舞。臣何惑王气如阳春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367492_comment'></div>始霁时雨。天𩵀不歌舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367492_comment'></div>臣何惑王心若已丧。而颓坏不主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367492_comment'></div>呜呼天𩵀。惑人至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367492_comment'></div>呜呼天𩵀。媚人至斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367492_comment'></div>如有𩵀顮。甡甡辅之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367492_comment'></div>使臣何惑王之心无所不欲。使臣何惑王之意无所不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367492_comment'></div>独言选女。于馀可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367492_comment'></div>其选女也。岂止嫈㜲美嫭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367492_comment'></div>及孁未笄。将龉将齯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367492_comment'></div>将嬩将嫛。可喜美者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367492_comment'></div>母姨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1367492", 1367492, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>负抱</span>。姑姊引提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367492_comment'></div>诣于王宫。字籍王闺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367492_comment'></div>然后割楚国庙右。为天𩵀作宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367492_comment'></div>分楚国社阳。为𩵀顮作馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367492_comment'></div>悉楚国之好。奉之已穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367492_comment'></div>于所奉之心。其犹未满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367492_comment'></div>楚国之人。已悲咨冤怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367492_comment'></div>日苦其毒。其臣何惑王尚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1367492", 1367492, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>熙恞</span>敷娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367492_comment'></div>日思未足。野有直士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367492_comment'></div>触而证曰。大王溺于天𩵀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367492_comment'></div>惑于𩵀顮。不顾宗庙遂亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367492_comment'></div>人民如何。下命其令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367492_comment'></div>且云舞者能变一度。歌者能变一声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367492_comment'></div>应𩵀乐之节数。充寡人之性情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367492_comment'></div>且能富其亲族。又能贵其父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367492_comment'></div>至于母姨姑姊。皆能与之封邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367492_comment'></div>以为世荣。令行逾月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367492_comment'></div>楚俗皆化。女忘蚕织。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367492_comment'></div>男忘耕稼。里开学歌之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367492_comment'></div>乡筑教舞之榭。遂使黄钟大吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367492_comment'></div>生溺惑之声。孤竹空桑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367492_comment'></div>起怨离之调。变风俗于一欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367492_comment'></div>忘正始于一笑。大王未觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367492_comment'></div>遂不节损。此所谓凿颠覆之源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367492_comment'></div>造乱亡之本。今之所好则妖恶之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367492_comment'></div>所为又怪丑之事。羲轩之耳必不肯听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367492_comment'></div>尧禹之心必不肯喜。臣何惑王悟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367492_comment'></div>于是使嬖臣挟玉鼓与𩵀乐。使阍尹抱天孁𩵀顮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367492_comment'></div>锁以金索。系于石人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367492_comment'></div>沈之深渊。飞楫而旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367492_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1367492_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367493' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367493' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367493?labeling=true' target='_blank'>说楚何惛王赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（下）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（750年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367493")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367493_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367493'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367493'>宠王曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367493_comment'></div>殆哉楚国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367493_comment'></div>几为浮宫𩵀乐所亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367493_comment'></div>君史曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367493_comment'></div>几亡楚国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367493_comment'></div>有甚于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367493_comment'></div>昔臣何惛王极暴极虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367493_comment'></div>使臣下得肆奸肆佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367493_comment'></div>肆凶肆恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367493_comment'></div>臣何惛王不知如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367493_comment'></div>亡可待矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367493_comment'></div>而乃叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367493_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367493_comment'></div>尧实皂帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367493_comment'></div>禹实隶王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367493_comment'></div>殷周君长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367493_comment'></div>并夫可方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367493_comment'></div>焉有惨然劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367493_comment'></div>而为人主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367493_comment'></div>焉有隘然九州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367493_comment'></div>而裂封诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367493_comment'></div>吾必合外荒夷狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367493_comment'></div>海内人民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367493_comment'></div>悉奉我为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367493_comment'></div>欲世世臣臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367493_comment'></div>此臣何惛王所云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367493_comment'></div>又谋变先王之典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367493_comment'></div>更万物之名号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367493_comment'></div>列宫官于海外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367493_comment'></div>穷天地而遍到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367493_comment'></div>而复思稽极变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367493_comment'></div>徵验怪异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367493_comment'></div>尽难得之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367493_comment'></div>充无穷之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367493_comment'></div>荒娱厌怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367493_comment'></div>思计所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367493_comment'></div>度国土之不大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367493_comment'></div>料财力之不支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367493_comment'></div>乃令人曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367493_comment'></div>吾欲劳汝人民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367493_comment'></div>休汝人民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367493_comment'></div>汝人民岂知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367493_comment'></div>今悉汝丁壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367493_comment'></div>妇人继之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367493_comment'></div>童翁分力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367493_comment'></div>负载而随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367493_comment'></div>我已老谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367493_comment'></div>我已名师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367493_comment'></div>人民听我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367493_comment'></div>当无二思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367493_comment'></div>所举既甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367493_comment'></div>所资不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367493_comment'></div>乃署官而贾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367493_comment'></div>钳孤而鬻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367493_comment'></div>始令国中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367493_comment'></div>绝人谤讟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367493_comment'></div>赞谋者侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367493_comment'></div>敢谏者族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367493_comment'></div>其令朝行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367493_comment'></div>其俗暮改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367493_comment'></div>有以逃罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367493_comment'></div>正言不发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367493_comment'></div>万口如封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367493_comment'></div>谄媚相与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367493_comment'></div>千颜一容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367493_comment'></div>野有忠臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367493_comment'></div>负符矫谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367493_comment'></div>伪为齐客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367493_comment'></div>绐而证曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367493_comment'></div>臣入君王之封域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367493_comment'></div>见君王之风化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367493_comment'></div>踟蹰路隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367493_comment'></div>不觉泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367493_comment'></div>或闻哀号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367493_comment'></div>或闻悲呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367493_comment'></div>讯于闾里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367493_comment'></div>必鳏寡茕孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367493_comment'></div>或见凶侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367493_comment'></div>或见骄奢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367493_comment'></div>讯于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367493_comment'></div>必公侯之家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367493_comment'></div>客说未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367493_comment'></div>臣何惛王曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367493_comment'></div>然乎谓何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367493_comment'></div>对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367493_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367493_comment'></div>君王不知忠正不植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367493_comment'></div>奸佞骈生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367493_comment'></div>能焇㱠仁惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367493_comment'></div>冒盖聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367493_comment'></div>令巧媚得口为矛戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367493_comment'></div>令奸凶得心为甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367493_comment'></div>此皆明迹甚于鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367493_comment'></div>发机有若雷霆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367493_comment'></div>实畏君王已刍于牢圈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367493_comment'></div>实恐君王已暴夫乾枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367493_comment'></div>君王如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367493_comment'></div>不是念乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367493_comment'></div>臣恐楚国化为荒野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1367493_comment'></div>臣恐君臣不如犬马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1367493_comment'></div>臣何惛王于是眄容而惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1367493_comment'></div>抚身而哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1367493_comment'></div>仰为客曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1367493_comment'></div>君幸怜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1367493_comment'></div>得无戒哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1367493_comment'></div>君为臣化心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1367493_comment'></div>心化身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367493_comment'></div>身化化人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367493_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1367493_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1367493", 1367493, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>递化</span>之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1367493_comment'></div>在制于内外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1367493_comment'></div>外之入也有视听言闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1367493_comment'></div>内之出也有性情嗜欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1367493_comment'></div>出入相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1367493_comment'></div>必有祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1367493_comment'></div>臣何惛王闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1367493_comment'></div>宴居化心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1367493_comment'></div>讽诵斯言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1367493_comment'></div>终身为箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1367493_comment'></div>遂罢已成之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1367493_comment'></div>寝未成之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1367493_comment'></div>废所贾之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1367493_comment'></div>复所鬻之孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1367493_comment'></div>敢谏者侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1367493_comment'></div>赞谋者诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1367493_comment'></div>君史言已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1367493_comment'></div>王客捧酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1367493_comment'></div>为宠王寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1367493_comment'></div>起而赞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1367493_comment'></div>君史说楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1367493_comment'></div>似欲戒梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1367493_comment'></div>敢愿君王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1367493_comment'></div>示鉴不忘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_132_1367493_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=751&endYear=751')">751年</a>　习静商余山，有诗。作品：《系乐府十二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：系乐府序有“天宝辛未中”天宝中无辛未年，恐为“辛卯”之误。）</span><div id='poem_6079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>系乐府十二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>思太古</a><span class='authorDate'>（751年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6079")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6079_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6079'>天宝辛未中，元子将前世尝可称叹者，为诗十二篇，为引其义以名之，总命曰〈系乐府〉。古人咏歌不尽其情声者，化金石以尽之，其欢怨甚邪戏尽欢欢怨之声音，可以上感于上，下化于下，故元子系之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6079'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6079'>东南三千里，沅湘为太湖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6079'>湖上山谷深，有人多似愚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6079'>婴孩寄树颠，就水捕鷠<span class='inlineComment2'>（于都切）</span>鲈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6079'>所欢同鸟兽，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_6079", 6079, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>身意</span>复何拘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6079'>吾行遍九州，此风皆已无。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6079'>吁嗟圣贤教，不觉久踌蹰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6079'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_6079_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6077' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6077' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6077?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>陇上叹</a><span class='authorDate'>（751年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6077_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6077'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6077'>援车登陇坂，穷高遂停驾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6077'>延望戎狄乡，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_6077", 6077, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>巡回</span>复悲咤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6077'>滋移有情教，草木犹可化。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6077'>圣贤礼让风，何不遍西夏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6077'>父子忍猜害，君臣敢欺诈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6077'>所适今若斯，悠悠欲安舍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6077_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6077'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_6077_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6081' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6081' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6081?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>颂东夷</a><span class='authorDate'>（751年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6081_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6081'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6081'>尝闻古天子，朝会张新乐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6081'>金石无全声，宫商乱清浊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6081'>东<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作来）</span>惊且悲叹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_6081", 6081, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>节变</span>何烦数。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6081'>始知中国人，耽此亡纯朴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6081'>尔为外方客，何为独能觉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6081'>其音若或在，蹈海吾将学。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6081_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6081'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_6081_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6080?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>贱士吟</a><span class='authorDate'>（751年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6080_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6080'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6080'>南风发天和，和气天下流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6080'>能使万物荣，不能变羁愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6080'>为愁亦何尔，自请说此由。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6080'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_6080", 6080, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>谄竞</span>实多路，苟邪皆共求。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6080'>尝闻古君子，指以为深羞。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6080'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_6080", 6080, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>正方</span>终莫可，江海有沧洲。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6080'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_6080_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6082' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6082' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_6072'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6072'>下客无黄金，岂思主人怜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6072'>客言胜黄金，主人然不然。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6072'>珠玉成<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作诚）</span>彩翠，绮罗如婵娟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6072'>终恐见斯好，有时去君前。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6072'>岂知保忠信，长使令德全。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6072'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_6072", 6072, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>风声</span>与时茂，歌颂万千年。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6072_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6072'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_6072_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　习静商余山，有自述文三篇。作品：《自述三篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：据《自述序》，天宝十一年作《述时》、《述命》2篇，并前所作《述居》，总命曰《自述》）</span><div id='poem_1367610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自述三篇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>述时</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367610")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367610_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367610'>天宝庚寅。元子初习静于商馀。人闻之非。非曰。此狂者也。见则茫然。无几。人闻之是。是曰。此学者也。见则猗然。及三年。人闻之参。参曰。此隐者也。见则崖然。有惑而问曰。子其隐乎。曰。吾岂隐者邪。愚者也。穷而然尔。或者不喻。遂为述时命以辩之。先曾为述居一篇。因刊而次之。总命曰自述。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367610'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367610'>昔隋氏逆天地之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367610_comment'></div>绝生人之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367610_comment'></div>使怨痛之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367610_comment'></div>满于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367610_comment'></div>四海之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367610_comment'></div>隋人未老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367610_comment'></div>隋社未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367610_comment'></div>而隋国已亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367610_comment'></div>何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367610_comment'></div>奢淫暴虐昏惑而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367610_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1367610", 1367610, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>烝人</span>苦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367610_comment'></div>上诉皇天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367610_comment'></div>皇天有命于我国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367610_comment'></div>六叶于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367610_comment'></div>高皇至勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367610_comment'></div>文皇至明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367610_comment'></div>身鉴隋室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367610_comment'></div>不敢满溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367610_comment'></div>清俭之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367610_comment'></div>听察之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367610_comment'></div>仁惠之极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367610_comment'></div>泱泱洋洋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367610_comment'></div>为万代则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367610_comment'></div>圣皇承之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367610_comment'></div>不言而化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367610_comment'></div>四十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367610_comment'></div>天下太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367610_comment'></div>礼乐化于戎夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367610_comment'></div>慈惠及于草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367610_comment'></div>虽奴隶齿类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367610_comment'></div>亦能诵周公孔父之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367610_comment'></div>说陶唐虞夏之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367610_comment'></div>至于歌颂讴吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367610_comment'></div>妇人童子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367610_comment'></div>皆纾性情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367610_comment'></div>美辞韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367610_comment'></div>指咏时物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367610_comment'></div>与丝竹谐会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367610_comment'></div>绮罗当称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367610_comment'></div>况世贵之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367610_comment'></div>博学君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367610_comment'></div>其文学声望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367610_comment'></div>安得不显闻于当时也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367610_comment'></div>故冠冕之士倾当时大利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367610_comment'></div>轩车之士富当时大农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367610_comment'></div>由此知官不胜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367610_comment'></div>逸于司领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367610_comment'></div>使秩次不能损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367610_comment'></div>又休罢以抑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367610_comment'></div>尚骈肩累趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367610_comment'></div>受任不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367610_comment'></div>予愚愚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367610_comment'></div>亦尝预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367610_comment'></div>日觉抵塞厌于无用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367610_comment'></div>乃以因慕古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367610_comment'></div>清和蕴纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367610_comment'></div>周周仲仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367610_comment'></div>瘱然全真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367610_comment'></div>上全忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367610_comment'></div>下尽仁信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367610_comment'></div>内顺元化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367610_comment'></div>外娭太和足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367610_comment'></div>如戚促蚩诸封蒙遏灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367610_comment'></div>暮为朝贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367610_comment'></div>心所不喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367610_comment'></div>亦由金可镕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367610_comment'></div>不可使为污腐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367610_comment'></div>水可浊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367610_comment'></div>不可使为尘粪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367610_comment'></div>然已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367610_comment'></div>鄙语曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367610_comment'></div>愚者似直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367610_comment'></div>弱者似仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367610_comment'></div>子殆有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367610_comment'></div>夫复何疑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1367610_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367611' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367611' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367611?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>述命</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367611_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367611'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367611'>元子尝问命于清惠先生。先生曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367611_comment'></div>子欲知命不如平心。平心不如忘情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367611_comment'></div>喏曰。幸先生教之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367611_comment'></div>先生曰。夫平心能正是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367611_comment'></div>忘情能灭有无。子何先焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367611_comment'></div>曰。请先忘情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367611_comment'></div>先生曰。子见草木乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367611_comment'></div>子见天地乎。草木无心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367611_comment'></div>天地无情也。而四时自化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367611_comment'></div>雨露自均。根柢自深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367611_comment'></div>枝干自茂。如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367611_comment'></div>天地岂丑授而成哉。草木岂忧求而生哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367611_comment'></div>人之命也。亦由是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367611_comment'></div>若夭若寿。若贵若贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367611_comment'></div>乌可强哉。不可强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367611_comment'></div>不可强也。不如忘情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367611_comment'></div>忘情当学草木。呜呼上皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367611_comment'></div>强化天下。天下化之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367611_comment'></div>养之以道德。道德伪薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367611_comment'></div>天下亦从而伪薄。呜呼后王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367611_comment'></div>急济天下。天下从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367611_comment'></div>救之以权宜。权宜侈恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367611_comment'></div>天下亦从而侈恶。故赴贪徇纷急之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367611_comment'></div>以至于今。圣贤者兢兢然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367611_comment'></div>犹伤命性。愚惑者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1367611", 1367611, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>慁慁</span>然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367611_comment'></div>遂忘家国。其由不审不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367611_comment'></div>丑授忧求而已。子不喻乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367611_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1367611_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367612?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>述居</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367612'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367612'>天宝庚寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367612_comment'></div>元子得商馀之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367612_comment'></div>山东有谷曰馀中谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367612_comment'></div>东有山曰少馀山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367612_comment'></div>谷中有田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367612_comment'></div>可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1367612", 1367612, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>耕艺</span>者三数夫<span class='inlineComment2'>（一夫百亩）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367612_comment'></div>有泉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1367612", 1367612, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>停浸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367612_comment'></div>可畦稻者数十亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367612_comment'></div>泉东南合肥溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367612_comment'></div>溪源在少馀山下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367612_comment'></div>溪流出谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367612_comment'></div>与潨水合汇于滍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367612_comment'></div>将成所居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367612_comment'></div>故人李才闻而来会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367612_comment'></div>乃叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367612_comment'></div>吾未始知夫子之所至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367612_comment'></div>今知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367612_comment'></div>吾闻在贫思富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367612_comment'></div>在贱思贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367612_comment'></div>人之常情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367612_comment'></div>圣贤所有然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367612_comment'></div>而知贫贱不可苟免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367612_comment'></div>富贵不可苟取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367612_comment'></div>上顺时命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367612_comment'></div>乘道御和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367612_comment'></div>下守虚澹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367612_comment'></div>修已推分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367612_comment'></div>称君子者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367612_comment'></div>始不忝乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367612_comment'></div>乃相与占山泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367612_comment'></div>辟榛莽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367612_comment'></div>依山腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367612_comment'></div>近泉源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367612_comment'></div>始为亭庑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367612_comment'></div>始作堂宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367612_comment'></div>因而习静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367612_comment'></div>适自保闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367612_comment'></div>夫人生于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367612_comment'></div>如行长道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367612_comment'></div>所行有极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367612_comment'></div>而道无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367612_comment'></div>奔走不停。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367612_comment'></div>夫然何适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367612_comment'></div>予当乘时和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367612_comment'></div>望年丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367612_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1367612", 1367612, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>耕艺</span>山田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367612_comment'></div>兼备药石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367612_comment'></div>与兄弟承欢于膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367612_comment'></div>与朋友和乐于琴酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367612_comment'></div>寥然顺命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367612_comment'></div>不为物累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367612_comment'></div>亦自得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367612_comment'></div>分在于此也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1367612_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　习静商余山，有文。作品：《七不如篇》《自箴》<div id='poem_1367553' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367553' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367553?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自箴</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367553")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367553_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367553'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367553'>有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1367553", 1367553, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>时士</span>教元子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1367553", 1367553, "Clauses/0/Comments/1")'>显身</span>之道曰，于时不争。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367553'>无以显荣，与世不佞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367553'>终身自病，君欲求权。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367553'>须曲须圆，君欲求位。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367553'>须奸须媚，不能此为。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367553'>穷贱勿辞，元子对曰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367553'>不能此为，乃吾之心。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367553'>反君之言，作我自箴。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367553'>与时仁让，人不汝上。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367553'>处世<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1367553", 1367553, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>清介</span>，人不汝害。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367553'>汝若全德，必忠必直。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367553'>汝若全行，必方必正。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1367553'>终身如此，可谓君子。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1367553_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1367553'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1367553_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　习静商余山，有诗。作品：《演兴四首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：《演兴》四首、《七不如篇》、《自箴》皆天宝十二载以前，习静商山时作。）</span><div id='poem_6130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6130?labeling=true' target='_blank'>演兴四首 招太灵</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6130")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6130_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6130'>商馀山有太灵古祠，传云豢龙氏祠大帝所立，祠在少馀西乳之下，邑人修之以祈田，予因为招词讼闵之文以演兴。</div><div id='poem_preface_6130_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6130'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6130'>招太灵兮山之巅，山屹𡵉兮水沦涟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6130'>祠之襰<span class='inlineComment2'>（音赖，坠坏也）</span>兮眇何年，木修修兮草鲜鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6130'>嗟魑魅兮淫厉，自古昔兮崇祭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6130'>禧太灵兮端清，予愿致夫精诚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6130'>久惄兮㤝㤝，招捃𢹝兮呼风。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6130'>风之声兮起飔飔，吹玄云兮散而浮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6130'>望太灵兮俨而安，澹油溶兮都清闲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6130_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6130'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_6130_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6128?labeling=true' target='_blank'>演兴四首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>初祀</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span
