class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6128_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6128'>商馀山有太灵古祠，传云豢龙氏祠大帝所立，祠在少馀西乳之下，邑人修之以祈田，予因为招词讼闵之文以演兴。</div><div id='poem_preface_6128_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6128'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6128'>山之乳兮葺太祠，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6128", 6128, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>木孙</span>为桷兮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6128", 6128, "Clauses/1/Comments/1")'>木母</span>榱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6128'>云缨为𣔺兮愚木栭，洞渊禅兮揭巍巍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6128'>涂木兰兮莳糅蔫，被弱草兮禘礿联。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6128'>仡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_6128", 6128, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>浑洪</span>兮馥阗阗，管化石兮洞刳天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6128'>翘修钐<span class='inlineComment2'>（山鉴切，大镰也）</span>兮掉芜殳，灵巫𧮢<span class='inlineComment2'>（力水切）</span>兮舞颙干。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6128'>荐天𩷨兮酒阳泉，献<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_6128", 6128, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>水芸</span>兮饭霜籼，与太灵兮千万年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_6128_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6127?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>讼木魅<span class='inlineComment2'>（第二十句缺一字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6127'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6127'>登高峰兮俯幽谷，心悴悴兮念群木。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6127'>见樗栲兮相阴覆，怜梫榕兮不丰茂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6127'>见榛梗之森梢，闵枞橎兮合蠹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6127'>槢<span class='inlineComment2'>（音习）</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_6127", 6127, "Clauses/6/Comments/1")'>桡桡</span>兮未坚，椲桹桹兮可屈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6127'>樒<span class='inlineComment2'>（音密，香木）</span>林樽兮不香，拔丰茸兮已实。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6127'>岂元化之不均兮，非雨露之偏殊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6127'>谅理性之不等于顺时兮，不如瘗吾心以冥想。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6127'>终念此兮不怡，佁予莫识天地之意兮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6127'>愿截恶木之根，倾枭獍之古巢。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6127'>取囗童以为薪，割大木使飞焰。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6127'>徯枯腐之烧焚，实非吾心之不仁惠也。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6127'>岂耻夫善恶之相纷，且欲畚三河之膏壤。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6127'>裨济水之清涟，将封灌乎善木。<div id='poem_sentence_12_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_6127'>令<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_6127", 6127, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>橚橚</span>以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_6127", 6127, "Clauses/26/Comments/1")'>梴梴</span>，尚畏乎众善之未茂兮。<div id='poem_sentence_13_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_6127'>为众恶之所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_6127", 6127, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>挑凌</span>，思聚义以为曹。<div id='poem_sentence_14_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_6127'>令敷扶以相胜，取方所以柯如兮。<div id='poem_sentence_15_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_6127'>吾将出于南荒，求寿藤与蟠木。<div id='poem_sentence_16_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_6127'>吾将出于东方，祈有德而来归。<div id='poem_sentence_17_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_6127'>辅神柽与坚香，且忧颙之翩翩。<div id='poem_sentence_18_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_6127'>又愁㺠<span class='inlineComment2'>（同狖）</span>之奔驰，及阴阳兮不和。<div id='poem_sentence_19_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_6127'>恶此土之失时，今神柽兮不茂。<div id='poem_sentence_20_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_6127'>使坚香兮不滋，重嗟惋兮何补。<div id='poem_sentence_21_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_6127'>每齐心以精意，切援祝于神明。<div id='poem_sentence_22_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_6127'>冀感通于天地，犹恐众妖兮木魅。<div id='poem_sentence_23_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_6127'>魍魉兮山精，山误惑于灵心。<div id='poem_sentence_24_6127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_6127'>经绐于言兮不听，敢引佩以指水，誓吾心兮自明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_6127_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6129?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>闵岭中<span class='inlineComment2'>（首句缺一字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6129'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6129'>囗群山以延想，吾独闵乎岭中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6129'>彼岭中兮何有，有天含之玉峰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6129'>殊<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_6129", 6129, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>閟绝</span>之极颠，上闻产乎翠茸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6129'>欲采之以将寿，眇不知夫所从。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6129'>大渊蕴蕴兮绝嶘岌岌，非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_6129", 6129, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>梯梁</span>以通险。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6129'>当无路兮可入，彼猛毒兮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_6129", 6129, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>曹聚</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6129'>必凭托乎阻修，常<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_6129", 6129, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>儗儗</span>兮伺人。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6129'>又如何兮不愁，彼妖精兮变怪。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6129'>必假见于风雨，常闪闪而伺人。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6129'>又如何兮不苦，欲仗仁兮托信。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6129'>将径往兮不难，久懹懹以㥄惋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6129'>却迟回而永叹，惧大灵兮不知。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6129'>以予心为永惟，若不可乎遂已。<div id='poem_sentence_12_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_6129'>吾终保夫直方，则必蒙皮篻<span class='inlineComment2'>（莫遥切）</span>以为矢。<div id='poem_sentence_13_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_6129'>弦毋筱<span class='inlineComment2'>（筱同）</span>以为弧，化毒铜以为戟。<div id='poem_sentence_14_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_6129'>刺棘竹以为殳，得猛烈之材。<div id='poem_sentence_15_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_6129'>获与之而并驱，且舂刺乎恶毒。<div id='poem_sentence_16_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_6129'>又引射夫妖怪，尽群类兮使无。<div id='poem_sentence_17_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_6129'>令善仁<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作人）</span>兮不害，然后采梫榕以驾深。<div id='poem_sentence_18_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_6129'>收枞橞兮梯险，跻予身之飘飘。<div id='poem_sentence_19_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_6129'>承予步之𨁹𨁹，入岭中而登玉峰。<div id='poem_sentence_20_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_6129'>极<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_6129", 6129, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>閟绝</span>而求翠茸，将吾寿兮随所从。<div id='poem_sentence_21_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_6129'>思未得兮马如龙，独翳蔽于山颠。<div id='poem_sentence_22_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_6129'>久低回而愠瘀，空仰讼<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作诉）</span>于上玄。<div id='poem_sentence_23_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_6129'>彼至精兮必应，宁古有而今无。<div id='poem_sentence_24_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_6129'>将与身而皆亡，岂言之而已乎。<div id='poem_sentence_25_6129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_6129'></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_6129_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　习静商余山，有文。作品：《心规》《戏规》《处规》《恶圆》《恶曲》《水乐说》《订司乐氏》《浪翁观化4篇》《时化》《世化》<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品：据颜鲁公《元君表墓碑铭》引结《自释》“少习静商余山，著《元子》十卷”，疑《心规》《戏规》《处规》，及《恶圆》《恶曲》《水乐说》《订司乐氏》《浪翁观化》《时化》《世化》等皆《元子》中篇目。）</span><div id='poem_1367584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367584?labeling=true' target='_blank'>心规</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367584")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367584'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367584'>元子病游世。归于商馀之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367584_comment'></div>以酒自肆。有醉歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367584_comment'></div>里夫公闻之。𮠨元子之酒请歌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367584_comment'></div>歌曰。元子乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367584_comment'></div>俾和者曰。何乐亦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367584_comment'></div>何乐亦然。我曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367584_comment'></div>我云我山。我林我泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367584_comment'></div>又曰。元子乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367584_comment'></div>俾和者曰。何乐然尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367584_comment'></div>何乐然尔。我曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367584_comment'></div>我鼻我目。我口我耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367584_comment'></div>歌已矣。夫公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367584_comment'></div>自乐山林可也。自乐耳目何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367584_comment'></div>人谁无此。元子引酒当夫公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367584_comment'></div>劝君此杯酒。缓饮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367584_comment'></div>听我说。子行于世间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367584_comment'></div>目不随人视。耳不随人听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367584_comment'></div>口不随人语。鼻不随人气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367584_comment'></div>其甚也。则须封苞裹塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367584_comment'></div>不尔。有灭身亡家之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367584_comment'></div>伤污毁辱之患生焉。虽王公大人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367584_comment'></div>亦不能自主口鼻耳目。夫公何思之不熟耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367584_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1367584_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367583?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戏规</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367583")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367583'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367583'>元子友倚于云邱之巅。戏牧儿曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367583_comment'></div>尔为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1367583", 1367583, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>牧歌</span>。当不责尔暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367583_comment'></div>牧儿歌去。乃暴他田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367583_comment'></div>田主鞭之。啼而冤元子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367583_comment'></div>啼不止。召其父而止之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367583_comment'></div>元子友真卿闻之。书过于元子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367583_comment'></div>嗟嗟次山。苟戏小儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367583_comment'></div>俾陷鞭焉。而蒙冤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367583_comment'></div>彼牧儿望次山。犹儓隶不敢干其主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367583_comment'></div>及苟戏。乃或与次山犹仇雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367583_comment'></div>斯岂慎德也欤。吾闻君子不苟戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367583_comment'></div>无似非。如何惑一儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367583_comment'></div>使不知所以蒙过。此非苟戏似非之非者邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367583_comment'></div>恶不必易此。元子报真卿曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367583_comment'></div>于戏。吾独立于空山之上戏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367583_comment'></div>牧儿得过。几不可免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367583_comment'></div>彼行于世上。有爱憎相忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367583_comment'></div>是非相反。名利相夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367583_comment'></div>祸福相从。至于有蒙戮辱者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367583_comment'></div>得不因苟戏似非。世儿惑之以及者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367583_comment'></div>真卿。吾当以戏为规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367583_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1367583_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367582' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367582' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367582?labeling=true' target='_blank'>处规</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367582")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367582_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367582'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367582'>州舒吾问元子曰。吾闻子多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367582_comment'></div>意将何为。对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367582_comment'></div>云山幸不求吾是。林泉又不责吾非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367582_comment'></div>熙然能自全。顺时而老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367582_comment'></div>可矣。复安为哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367582_comment'></div>舒吾曰。元子其过误乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367582_comment'></div>其太矫也。吾厌世人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1367582", 1367582, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>饰言</span>以由道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367582_comment'></div>藏智以全璞。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1367582", 1367582, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>退身</span>以显行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367582_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1367582", 1367582, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>设机</span>以树名。吾子由之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367582_comment'></div>使我何信。元子俛而谢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367582_comment'></div>滕许大夫友元子。闻不应舒吾之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367582_comment'></div>乃曰。嗟嗟元子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367582_comment'></div>少辞者邪。何不曰使吾得所处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367582_comment'></div>但如山林。不见吾是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367582_comment'></div>吾将娭而往也。以子为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1367582", 1367582, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>饰言</span>藏智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367582_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1367582", 1367582, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>退身</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1367582", 1367582, "Clauses/30/Comments/1")'>设机</span>。何不曰如此岂不多于盗权窃位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367582_comment'></div>蒙污万物。富贵始及而刑祸促之者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367582_comment'></div>元子谢不及。季川问曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367582_comment'></div>兟终不复二论。兟有意乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367582_comment'></div>于戏季川。吾有言则自是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367582_comment'></div>言达则人非。吾安能使吾身之有是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367582_comment'></div>而令他人之有非。至于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1367582", 1367582, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>闻闻</span>也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367582_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1367582_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恶圆</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367586")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367586'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367586'>元子家有乳母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367586_comment'></div>为圆转之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367586_comment'></div>以悦婴儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367586_comment'></div>婴儿喜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367586_comment'></div>母使为之聚孩孺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367586_comment'></div>助婴儿之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367586_comment'></div>友人公植者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367586_comment'></div>闻有戏儿之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367586_comment'></div>请见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367586_comment'></div>及见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367586_comment'></div>趋焚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367586_comment'></div>责元子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367586_comment'></div>吾闻古之恶圆之士歌曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367586_comment'></div>宁方为皂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367586_comment'></div>不圆为卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367586_comment'></div>宁方为污辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367586_comment'></div>不圆为显荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367586_comment'></div>其甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367586_comment'></div>则终身不仰视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367586_comment'></div>曰吾恶天圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367586_comment'></div>或有喻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367586_comment'></div>以天大无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367586_comment'></div>人不能极远视四垂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367586_comment'></div>因谓之圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367586_comment'></div>天不圆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367586_comment'></div>对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367586_comment'></div>天纵不圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367586_comment'></div>为人称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367586_comment'></div>我亦恶焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367586_comment'></div>次山奈何任造圆转之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367586_comment'></div>恣令悦媚婴儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367586_comment'></div>小喜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367586_comment'></div>长必好之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367586_comment'></div>教儿学圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367586_comment'></div>且陷不义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367586_comment'></div>躬自戏圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367586_comment'></div>又失方正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367586_comment'></div>嗟嗟次山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367586_comment'></div>入门爱婴儿之乐圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367586_comment'></div>出门当爱小人之趋圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367586_comment'></div>吾安知次山异日不言圆行圆动圆静圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367586_comment'></div>以终身乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367586_comment'></div>吾岂次山之友也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367586_comment'></div>元子召季川谓曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367586_comment'></div>吾自婴儿戏圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367586_comment'></div>公植尚辱我言绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367586_comment'></div>忽乎吾与汝圆以应物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367586_comment'></div>圆以趋时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367586_comment'></div>非圆不预。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367586_comment'></div>非圆不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367586_comment'></div>公植其操矛戟刑我乎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1367586_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367587?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恶曲</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367587")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367587_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367587'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367587'>元子时与邻里会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367587_comment'></div>曲全当时之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367587_comment'></div>以顺长老之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367587_comment'></div>归泉上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367587_comment'></div>叔盈问曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367587_comment'></div>向夫子曲全其欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367587_comment'></div>道然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367587_comment'></div>苟为尔乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367587_comment'></div>元子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367587_comment'></div>叔盈视吾曲其心以徇财利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367587_comment'></div>曲其行以希名位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367587_comment'></div>当过吾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367587_comment'></div>吾苟全一欢于邻里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367587_comment'></div>无恶然可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367587_comment'></div>东邑有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1367587", 1367587, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>全直</span>之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367587_comment'></div>闻元子对叔盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367587_comment'></div>恐曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367587_comment'></div>吾闻元次山约其门人曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367587_comment'></div>无恶我之小曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367587_comment'></div>真惛鄙恶辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367587_comment'></div>吾辈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1367587", 1367587, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>全直</span>三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367587_comment'></div>未尝曲气以转声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367587_comment'></div>曲辞以达意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367587_comment'></div>曲步以便往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367587_comment'></div>曲视以回目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367587_comment'></div>犹患于古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367587_comment'></div>古人有恶曲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367587_comment'></div>不曲臂以取物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367587_comment'></div>不曲膝以便坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367587_comment'></div>见天下有曲于君曲于民曲于鬼神者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367587_comment'></div>往劫而死之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367587_comment'></div>今元次山苟曲言貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367587_comment'></div>强全一欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367587_comment'></div>以为不亵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367587_comment'></div>其直慁哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367587_comment'></div>若能苟曲于邻里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367587_comment'></div>强全一欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367587_comment'></div>岂不能苟曲于乡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367587_comment'></div>以全言行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367587_comment'></div>能苟曲于乡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367587_comment'></div>岂不能苟曲于邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367587_comment'></div>以彰名誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367587_comment'></div>能苟曲于邦国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367587_comment'></div>岂不能苟曲于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367587_comment'></div>以扬德义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367587_comment'></div>若言行名誉德义偕显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367587_comment'></div>岂有钟鼎不入门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367587_comment'></div>权位不在已乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367587_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367587_comment'></div>曲为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367587_comment'></div>小为大之渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367587_comment'></div>曲为之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367587_comment'></div>有何不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367587_comment'></div>奸邪凶恶其囮乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367587_comment'></div>元子闻之颂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367587_comment'></div>吾以颜貌曲全一欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367587_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1367587", 1367587, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>全直</span>君子之恶我如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367587_comment'></div>由有过于此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367587_comment'></div>何以自免。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1367587_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367577?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水乐说</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367577")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367577'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367577'>元子于山中尤所耽爱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367577_comment'></div>有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1367577", 1367577, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>水乐</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367577_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1367577", 1367577, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>水乐</span>是南磳之悬水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367577_comment'></div>淙淙然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367577_comment'></div>闻之多久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367577_comment'></div>于耳尤便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367577_comment'></div>不至南磳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367577_comment'></div>即悬庭前之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367577_comment'></div>取欹曲窦缺之石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367577_comment'></div>高下承之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367577_comment'></div>水声少似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367577_comment'></div>听之亦便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367577_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367577_comment'></div>烟才通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367577_comment'></div>寒淙淙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367577_comment'></div>隔山风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367577_comment'></div>老鼓钟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1367577_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>订司乐氏</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367588")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367588'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367588'>或有将元子水乐说于司乐氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367588_comment'></div>乐官闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367588_comment'></div>谓元子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367588_comment'></div>能和分五音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367588_comment'></div>韵谐水声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367588_comment'></div>可传之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367588_comment'></div>来请观学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367588_comment'></div>元子辞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367588_comment'></div>使门人以南磳及庭前悬水指之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367588_comment'></div>乐氏丑恶慢骂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367588_comment'></div>韵聩多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367588_comment'></div>焉有听而云乐乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367588_comment'></div>此言闻元子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367588_comment'></div>元子谢曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367588_comment'></div>次山病馀惛固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367588_comment'></div>自顺于空山穷谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367588_comment'></div>偶有悬水淙石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367588_comment'></div>泠然便耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367588_comment'></div>醉甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367588_comment'></div>或与酒徒戏言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367588_comment'></div>呼为水乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367588_comment'></div>不防君子过闻而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367588_comment'></div>实污辱君子之车仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367588_comment'></div>乐官去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367588_comment'></div>季川问曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367588_comment'></div>向先生谢乐官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367588_comment'></div>不亦过甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367588_comment'></div>曰然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367588_comment'></div>吾为汝订之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367588_comment'></div>汝岂不知彼为司乐之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367588_comment'></div>老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367588_comment'></div>八音教其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367588_comment'></div>五声传其耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367588_comment'></div>不得异闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367588_comment'></div>则以为错乱纷惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367588_comment'></div>甚不可听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367588_comment'></div>况悬水淙石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367588_comment'></div>宫商不能合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367588_comment'></div>律吕不能主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367588_comment'></div>变之不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367588_comment'></div>会之无由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367588_comment'></div>此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1367588", 1367588, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>全声</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367588_comment'></div>司乐氏非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1367588", 1367588, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>全士</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367588_comment'></div>安得不甚谢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367588_comment'></div>嗟乎司乐氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367588_comment'></div>欲以金石之顺和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367588_comment'></div>丝竹之流妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367588_comment'></div>宫商角羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367588_comment'></div>丰然迭生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367588_comment'></div>以化<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1367588", 1367588, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>全士</span>之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367588_comment'></div>犹以悬水淙石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367588_comment'></div>激浅注深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367588_comment'></div>清瀛灉溶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367588_comment'></div>不变司乐氏之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367588_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367588_comment'></div>天下谁为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1367588", 1367588, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>全士</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367588_comment'></div>能爱夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1367588", 1367588, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>全声</span>也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1367588_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浪翁观化<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>时化</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367593")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367593'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367593'>元子闻浪翁说化。化无穷极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367593_comment'></div>因论谕曰。翁亦未知时之化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367593_comment'></div>多于此乎。曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367593_comment'></div>时焉何化。我未之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367593_comment'></div>元子曰。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367593_comment'></div>时之化也。道德为嗜欲化为险薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367593_comment'></div>仁义为贪暴化为凶乱。礼乐为耽淫化为侈靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367593_comment'></div>政教为烦急化为苛酷。翁能记于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367593_comment'></div>时之化也。夫妇为溺惑所化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367593_comment'></div>化为犬豕。父子为惛欲所化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367593_comment'></div>化为禽兽。兄弟为猜忌所化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367593_comment'></div>化为雠敌。宗戚为财利所化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367593_comment'></div>化为行路。朋友为世利所化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367593_comment'></div>化为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1367593", 1367593, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>市儿</span>。翁能记于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367593_comment'></div>时之化也。大臣为威权所恣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367593_comment'></div>忠信化为奸谋。庶官为禁忌所拘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367593_comment'></div>公正化为邪佞。公族为猜忌所限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367593_comment'></div>贤哲化为庸愚。人民为征赋所伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367593_comment'></div>州里化为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1367593", 1367593, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>祸邸</span>。奸凶为恩幸所迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367593_comment'></div>厮皂化为将相。翁能记于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367593_comment'></div>时之化也。山泽化为井陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367593_comment'></div>或曰尽于草木。原野化为狴犴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367593_comment'></div>或曰殚于鸟兽。江湖化为鼎镬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367593_comment'></div>或曰暴于鱼鳖。祠庙化为宫寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367593_comment'></div>或曰数于祀祷。翁能记于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367593_comment'></div>时之化也。情性为风俗所化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367593_comment'></div>无不作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1367593", 1367593, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>狙狡</span>诈诳之心。声呼为风俗所化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367593_comment'></div>无不作谄媚僻淫之辞。颜容为风俗所化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367593_comment'></div>无不作奸邪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1367593", 1367593, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>蹙促</span>之色。翁能记于此乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367593_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1367593_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367594?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>世化</a><span class='authorDate'>（752年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367594'>浪翁闻元子说时化。叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367594_comment'></div>吾昔闻世化。可说又异于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367594_comment'></div>昔世之化也。天地化为斧锧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367594_comment'></div>日月化为豺虎。山泽化为州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367594_comment'></div>草木化为宗族。风雨化为邸舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367594_comment'></div>雪霜化为衣裘。呻吟化为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1367594", 1367594, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>常声</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367594_comment'></div>粪污化为梁肉。一息化为千岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367594_comment'></div>乌犬化为君子。元子惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367594_comment'></div>浪翁曰。子不闻往昔世之化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367594_comment'></div>四海之内。巷战门斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367594_comment'></div>断骨腐肉。万里相藉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367594_comment'></div>天地非斧锧也邪。人民暗夜盗起求食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367594_comment'></div>昼游则死伤相及。日月非豺虎也邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367594_comment'></div>人民相与寄身命于绝崖深谷之底。始能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1367594", 1367594, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>声呼</span>动息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367594_comment'></div>山泽非州里也邪。人民奔走非深林荟丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367594_comment'></div>不能藏蔽。草木非宗族也邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367594_comment'></div>人民去乡国入山海。千里一息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367594_comment'></div>力尽暂休。风雨非邸舍也邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367594_comment'></div>人民相持于死伤之中。裸露而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367594_comment'></div>霜雪非衣裘也邪。人民劳苦相冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367594_comment'></div>疮痍相痛。老弱孤独相苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367594_comment'></div>死亡不相救。呻吟非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1367594", 1367594, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>常声</span>也邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367594_comment'></div>人民多饥饿沟渎。痛伤道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367594_comment'></div>粪污非梁肉也邪。人民奔亡潜伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367594_comment'></div>戈矛相拂。前伤后死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367594_comment'></div>免而存者。一息非千岁也邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367594_comment'></div>僵主腐卿。相枕路隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367594_comment'></div>鸟兽让其骨肉。乌犬非君子也邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367594_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1367594_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='269d5dd7dab2418299146db4ef7b5ae6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("269d5dd7dab2418299146db4ef7b5ae6");'><span id='269d5dd7dab2418299146db4ef7b5ae6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=755')">754-755年</a>，36-37岁</div><div id='269d5dd7dab2418299146db4ef7b5ae6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年</a>　从兄元德秀卒于陆浑草堂，作墓表。作品：《元鲁山墓表》<div id='poem_1367613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元鲁县墓表</a><span class='authorDate'>（754年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367613")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367613'>天宝十三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367613_comment'></div>元子从兄前鲁县大夫德秀卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367613_comment'></div>元子哭之哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367613_comment'></div>门人叔盈问曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367613_comment'></div>夫子哭从兄也哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367613_comment'></div>不亦过乎礼欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367613_comment'></div>对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367613_comment'></div>汝知礼之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367613_comment'></div>而不知情之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367613_comment'></div>叔盈退谓其徒曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367613_comment'></div>夫子之哭元大夫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367613_comment'></div>兼师友之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367613_comment'></div>亦过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367613_comment'></div>元子闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367613_comment'></div>召叔盈谓曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367613_comment'></div>吾诚哀过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367613_comment'></div>汝所云也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367613_comment'></div>元大夫弱无所固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367613_comment'></div>壮无所专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367613_comment'></div>老无所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367613_comment'></div>死无所馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367613_comment'></div>此非人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367613_comment'></div>人情所耽溺喜爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367613_comment'></div>似可恶者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367613_comment'></div>大夫无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367613_comment'></div>如戒如惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367613_comment'></div>如憎如恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367613_comment'></div>此其无情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367613_comment'></div>此非有心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367613_comment'></div>士君子知焉不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367613_comment'></div>吾今之哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367613_comment'></div>汝知之焉而不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367613_comment'></div>呜呼元大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367613_comment'></div>生六十馀年而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367613_comment'></div>未尝识妇人而视锦绣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367613_comment'></div>不颂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367613_comment'></div>何以诫荒淫侈靡之徒也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367613_comment'></div>未尝求足而言利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367613_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1367613", 1367613, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>苟辞</span>而便色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367613_comment'></div>不颂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367613_comment'></div>何以诫贪猥佞媚之徒也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367613_comment'></div>未尝主十亩之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367613_comment'></div>十尺之舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367613_comment'></div>十岁之童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367613_comment'></div>不颂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367613_comment'></div>何以诫占田千夫室宇千柱家童百指之徒也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367613_comment'></div>未尝皂布帛而衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367613_comment'></div>具五味而食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367613_comment'></div>不颂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367613_comment'></div>何以诫绮纨梁肉之徒也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367613_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367613_comment'></div>吾以元大夫德行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367613_comment'></div>遗来世清独君子方直之士也欤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1367613_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　公友吴兴张君为玄武县大夫，有序。作品：《送张玄武序》<div id='poem_1367532' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367532' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367532?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张元武序</a><span class='authorDate'>（755年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367532")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367532_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367532'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367532'>乙未中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367532_comment'></div>诏吴兴张公为元武县大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367532_comment'></div>公旧友河东柳潜夫裴季安扶风窦伯明赵郡李长源河南元次山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367532_comment'></div>将辞宴言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367532_comment'></div>悉以言赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367532_comment'></div>上有劝仁惠恤劳苦之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367532_comment'></div>下有惜离异戒行役之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367532_comment'></div>元子闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367532_comment'></div>中有所指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367532_comment'></div>国家将日极太宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367532_comment'></div>垂休八荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367532_comment'></div>故自近年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367532_comment'></div>兵出滇外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367532_comment'></div>订者或曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367532_comment'></div>西南少疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367532_comment'></div>是以天子特有命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367532_comment'></div>将天之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367532_comment'></div>斯未易然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367532_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367532_comment'></div>蜀之遗民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367532_comment'></div>化于秦汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367532_comment'></div>纯古之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367532_comment'></div>其由未知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367532_comment'></div>无置此焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367532_comment'></div>姑取废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367532_comment'></div>如德以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1367532", 1367532, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>涵灌</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367532_comment'></div>义以封植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367532_comment'></div>其教迟远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367532_comment'></div>其人迎喁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367532_comment'></div>至乎不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367532_comment'></div>固未必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367532_comment'></div>则曰保仁以敦养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367532_comment'></div>流惠以怀恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367532_comment'></div>知其所劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367532_comment'></div>示其所安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367532_comment'></div>无以丑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367532_comment'></div>当可然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367532_comment'></div>潜夫闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367532_comment'></div>中兴不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367532_comment'></div>叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367532_comment'></div>吾尝与朋友有四方之异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367532_comment'></div>不甚感人如今之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367532_comment'></div>多问其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367532_comment'></div>对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367532_comment'></div>嗟嗟子能有是言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367532_comment'></div>吾故感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367532_comment'></div>行有规矣多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367532_comment'></div>无曰我四十于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367532_comment'></div>无曰我时禄位下哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367532_comment'></div>公乃复曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367532_comment'></div>当不失于二公之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367532_comment'></div>为异年观会之方也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367532_comment'></div>敢戒行役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367532_comment'></div>敢自清慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367532_comment'></div>终不贻朋友之忧何如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367532_comment'></div>于是醉歌中堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367532_comment'></div>极乐而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367532_comment'></div>诸公有赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367532_comment'></div>递相编次。</div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1367532_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　安禄山既反，公父延祖召结，戒勿自安山林。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　公父延祖卒，葬于鲁山。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
淮安（淮阴）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1db2722035c94f599a1ce2d78e7eae90_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1db2722035c94f599a1ce2d78e7eae90");'><span id='1db2722035c94f599a1ce2d78e7eae90_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=746&endYear=746')">746年</a>，28岁</div><div id='1db2722035c94f599a1ce2d78e7eae90' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=746&endYear=746')">746年</a>　浮游隋河至淮阴间，有诗。作品：《闵荒诗》<div id='poem_6099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6099?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闵荒诗一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（746年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6099")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6099_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6099'>天宝丙戌中，元子浮隋河至淮阴间。其年，水坏河防，得〈隋人冤歌〉五篇，考其歌义，似冤怨时主。故广其意，采其歌，为〈闵荒诗〉一篇，其馀载于《异录》。</div><div id='poem_preface_6099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6099'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6099'>炀皇嗣君位，隋德滋昏幽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6099'>日作及身祸，以为长世谋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6099'>居常耻前王，不思天子游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6099'>意欲出明堂，便登浮海舟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6099'>令行山川改，功与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_6099", 6099, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>玄造</span>侔。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6099'>河淮可支合，峰𡻮生回沟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6099'>封陨下泽中，作山防逸流。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6099'>船𦫃状龙鹢，若负宫阙浮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6099'>荒娱未<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_6099", 6099, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>央极</span>，始到沧海头。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6099'>忽见海门山，思作望海楼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6099'>不知新都城，已为征战丘。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6099'>当时有遗歌，歌曲太冤愁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6099'>四海非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_6099", 6099, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>天狱</span>，何为非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_6099", 6099, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>天囚</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_6099'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_6099", 6099, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>天囚</span>正凶忍，为我万姓雠。<div id='poem_sentence_13_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_6099'>人将引天钐，人将持天锼。<div id='poem_sentence_14_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_6099'>所欲充其心，相与绝悲忧。<div id='poem_sentence_15_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_6099'>自得隋人歌，每为隋君羞。<div id='poem_sentence_16_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_6099'>欲歌当阳春，似觉天下秋。<div id='poem_sentence_17_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_6099'>更歌曲未终，如有怨气浮。<div id='poem_sentence_18_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_6099'>奈何昏王心，不觉此怨尤。<div id='poem_sentence_19_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_6099'>遂令一夫唱，四海欣提矛。<div id='poem_sentence_20_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_6099'>吾闻古贤君，其道常静柔。<div id='poem_sentence_21_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_6099'>慈惠恐不足，端和忘所求。<div id='poem_sentence_22_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_6099'>嗟嗟有隋氏，惛惛谁与俦。<div id='poem_sentence_23_6099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_6099'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_6099_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安（长安）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8fc3332f240a42ea941db96ae02f0f79_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8fc3332f240a42ea941db96ae02f0f79");'><span id='8fc3332f240a42ea941db96ae02f0f79_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>，29岁</div><div id='8fc3332f240a42ea941db96ae02f0f79' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>应试长安，有文。作品：《皇谟》<span class='inlineComment2'>（天宝六年，玄宗以承平日久，欲广求天下之事，命通一艺已上，皆诣京师，元结与杜甫俱应试长安。相国李林甫以草野之士猥多，恐漏洩当时之机，斥言其奸恶，乃令尚书省试，皆下之，而表贺野无余贤。）</span><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>应试长安，有诗。作品：《二风诗十篇》<div id='poem_6051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二风诗十篇 治风诗五篇 其一<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>至仁</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6051")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_6051_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6051'>天宝丁亥中。元子以文辞待制阙下。著皇谟三篇。二风诗十篇。将欲求干司匦氏以裨天监。会有司奏待制者悉去之。于是归于州里。后三岁。以多病习静于商馀山。病间。遂题括存之。此亦古之贱士不忘尽臣之分耳。其义有论订之。至仁篇之序：古有仁帝。能全仁明以封天下。故为至仁之诗二章四韵十二句。</div><div id='poem_preface_6051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6051'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6051'>猗皇至圣兮，至惠至仁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6051'>德施蕴蕴，蕴蕴如何。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6051'>不全不缺，莫知所贶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6051'>猗皇至圣兮，至俭至明。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6051'>化流瀛瀛，瀛瀛如何。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6051'>不虢不赩<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作{赤包}）</span>，莫知其极。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6051'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_6051_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二风诗十篇 治风诗五篇 其二<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>至慈</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_preface_6052'>古有慈帝，能保静顺以涵万物，故为《至慈》之诗二章四韵十四句</div><div id='poem_preface_6052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6052'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6052'>至化之深兮，猗猗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6052", 6052, "Clauses/1/Comments/1")'>娭娭</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（嬉同）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6052'>如煦如吹，如负如持。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二风诗十篇 治风诗五篇 其三<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>至劳</a><span id='poem_preface_6057'>古有乱王，肆极凶虐，乱亡乃已，故为《至乱》之诗二章二韵十二句</div><div id='poem_preface_6057_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6057'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6057'>嘻乎王家，曾有凶王。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6057'>中世失国，岂非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_6057", 6057, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>骄荒</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6057'>复复之难，令则可忘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6057'>嘻乎乱王，王心何思。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6057'>暴淫虐惑，无思不为。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6057'>生人冤怨，言何极之。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6057'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_6057_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6058?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二风诗十篇 乱风诗五篇 其三<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>至虐</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_preface_6058'>古有虐王，昏毒狂忍，无恶不及，故为《至虐》之诗二章四韵十八句</div><div id='poem_preface_6058_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6058'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6058'>夫为君上兮，慈顺明恕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6058'>可以化人，忍行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_6058", 6058, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>昏恣</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6058'>独乐其身，一徇所欲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6058'>万方悲哀，于斯而喜，当云何哉？<div id='poem_sentence_3_6058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6058'>夫为君上兮，兢慎俭约。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6058'>可以保身，忍行荒惑。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6058'>虐暴于人，前世失国。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6058'>如王者多，于斯不寤，当如之何？</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_6058_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二风诗十篇 乱风诗五篇 其四<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span>至惑</a><span /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_6059_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6059'>古有惑王，用奸臣以虐外，宠妖女以乱内，内外用乱，至于崩亡，故为《至惑》之诗二章六韵二十句</div><div id='poem_preface_6059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6059'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6059'>贤圣为上兮，必俭约戒身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6059'>鉴察化人，所以保福也。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6059'>如何不思，荒恣是为。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6059'>上下隔塞，人神<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_6059", 6059, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>怨奰</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（音备）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6059'>敖恶无厌，不畏颠坠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6059'>圣贤为上兮，必用贤正。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6059'>黜奸佞之臣，所以长久也。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6059'>如何反是，以为乱矣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6059'>宠邪信惑，近佞好谀。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6059'>废嫡立庶，忍为祸谟。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6059'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_6059_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6142' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6142' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6142?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二风诗十篇 乱风诗五篇 其五<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span>至伤</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6142")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_6142_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6142'>古有伤王，以崩荡之馀，无恶不为也。乱亡之由，固在累积。故为《至伤》之诗一章</div><div id='poem_preface_6142_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6142'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6142'>夫何伤兮，伤王乎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6142'>欲何为乎，将蠹枯矣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6142'>无人救乎，蠹枯及矣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6142'>不可救乎，嗟伤王。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6142'>自为人君，变为人奴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6142'>为人君者，忘戒<span class='inlineComment2'>（一本有此字）</span>乎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6142_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6142'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_6142_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>应试长安，有文。作品：《二风诗论》《喻友》<div id='poem_1367546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二风诗论</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367546")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367546_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367546'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367546'>客有问元子曰。子著二风诗何也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367546_comment'></div>曰。吾欲极帝王理乱之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367546_comment'></div>系古人规讽之流。曰何如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367546_comment'></div>夫至理之道。先之以仁明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367546_comment'></div>故颂帝尧为仁帝。安之以慈顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367546_comment'></div>故颂帝舜为慈帝。成之以劳俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367546_comment'></div>故颂夏禹为劳王。修之以敬慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367546_comment'></div>故颂殷宗为正王。守之以清一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367546_comment'></div>故颂周成为理王。此理风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367546_comment'></div>夫至乱之道。先之以逸惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367546_comment'></div>故闵太康为荒王。坏之以苛纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367546_comment'></div>故闵夏桀为乱王。覆之以淫暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367546_comment'></div>故闵殷纣为虐王。危之以用乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367546_comment'></div>故闵周幽为惑王。亡之于积累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367546_comment'></div>故闵周赧为伤王。此乱风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367546_comment'></div>订曰。子颂善上不及羲轩汤武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367546_comment'></div>闵恶又不及始皇哀灵。焉可称极帝王理乱之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367546_comment'></div>对曰。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367546_comment'></div>吾敢言极。极其中道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367546_comment'></div>吾且不曰著斯诗也。将系规讽乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367546_comment'></div>如羲轩之道也久矣。谁能师尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367546_comment'></div>如汤武之德。吾则不敢颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367546_comment'></div>为规法过于是也。吾子审之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367546_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1367546_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367580' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367580' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367580?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喻友</a><span class='authorDate'>（747年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367580")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367580'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367580'>天宝丁亥中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367580_comment'></div>诏徵天下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367580_comment'></div>人有一艺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367580_comment'></div>皆得诣京师就选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367580_comment'></div>相国晋公林甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367580_comment'></div>以草野之士猥多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367580_comment'></div>恐泄漏当时之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367580_comment'></div>议于朝廷曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367580_comment'></div>举人多卑贱愚聩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367580_comment'></div>不识礼度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367580_comment'></div>恐有⿰<span class='inlineComment2'>（言里）</span>言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367580_comment'></div>污浊圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367580_comment'></div>于是奏待制者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367580_comment'></div>悉令尚书长官考试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367580_comment'></div>御史中丞监之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367580_comment'></div>试如常吏<span class='inlineComment2'>（如吏部试诗赋论策）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367580_comment'></div>已而布衣之士无有第者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367580_comment'></div>遂表贺人主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367580_comment'></div>以为野无遗贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367580_comment'></div>元子时在举中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367580_comment'></div>将东归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367580_comment'></div>乡人有苦贫贱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367580_comment'></div>欲留长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367580_comment'></div>依托时权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367580_comment'></div>徘徊相谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367580_comment'></div>因谕之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367580_comment'></div>昔世已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367580_comment'></div>共尚丘园洁白之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367580_comment'></div>盖为其能外独自全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367580_comment'></div>不和不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367580_comment'></div>饥寒切之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367580_comment'></div>不为劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367580_comment'></div>自守穷贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367580_comment'></div>甘心不辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367580_comment'></div>忽天子有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367580_comment'></div>聘之元纁束帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367580_comment'></div>以先意荐论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367580_comment'></div>拥彗以导道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367580_comment'></div>欲有所问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367580_comment'></div>如咨师傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367580_comment'></div>听其言则可为规戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367580_comment'></div>考其行则可为师范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367580_comment'></div>用其材则可为经济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367580_comment'></div>与之权位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367580_comment'></div>乃社稷之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367580_comment'></div>君能忘此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367580_comment'></div>而欲随逐驽骀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367580_comment'></div>入栈枥中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367580_comment'></div>食下厩藖麧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367580_comment'></div>为人后骑负皂隶受鞭策耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367580_comment'></div>人生不方正忠信以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1367580", 1367580, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>显荣</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367580_comment'></div>则介洁静和以终老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367580_comment'></div>乡人于是与元子偕归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367580_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367580_comment'></div>贵不专权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367580_comment'></div>罔惑上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367580_comment'></div>贱能守分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367580_comment'></div>不苟求取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367580_comment'></div>始为君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367580_comment'></div>因喻乡人得及林甫言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367580_comment'></div>意可存编为喻友。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1367580_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6fec27db1ec14b7aa4a6322b8c2a57d4_label'><a
