ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=749')">748-749年</a>，30-31岁</div><div id='6fec27db1ec14b7aa4a6322b8c2a57d4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=748')">748年</a>　游长安，有文章以讽当道。作品：《丐论》<div id='poem_1367548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丐论</a><span class='authorDate'>（748年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367548")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367548'>天宝戊子中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367548_comment'></div>元子游长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367548_comment'></div>与丐者为友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367548_comment'></div>或曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367548_comment'></div>君友丐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367548_comment'></div>不太下乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367548_comment'></div>对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367548_comment'></div>古人乡无君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367548_comment'></div>则与云山为友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367548_comment'></div>里无君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367548_comment'></div>则与松柏为友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367548_comment'></div>坐无君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367548_comment'></div>则与琴酒为友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367548_comment'></div>出游于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367548_comment'></div>见君子则友之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367548_comment'></div>丐者今之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367548_comment'></div>吾恐不得与之友也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367548_comment'></div>丐者丐论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367548_comment'></div>子能听乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367548_comment'></div>吾既与丐者相友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367548_comment'></div>喻求罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367548_comment'></div>丐友相喻曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367548_comment'></div>子羞吾为丐邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367548_comment'></div>有可羞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367548_comment'></div>亦曾知未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367548_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367548_comment'></div>于今之世有丐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367548_comment'></div>丐宗属于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367548_comment'></div>丐嫁娶于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367548_comment'></div>丐名位于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367548_comment'></div>丐颜色于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367548_comment'></div>甚者则丐权家奴齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367548_comment'></div>以售邪佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367548_comment'></div>丐权家婢颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367548_comment'></div>以容媚惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367548_comment'></div>有自富丐贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367548_comment'></div>自贵丐贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367548_comment'></div>于刑丐命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367548_comment'></div>命不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367548_comment'></div>就死丐时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367548_comment'></div>就时丐息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367548_comment'></div>至死丐全形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367548_comment'></div>而终有不可丐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367548_comment'></div>更有甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367548_comment'></div>丐家族于仆圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367548_comment'></div>丐性命于臣妾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367548_comment'></div>丐宗庙而不敢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367548_comment'></div>丐妻子而无辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367548_comment'></div>有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367548_comment'></div>不可为羞哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367548_comment'></div>吾所以丐人之弃衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367548_comment'></div>丐人之弃食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367548_comment'></div>提罂荷杖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367548_comment'></div>在于路傍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367548_comment'></div>且欲与天下之人为同类耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367548_comment'></div>不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367548_comment'></div>则无颜容行于人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367548_comment'></div>夫丐衣食贫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367548_comment'></div>以贫乞丐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367548_comment'></div>心不惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367548_comment'></div>迹与人同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367548_comment'></div>示无异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367548_comment'></div>此君子之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367548_comment'></div>吾君子不欲全道邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367548_comment'></div>幸不在山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367548_comment'></div>亦宜具罂杖随我作丐者之状貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367548_comment'></div>学丐者之言辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367548_comment'></div>与丐者之相逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367548_comment'></div>使丐者之无耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367548_comment'></div>庶几时世始能相容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367548_comment'></div>吾子无矫然取不容也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367548_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367548_comment'></div>丐者言语如斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367548_comment'></div>可编为丐论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367548_comment'></div>以补时规。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1367548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=748')">748年</a>　游长安，有文。作品：《寱论》<div id='poem_1367547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寱论</a><span class='authorDate'>（748年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367547")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367547_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367547'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367547'>元子天宝中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367547_comment'></div>曾预燕于谏议大夫之坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367547_comment'></div>酒尽而无以续之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367547_comment'></div>大夫叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367547_comment'></div>谏议冗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367547_comment'></div>贫无以继酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367547_comment'></div>嗟哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367547_comment'></div>元子醉中议之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367547_comment'></div>大夫颇能用一谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367547_comment'></div>令大夫尊重如侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367547_comment'></div>威权等司隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367547_comment'></div>若何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367547_comment'></div>大夫问谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367547_comment'></div>对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367547_comment'></div>大夫得寱婢一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367547_comment'></div>在人主左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367547_comment'></div>以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1367547", 1367547, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>寱言</span>为先讽则可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367547_comment'></div>请有所说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367547_comment'></div>大夫不闻古有邰侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367547_comment'></div>侯家得寱婢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367547_comment'></div>寐则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1367547", 1367547, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>寱言</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367547_comment'></div>言则侯辄鞭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367547_comment'></div>如是一岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367547_comment'></div>婢寱如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367547_comment'></div>侯无如婢何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367547_comment'></div>有夷奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367547_comment'></div>每厌劳辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367547_comment'></div>寐则假寱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367547_comment'></div>其言似不怨主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367547_comment'></div>而若忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367547_comment'></div>侯闻问之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367547_comment'></div>则曰素有寱病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367547_comment'></div>寐中<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1367547", 1367547, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>寱言</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367547_comment'></div>非所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367547_comment'></div>引寱婢自辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367547_comment'></div>词说云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367547_comment'></div>侯疑学婢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367547_comment'></div>鞭之不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367547_comment'></div>瞢之钳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367547_comment'></div>奴寱愈甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367547_comment'></div>奴于是重窥侯意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367547_comment'></div>先事寱说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367547_comment'></div>说侯之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367547_comment'></div>警以祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367547_comment'></div>侯又无如奴何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367547_comment'></div>客有知侯祸机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367547_comment'></div>因寱奴之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367547_comment'></div>扣侯门谏侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367547_comment'></div>侯以改过免祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367547_comment'></div>侯纳客为上宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367547_comment'></div>复其奴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367547_comment'></div>命曰寱良氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367547_comment'></div>子孙世在于邰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367547_comment'></div>大夫诚能学奴效婢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367547_comment'></div>假<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1367547", 1367547, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>寱言</span>以规谏人主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367547_comment'></div>俾悔过<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1367547", 1367547, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>追误</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367547_comment'></div>与天下如新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367547_comment'></div>大夫见尊重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367547_comment'></div>威权何止侍中司隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367547_comment'></div>大夫乃叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367547_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367547_comment'></div>吾谓今之士君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367547_comment'></div>曾不如邰侯夷奴邪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1367547_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年</a>　长安应试，举进士，有文编集子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年</a>　长安应试，有文。作品：《订古五篇》<div id='poem_1367605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>订古五篇<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（753年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367605")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367605_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367605'>天宝癸巳。元子作订古。订古前世君臣父子兄弟夫妇朋友之道。于戏。上古失之。中古乱之。至于近世。有穷极凶恶者矣。或曰。欲如之何。对曰。将如之何。吾且闻之订之。嗟之伤之。泣而恨之而已也。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367605'>吾观君臣之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367605_comment'></div>且有猜忌而闻疑惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367605_comment'></div>其由禅让革代之道误也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367605_comment'></div>故后世有劫篡废放之恶兴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367605_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367605_comment'></div>即有孤弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367605_comment'></div>将安托哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367605_comment'></div>即有功业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367605_comment'></div>将安保哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1367605_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367606?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367606_comment'></div>故后世有幽毒囚杀之患起焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367606_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367606_comment'></div>即有深慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367606_comment'></div>将安兴哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367606_comment'></div>即有至孝。<div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367607'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367607'>吾观兄弟之中。<div class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367585")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367585'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367585'>乾元己亥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367585_comment'></div>漫叟待诏在长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367585_comment'></div>时中行公掌制在中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367585_comment'></div>中书有醇酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367585_comment'></div>时得一醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367585_comment'></div>醉中叟诞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367585_comment'></div>愿穷天下鸟兽虫鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367585_comment'></div>以充杀者之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367585_comment'></div>愿穷天下醇酎美色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367585_comment'></div>以充欲者之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367585_comment'></div>中行公闻之叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367585_comment'></div>子何思不尽耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367585_comment'></div>何不曰愿得如九州之地者亿万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367585_comment'></div>分封君臣父子兄弟之争国者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367585_comment'></div>使人民免贼虐残酷者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367585_comment'></div>何不曰愿得布帛钱货珍宝之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367585_comment'></div>溢于王者府藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367585_comment'></div>满将相权势之家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367585_comment'></div>使人民免饥寒劳苦者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367585_comment'></div>叟闻公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367585_comment'></div>退而书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367585_comment'></div>授于学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367585_comment'></div>用为时规。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1367585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>向唐肃宗献《时议》三篇。作品：《时议三篇》<div id='poem_1367521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>时议三篇<span class='inlineComment2'>（并表）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>上篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367521")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367521_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367521'>臣某言。臣自以昏庸无堪。逸浪江海。陛下忽降公诏。远徵愚臣。陛下岂不以凶逆未除。盗贼屡起。百姓劳苦。力用不足。将社稷大计。与天下图之者乎。荒野贱臣。始见轩陛。又拘限忌讳。不能悉下情以上闻。则陛下又安用烦劳车乘。招礼贤异。臣实不能当君子之羞。受小人之辱。故编舆皂之说为三篇。名曰时议。敢以上闻。抵冒天威。谨伏待罪。臣结顿首谨上。乾元二年九月日。前进士元结表上。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367521'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367521'>时之议者或相问曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367521_comment'></div>往年逆乱之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367521_comment'></div>东穷江海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367521_comment'></div>南极淮汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367521_comment'></div>西抵秦塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367521_comment'></div>北尽幽都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367521_comment'></div>令赵卫之疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367521_comment'></div>悉为盗有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367521_comment'></div>凶勇之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367521_comment'></div>在四方者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367521_comment'></div>几百馀万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367521_comment'></div>如屯守二京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367521_comment'></div>从卫魁帅者不计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367521_comment'></div>当时之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367521_comment'></div>可谓强矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367521_comment'></div>当时人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367521_comment'></div>已不固矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367521_comment'></div>天子独以数骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367521_comment'></div>仅至灵武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367521_comment'></div>引聚馀弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367521_comment'></div>凭陵强寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367521_comment'></div>顿军岐阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367521_comment'></div>师及渭西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367521_comment'></div>曾不踰时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367521_comment'></div>竟能摧坚锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367521_comment'></div>复两京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367521_comment'></div>逃降逆类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367521_comment'></div>悉收河南州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367521_comment'></div>今河北陇阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367521_comment'></div>奸逆尚馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367521_comment'></div>今山谷江湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367521_comment'></div>稍多亡命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367521_comment'></div>今所在盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367521_comment'></div>屡犯州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367521_comment'></div>今天下百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367521_comment'></div>咸转流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367521_comment'></div>今临敌将士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367521_comment'></div>多喜奔散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367521_comment'></div>今贤士君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367521_comment'></div>不求任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367521_comment'></div>天子往在灵武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367521_comment'></div>至于凤翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367521_comment'></div>无今日兵革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367521_comment'></div>而能胜敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367521_comment'></div>无今日禁制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367521_comment'></div>而无亡命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367521_comment'></div>无今日威令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367521_comment'></div>而盗贼不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367521_comment'></div>无今日财用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367521_comment'></div>而百姓不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367521_comment'></div>无今日封赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367521_comment'></div>而将士不散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367521_comment'></div>无今日朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367521_comment'></div>而人思任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367521_comment'></div>何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367521_comment'></div>岂天子能以弱制强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367521_comment'></div>不能以强制弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367521_comment'></div>岂天子能以危求安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367521_comment'></div>而忍以未安忘危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367521_comment'></div>时之议者或相对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367521_comment'></div>此非难言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367521_comment'></div>甚易言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367521_comment'></div>天子往年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367521_comment'></div>悲恨陵庙为凶逆伤污。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367521_comment'></div>怨愤上皇忽南幸巴蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367521_comment'></div>哀伤宗戚多见诛害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367521_comment'></div>惊惶圣躬动息无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367521_comment'></div>是以勤劳不辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367521_comment'></div>亲抚士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367521_comment'></div>与人权位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367521_comment'></div>信而不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367521_comment'></div>渴闻忠直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367521_comment'></div>过则喜改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367521_comment'></div>如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367521_comment'></div>所以能以弱制强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367521_comment'></div>以危求安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367521_comment'></div>今天子重城深宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367521_comment'></div>燕私而居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367521_comment'></div>冕旒清晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367521_comment'></div>缨佩而朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367521_comment'></div>太官具味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367521_comment'></div>当时而食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367521_comment'></div>太常修乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367521_comment'></div>和声而听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367521_comment'></div>军国机务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367521_comment'></div>参详而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367521_comment'></div>万姓疾苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367521_comment'></div>时或不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367521_comment'></div>而厩有良马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367521_comment'></div>宫有美女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367521_comment'></div>舆服礼物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367521_comment'></div>日月以备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367521_comment'></div>休符佳瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367521_comment'></div>相继而有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367521_comment'></div>朝廷歌颂盛德大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367521_comment'></div>四方贡赋尤异品物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367521_comment'></div>公族姻戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367521_comment'></div>喜符帝恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1367521_comment'></div>谐臣戏官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1367521_comment'></div>怡愉天颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1367521_comment'></div>而文武大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1367521_comment'></div>至于公卿庶官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1367521_comment'></div>皆权位爵赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1367521_comment'></div>名实之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1367521_comment'></div>似已过望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1367521_comment'></div>此所以不能以强制弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1367521_comment'></div>忍以未安忘危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1367521_comment'></div>若天子能视今日之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1367521_comment'></div>如灵武之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1367521_comment'></div>事无大小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1367521_comment'></div>皆若灵武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1367521_comment'></div>何寇盗强弱可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1367521_comment'></div>当天下日无事矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_112_1367521_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367522?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>中篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367522'>时之议者或相谓曰。吾闻道路云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367522_comment'></div>说士人共自谋曰。昔我奉天子拒凶逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367522_comment'></div>胜敌则家国两存。不胜则家国两亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367522_comment'></div>所以生死决战。是非极谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367522_comment'></div>今吾属名位已重。财货已足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367522_comment'></div>爵赏已厚。勤劳已极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367522_comment'></div>天下若安。吾何苦哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367522_comment'></div>天下若不安。吾属外无仇雠相害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367522_comment'></div>内无穷贱相迫。何苦更当锋刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367522_comment'></div>以近死乎。何苦更忤人主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367522_comment'></div>以近祸乎。又闻曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367522_comment'></div>呜呼。吾州里有忠义之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367522_comment'></div>仁信之者。方直之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367522_comment'></div>今或有病父老母。孤儿寡妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367522_comment'></div>如身能存者。皆力役乞丐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367522_comment'></div>冻馁不足。况于死者父母妻子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367522_comment'></div>人谁哀之。又闻曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367522_comment'></div>今天下残破。苍生危急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367522_comment'></div>受赋役者。多寡弱贫独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367522_comment'></div>流亡死生。悲忧道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367522_comment'></div>盖亦极矣。天下若安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367522_comment'></div>我等岂无陇亩以自处。若不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367522_comment'></div>我等不复以忠义仁信方直死矣。纵有盗于我者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367522_comment'></div>安则随之。人且如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367522_comment'></div>其然何故。时之议者相对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367522_comment'></div>今国家非欲其然。盖失于太明太信而然耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367522_comment'></div>夫太明则见其内情。将藏内情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367522_comment'></div>则罔惑生焉。罔上惑下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367522_comment'></div>能令必信。信可必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367522_comment'></div>故太信焉。太信之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367522_comment'></div>至奸元恶。卓然而存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367522_comment'></div>如此。使朝廷遂亡公直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367522_comment'></div>天下遂失忠信。苍生遂益冤怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367522_comment'></div>如公直亡矣。忠信失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367522_comment'></div>冤怨生矣。岂天子大臣之所喜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367522_comment'></div>将欲理之。能无端由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367522_comment'></div>吾属议于野者。又何所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367522_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1367522_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367523?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>下篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367523'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367523'>时之议者或相问曰。今天子思安苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367523_comment'></div>思灭奸逆。思致太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367523_comment'></div>方力图之。非不勤劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367523_comment'></div>于今四年。而说者异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367523_comment'></div>何哉。时之议者或相对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367523_comment'></div>如天子所思。如说者所异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367523_comment'></div>天子大臣。非不知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367523_comment'></div>凡有制诰。皆尝言及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367523_comment'></div>言虽慇勤。事皆不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367523_comment'></div>前后再三。颇类<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1367523", 1367523, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>谐戏</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367523_comment'></div>今或有仁恤之诏。忧勤之诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367523_comment'></div>人皆族立党语。指而议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367523_comment'></div>其由何哉。以言而不行之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367523_comment'></div>天子不知其然。以为言虽不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367523_comment'></div>足堪沮劝。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367523_comment'></div>沮劝之道。在明审均当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367523_comment'></div>而必行也。必不行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367523_comment'></div>有言何为。自太古以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367523_comment'></div>致理兴化。未有言之不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367523_comment'></div>而能至矣。若天子能追行已言之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367523_comment'></div>必行将来之法。且免天下无端杂徭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367523_comment'></div>且除天下随时<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1367523", 1367523, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>弊法</span>。且去天下拘忌烦令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367523_comment'></div>必任天下贤异君子。屏斥天下奸邪小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367523_comment'></div>然后推仁信威令。与之不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367523_comment'></div>此帝王常道。何为不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367523_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1367523_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>拜谒中书侍郎同平章事李揆，有文。作品：《与李相公书》<div id='poem_1367525' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367525' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367525?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李相公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367525")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367525_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367525'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367525'>月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367525_comment'></div>新授右金吾兵曹参军摄监察御史元结顿首相公执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367525_comment'></div>某性愚弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367525_comment'></div>本不敢干时求进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367525_comment'></div>十馀年间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367525_comment'></div>在山野过为知已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367525_comment'></div>猥见称誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367525_comment'></div>辱在乡选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367525_comment'></div>名污上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367525_comment'></div>退而知耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367525_comment'></div>更自委顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367525_comment'></div>亦数年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367525_comment'></div>中逢丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367525_comment'></div>奔走江海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367525_comment'></div>当死复生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367525_comment'></div>见有今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367525_comment'></div>林壑不保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367525_comment'></div>敢思禄位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367525_comment'></div>忽枉公诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367525_comment'></div>命诣京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367525_comment'></div>州县发遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367525_comment'></div>不得辞避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367525_comment'></div>三四千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367525_comment'></div>烦劳公车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367525_comment'></div>始命蹈舞帝庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367525_comment'></div>即日辞命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367525_comment'></div>担囊乞丐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367525_comment'></div>复归海滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367525_comment'></div>今则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1367525", 1367525, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>过次</span>授官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367525_comment'></div>又令将命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367525_comment'></div>谋人军者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367525_comment'></div>谁曰易乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367525_comment'></div>相公见某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367525_comment'></div>但礼文拜揖之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367525_comment'></div>无所问焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367525_comment'></div>忽然狂妄男子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367525_comment'></div>不称任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367525_comment'></div>坐招败辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367525_comment'></div>相公如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367525_comment'></div>某所以尽所知见闻于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367525_comment'></div>不审相公以为可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367525_comment'></div>如曰不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367525_comment'></div>合正典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367525_comment'></div>欺上誷下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367525_comment'></div>是某之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367525_comment'></div>谨奉诏书及章服待命屏外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367525_comment'></div>某顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1367525_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>奉旨于唐、邓、汝、蔡等州招缉义兵。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b776442f4c644272a7d0e6229b18317a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b776442f4c644272a7d0e6229b18317a");'><span id='b776442f4c644272a7d0e6229b18317a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>，54岁</div><div id='b776442f4c644272a7d0e6229b18317a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年4月</a>　朝京师遇疾薨于永崇坊旅馆，赠礼部侍郎。<br /></div>

-----title
大冶（武昌）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4a5595fd96ec4a1db99125cf7aa1e689_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a5595fd96ec4a1db99125cf7aa1e689");'><span id='4a5595fd96ec4a1db99125cf7aa1e689_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=757')">756-757年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='4a5595fd96ec4a1db99125cf7aa1e689' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=757')">756-757年</a>　在湖北大冶，有文。作品：《虎蛇颂》《异泉铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：又见孙望校《元次山集》第85页。）</span>《管仲论》《为董江夏自陈表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：约至德元载末或至德二载初作。）</span><div id='poem_1367563' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367563' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367563?labeling=true' target='_blank'>异泉铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（756年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367563")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367563_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367563'>天宝十三年。春至夏甚旱。秋至冬积雨。西塞西南有回山。山巅是秋崩坼。有穴出泉。泉垂流三四百仞。浮江中可望。于戏。阴阳旱雨。时异。以至柔破至坚。事异。以至下处至高。理异。故命斯泉曰异泉。铭于泉上。其意岂独旌异而已乎。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367563_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367563'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367563'>何故作铭，铭于异泉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367563'>为其当不可阏，坼石出焉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367563'>何用作铭，铭于异泉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367563'>为其当不可下，穷高流焉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367563'>君子之德，显与晦殊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367563'>为此铭者，忘道也欤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367563_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367563'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1367563_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367551' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367551' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367551?labeling=true' target='_blank'>管仲论</a><span class='authorDate'>（757年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367551")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367551_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367551'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367551'>自兵兴已来。今三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367551_comment'></div>论者多云。得如管仲者一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367551_comment'></div>以辅人主。当见天下太平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367551_comment'></div>元子异之曰。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367551_comment'></div>何是言之误邪。彼管仲者人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367551_comment'></div>止可与议私家畜养之计。止可以修乡里畎浍之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367551_comment'></div>如此仲可当焉。至如相诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367551_comment'></div>材量已似不足。致齐及霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367551_comment'></div>材量极矣。使仲见帝王之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367551_comment'></div>识兴国之礼。则天子之国不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367551_comment'></div>诸侯之国不盛。如曰不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367551_comment'></div>请有所说。仲之相齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367551_comment'></div>及齐彊富。则合请其君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367551_comment'></div>恢复王室。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1367551", 1367551, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>节正</span>诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367551_comment'></div>君若惑之。则引祸福以喻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367551_comment'></div>君既听矣。然后约诸侯曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367551_comment'></div>今王室将卑。诸侯更彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367551_comment'></div>文王风化。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1367551", 1367551, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>残削</span>向尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367551_comment'></div>武王疆域。割夺无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367551_comment'></div>礼乐不知其田。征伐何因而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367551_comment'></div>我是故谨疆域。勉日夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367551_comment'></div>望振兵威。可临列国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367551_comment'></div>得与诸侯会盟。一旦能新复天子之正朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367551_comment'></div>更定天子之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1367551", 1367551, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>封畿</span>。上奉天子复先王之风化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367551_comment'></div>下令诸侯复先公之制度。以为何如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367551_comment'></div>若皆不从。我则以兵临于鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367551_comment'></div>鲁不敢不从。鲁从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367551_comment'></div>则与鲁西临宋郑。宋郑从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367551_comment'></div>则与三国北临燕卫。燕卫从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367551_comment'></div>则与诸国西临秦晋。秦晋从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367551_comment'></div>则与七国以尺简约吴楚。吴楚从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367551_comment'></div>则天下无不从之国。然后定约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367551_comment'></div>若有果不从者。则约从者曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367551_comment'></div>吾属以礼乐尊天子。以法度正诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367551_comment'></div>使小国不常患弱。大国不敢怙彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367551_comment'></div>此诚长世之策。若天子国亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367551_comment'></div>则诸侯交争。兵戈相临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367551_comment'></div>谁为彊者。则安得世世礼让相服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367551_comment'></div>宗庙血食。我是故力劝诸侯尊天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367551_comment'></div>今某国犹豫。宜往问之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367551_comment'></div>若不从约。则与诸侯率兵伐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367551_comment'></div>分其疆土。迁其子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367551_comment'></div>留百里之地奉其宗社。下为诸侯广子孙之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367551_comment'></div>上为天子除不顺之臣何如。如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367551_comment'></div>则诸侯谁敢不从。然后定天子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1367551", 1367551, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>封畿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367551_comment'></div>诸侯疆域。舆服器玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367551_comment'></div>礼乐法度。征赋贡输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367551_comment'></div>自齐鲁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1367551", 1367551, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>节正</span>。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1367551", 1367551, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>节正</span>既定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367551_comment'></div>乃共盟曰。有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1367551", 1367551, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>贰约</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367551_comment'></div>当请命天子。废其骄凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367551_comment'></div>以立恭顺。废其荒惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367551_comment'></div>以立明哲。敢不听者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367551_comment'></div>伐而分之。如初约制定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367551_comment'></div>于是诸侯先各造邸于天子之都。诸侯乃相率朝觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367551_comment'></div>已而从天子齐戒拜宗庙。礼毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367551_comment'></div>天子誓曰。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367551_comment'></div>王室之卑久矣。予不敢望皇天后土之所覆载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367551_comment'></div>将旦暮皂隶于诸侯。不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367551_comment'></div>则愿全肌骨下见先王。今诸侯不忘先王之大德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367551_comment'></div>不忘先公之忠烈。共力正王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367551_comment'></div>俾予主先王宗祀。予若昏荒淫虐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367551_comment'></div>不纳谏诤。失先王法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367551_comment'></div>上不能奉宗祀。下不能安人民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367551_comment'></div>尔诸侯当理尔军卒。修尔矛戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367551_comment'></div>约尔列国。罪予凶恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367551_comment'></div>嗣立明辟。予若能日勉孱弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367551_comment'></div>力遵先王法度。上奉宗祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367551_comment'></div>下安人民。尔诸侯当保尔疆域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367551_comment'></div>安尔人民。修尔贡赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1367551_comment'></div>共予郊祀。予有此誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1367551_comment'></div>岂云及予。将及来世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1367551_comment'></div>予敢以此誓誓于宗庙。予敢以此誓誓于天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1367551_comment'></div>诸侯闻天子之誓。相率盟曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1367551_comment'></div>天子有誓。俾我诸侯世世得力扶王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1367551_comment'></div>使先王先公。德业永长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1367551_comment'></div>诸侯其各铭天子之誓。传之后嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1367551_comment'></div>我诸侯重自约曰。诸侯有昏惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1367551_comment'></div>当如前盟。若天子昏惑不嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1367551_comment'></div>虐乱天下。诸侯当力共规讽谏诤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1367551_comment'></div>如甚不可。则我诸侯共率礼兵及王之畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1367551_comment'></div>复谏诤如初。又甚不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1367551_comment'></div>进礼兵及王之郊。终不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1367551_comment'></div>进礼兵及王之宫。兵及王之宫矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1367551_comment'></div>当以宗庙之忧咨之。当以人民之怨咨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1367551_comment'></div>当以天子昔誓咨之。当以诸侯昔盟咨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1367551_comment'></div>以不敢欺先王先公告之。以不敢欺皇天后土告之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1367551_comment'></div>然后如天子昔誓。如诸侯昔盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1367551_comment'></div>使管仲能如此。则周之天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1367551_comment'></div>未为奴矣。诸侯之国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1367551_comment'></div>则未亡矣。秦于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1367551_comment'></div>未至是矣。如曰仲才及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1367551_comment'></div>君不从也。仲智及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1367551_comment'></div>时不可也。则仲曾是谋也乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1367551_comment'></div>君不从之也欤。仲曾是为也乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1367551_comment'></div>时之不可也欤。况今日之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1367551_comment'></div>不可以礼义节制。不可以盟誓禁止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1367551_comment'></div>如仲之辈。欲何为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1367551_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1367551_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为董江夏自陈表</a><span class='authorDate'>（757年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367511")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367511'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367511'>臣某言。月日敕使某官某乙至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367511_comment'></div>赐臣制书示臣云云者。臣伏见诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367511_comment'></div>感深惊惧。臣岂草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367511_comment'></div>不知天心。顷者潼关失守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367511_comment'></div>皇舆不安。四方之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367511_comment'></div>无所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1367511", 1367511, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>系命</span>。及永王承制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367511_comment'></div>出镇荆南。妇人童子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367511_comment'></div>忻奉王教。意其然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367511_comment'></div>人未离心。臣谓此时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367511_comment'></div>可奋臣节。王初见臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367511_comment'></div>谓臣可任。遂授臣江夏郡太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367511_comment'></div>近日王以寇盗侵逼。总兵东下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367511_comment'></div>傍牒郡县。皆言巡抚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367511_comment'></div>今诸道节度以为王不奉诏。兵临郡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367511_comment'></div>疑王之议。闻于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367511_comment'></div>臣则王所授官。有兵防御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367511_comment'></div>邻郡并邑。疑臣顺王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367511_comment'></div>旬日之閒。置身无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367511_comment'></div>臣本受王之命。为王奉诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367511_comment'></div>王所授臣之官。为臣许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367511_comment'></div>忠正之分。臣实未亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367511_comment'></div>苍黄之中。死几无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367511_comment'></div>不图今日得达圣聪。臣今年将六十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367511_comment'></div>老母在堂。纵未能奉义捐生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367511_comment'></div>则岂忍两忘忠孝。臣少以文学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367511_comment'></div>为诸生所多。中年自颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367511_comment'></div>逸在山泽。圣明无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367511_comment'></div>甘为外臣。无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367511_comment'></div>以鄙僻之故。返为人知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367511_comment'></div>遂污<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1367511", 1367511, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>官次</span>。以至今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367511_comment'></div>臣又顷年贬谪。罪未昭洗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367511_comment'></div>今所授官。复超越班秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367511_comment'></div>罢归待罪。是臣之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367511_comment'></div>今陛下以王室艰难。寄臣方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367511_comment'></div>臣亦以忘身许国。誓于皇天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367511_comment'></div>伏惟陛下念臣恳至。谨因敕使臣某官奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367511_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1367511_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
瑞昌（浔阳）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='24c7e33959da45a28027587936951aed_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("24c7e33959da45a28027587936951aed");'><span id='24c7e33959da45a28027587936951aed_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>，40岁</div><div id='24c7e33959da45a28027587936951aed' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在江西瑞昌，有文。作品：《瀼溪铭》《浪说七篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（浪说七篇今逸。）</span><div id='poem_1367564' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367564' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367564?labeling=true' target='_blank'>瀼溪铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367564")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367564_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367564'>乾元戊戌。浪生元结始浪家瀼溪之滨。瀼溪盖湓水。分称瀼水。夏瀼江海。则百里为瀼湖。二十里为瀼溪。瀼溪浪士爱之。铭之其滨。于戏。古人喜尚君子。不见君子。见如似者。亦称颂之。瀼溪可谓让矣。让君子之道也。称颂如此。可遗瀼溪。若天下有如似让者。吾岂先瀼溪而称颂者乎。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367564_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367564'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367564'>瀼溪之澜，谁取盥焉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367564'>瀼溪之漪，谁取饮之。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367564'>盥实可矣，饮岂难矣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367564'>得不惭其心，不如此水。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367564'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1367564", 1367564, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>浪士</span>作铭，将戒何人。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367564'>欲不让者，惭游瀼滨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367564_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367564'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1367564_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
汝州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7f69786db1f4451db6380ec43cac08f7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7f69786db1f4451db6380ec43cac08f7");'><span id='7f69786db1f4451db6380ec43cac08f7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>，41岁</div><div id='7f69786db1f4451db6380ec43cac08f7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　从浔阳北上经汝上，与山龟俱乘邮诣京师。<br /></div>

-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c9ef647693534a73a7fde5c67fdeee18_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c9ef647693534a73a7fde5c67fdeee18");'><span id='c9ef647693534a73a7fde5c67fdeee18_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　拜谒礼部尚书东都留守韦陟，有文。作品：《与韦尚书书》<div id='poem_1367524' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367524' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367524?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与韦尚书书</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367524")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367524_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367524'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367524'>某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367524_comment'></div>前进士元结顿首尚书公閤下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367524_comment'></div>结每闻贤卿大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367524_comment'></div>能以至公之道推引君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367524_comment'></div>使名声德业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367524_comment'></div>相继称显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367524_comment'></div>则思见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367524_comment'></div>若不以至公之道推引君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367524_comment'></div>使祸恶凶辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367524_comment'></div>同日更受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367524_comment'></div>则不思见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367524_comment'></div>结所以年四十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367524_comment'></div>足不入于公卿之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367524_comment'></div>身不齿于利禄之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367524_comment'></div>岂忘荣显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367524_comment'></div>盖惧污辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367524_comment'></div>昨者有诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367524_comment'></div>使结得诣京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367524_comment'></div>至汝上逢山龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367524_comment'></div>亦承诏诣京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367524_comment'></div>结与山龟俱得乘邮而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367524_comment'></div>邮长待结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367524_comment'></div>颇如龟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367524_comment'></div>前日谒见尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367524_comment'></div>俯拜阶下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367524_comment'></div>本望齿乘邮与诸龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367524_comment'></div>结待命而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367524_comment'></div>不望尚书不以结齿之于龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367524_comment'></div>以士君子见礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367524_comment'></div>问及词赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367524_comment'></div>许且休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367524_comment'></div>此结之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367524_comment'></div>岂结望尚书之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367524_comment'></div>古人所以爱经术之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367524_comment'></div>重山野之客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367524_comment'></div>采<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1367524", 1367524, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>舆童</span>之诵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367524_comment'></div>盖为其能明古以论今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367524_comment'></div>方正而不讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367524_comment'></div>悉人之下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367524_comment'></div>结虽昧于经术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367524_comment'></div>然自山野而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367524_comment'></div>能悉下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367524_comment'></div>尚书与国休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367524_comment'></div>能无问乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367524_comment'></div>事有在尚书力及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367524_comment'></div>能不行乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367524_comment'></div>结顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1367524_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泌阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b4e26d107d7b40e3b3f6cd71687aab0f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b4e26d107d7b40e3b3f6cd71687aab0f");'><span id='b4e26d107d7b40e3b3f6cd71687aab0f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>，42岁</div><div id='b4e26d107d7b40e3b3f6cd71687aab0f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　结收瘗战死者尸骨，作《哀丘表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（活动内容：曹玠杀山南东道节度使史翙，结为闻奏，特蒙嘉纳。）</span><div id='poem_1367615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哀邱表</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367615")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367615_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367615'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367615'>乾元庚子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367615_comment'></div>元子理兵于有泌之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367615_comment'></div>泌南至德丁酉为陷邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367615_comment'></div>乾元已亥为境上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367615_comment'></div>杀伤劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367615_comment'></div>言可极耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367615_comment'></div>街郭乱骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367615_comment'></div>如古屠肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367615_comment'></div>于是收而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367615_comment'></div>命曰哀邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367615_comment'></div>或曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367615_comment'></div>次山之命哀邱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367615_comment'></div>哀生人将尽而乱骨不藏者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367615_comment'></div>哀壮勇已死而名迹不显者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367615_comment'></div>对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367615_comment'></div>非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367615_comment'></div>吾哀凡人不能绝贪争毒乱之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367615_comment'></div>守正和仁让之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367615_comment'></div>至令吾有哀邱之怨欤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1367615_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　结屯泌阳守险，全十五城，以讨贼功，迁监察御史里行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　参山南东道来瑱府参谋，有文。作品：《请省官状》<div id='poem_1367518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请省官状<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>唐邓等州县官</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367518")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367518_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1367518_0'>① 乾元三年上来大夫</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367518'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367518'>右方城县旧万馀户今二百户已下其南阳向城等县更破碎于方城每县正员官及摄官共有六十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367518_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367518'>以前件如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367518_comment'></div>自经逆乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367518_comment'></div>州县残破。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367518_comment'></div>唐邓两州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367518_comment'></div>实为尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367518_comment'></div>荒草千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367518_comment'></div>是其疆畎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367518_comment'></div>万室空虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367518_comment'></div>是其井邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367518_comment'></div>乱骨相枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367518_comment'></div>是其百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367518_comment'></div>孤老寡弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367518_comment'></div>是其遗人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367518_comment'></div>哀而恤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367518_comment'></div>尚恐冤怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367518_comment'></div>肆其侵暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367518_comment'></div>实恐流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367518_comment'></div>今贼寇凭陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367518_comment'></div>镇兵资其给养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367518_comment'></div>今河路阻绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367518_comment'></div>邮驿在其供承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367518_comment'></div>若不触事救之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367518_comment'></div>无以劳勉其苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367518_comment'></div>为之计者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367518_comment'></div>在先省官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367518_comment'></div>其方城湖阳等县正官及摄官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367518_comment'></div>并户口多少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367518_comment'></div>具状如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367518_comment'></div>每县伏望量留令并佐官一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367518_comment'></div>馀并望勒停。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367518_comment'></div>谨录状上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1367518_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　编沈千运、王季友等七人诗为《箧中集》作品：《箧中集序》<div id='poem_1367531' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367531?labeling=true' target='_blank'>箧中集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367531")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367531_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367531'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367531'>元结作箧中集。或问曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367531_comment'></div>公所集之诗。何以订之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367531_comment'></div>对曰。风雅不兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367531_comment'></div>几及千岁。溺于时者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367531_comment'></div>世无人哉。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367531_comment'></div>有名位不显。年寿不终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367531_comment'></div>独无知音。不见称颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367531_comment'></div>死而已矣。谁云无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367531_comment'></div>近世作者。更相沿袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367531_comment'></div>拘限声病。喜尚形似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367531_comment'></div>且以流易为辞。不知丧于雅正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367531_comment'></div>然哉。彼则指咏时物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367531_comment'></div>会谐丝竹。与歌儿舞女生污惑之声于私可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367531_comment'></div>若令方直之士。大雅君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367531_comment'></div>听而诵之。则未见其可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367531_comment'></div>吴兴沈千运。独挺于流俗之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367531_comment'></div>强攘于已溺之后。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1367531", 1367531, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>穷老</span>不惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367531_comment'></div>五十馀年。凡所为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367531_comment'></div>皆与时异。故朋友后生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367531_comment'></div>稍见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1367531", 1367531, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>师效</span>。能似类者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367531_comment'></div>有五六人。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367531_comment'></div>自沈公及二三子。皆以正直而无禄位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367531_comment'></div>皆以忠信而久贫贱。皆以仁让而至丧亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367531_comment'></div>异于是者。显荣当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367531_comment'></div>谁为辩士。吾欲问之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367531_comment'></div>天下兵兴。于今六岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367531_comment'></div>人皆务武。斯焉谁嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367531_comment'></div>已长逝者。遗文散失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367531_comment'></div>方阻绝者。不见近作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367531_comment'></div>尽箧中所有。总编次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367531_comment'></div>命曰箧中集。且欲传之亲故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367531_comment'></div>冀其不亡。于今凡七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367531_comment'></div>诗二十二首。时乾元三年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367531_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1367531_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　结在来瑱幕府，有文。作品：《请给将士父母粮状》《请收养孤弱状》<div id='poem_1367520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请给将士父母粮状</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367520")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367520'>当军将二千人父随子者四人母随子者二十八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367520_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367520'>以前件如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367520_comment'></div>将士父母等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367520_comment'></div>皆因丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367520_comment'></div>不知所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367520_comment'></div>在于军中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367520_comment'></div>为日亦久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367520_comment'></div>夫孝而仁者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367520_comment'></div>可与言忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367520_comment'></div>而忠信者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367520_comment'></div>可以全义勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367520_comment'></div>岂有责其忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367520_comment'></div>使之义勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367520_comment'></div>而不劝之孝慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367520_comment'></div>恤以仁惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367520_comment'></div>今军中有父母者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367520_comment'></div>皆共分衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367520_comment'></div>先其父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367520_comment'></div>寒馁日甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367520_comment'></div>未尝有辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367520_comment'></div>其将士父母等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367520_comment'></div>伏望各量事给其衣食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367520_comment'></div>则义有所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367520_comment'></div>恩有所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367520_comment'></div>俾人感劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367520_comment'></div>实在于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367520_comment'></div>谨录状上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1367520_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367519' class='poemTitle href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367519")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367519'>当军孤弱小儿都七十六人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367519_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367519'>以前件状如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367519_comment'></div>小儿等无父母者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367519_comment'></div>乡国<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1367519", 1367519, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>沦陷</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367519_comment'></div>亲戚俱亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367519_comment'></div>谁家可归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367519_comment'></div>佣丐未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367519_comment'></div>有父兄者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367519_comment'></div>其父兄自经艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367519_comment'></div>久从征戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367519_comment'></div>多以忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367519_comment'></div>遭逢诛贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367519_comment'></div>有遗孤弱子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367519_comment'></div>不忍弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367519_comment'></div>力相恤养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367519_comment'></div>以至今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367519_comment'></div>迄令诸将有孤儿投军者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367519_comment'></div>许收驱使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367519_comment'></div>有孤弱子弟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367519_comment'></div>许令存养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367519_comment'></div>当军小儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367519_comment'></div>先取<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1367519", 1367519, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>回残</span>及<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1367519", 1367519, ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　辞监察御史，有文。作品：《辞监察御史表》<div id='poem_1367504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367504?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞监察御史表</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367504")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367504'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367504'>臣某言。臣伏奉某月日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367504_comment'></div>除臣监察御史里行。依前充山南东道节度参谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367504_comment'></div>忽承天泽。不胜庆喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367504_comment'></div>负荷恩任。伏增忧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367504_comment'></div>臣在至德元年。举家逃难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367504_comment'></div>生几于死。出自贼庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367504_comment'></div>远如海滨。敢望冠冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367504_comment'></div>陛下过听。疑臣有才谋可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367504_comment'></div>谓臣以忠正可嘉。枉以公诏徵臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367504_comment'></div>延问当时之事。言未可取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367504_comment'></div>荣宠已殊。事未可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367504_comment'></div>授任过次。其时以康元狡逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367504_comment'></div>陛下忧劳。臣亦不辞疲驽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367504_comment'></div>奉宣圣旨。招集士卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367504_comment'></div>师旅未成。又逢张瑾奸凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367504_comment'></div>再惊江汉。臣恐陛下忧无制变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367504_comment'></div>遂曾表请用兵。陛下嘉臣恳愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367504_comment'></div>频降恩诏。圣私殊甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367504_comment'></div>特加超擢至今。臣自布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367504_comment'></div>未踰数月。官忝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1367504", 1367504, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>风宪</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367504_comment'></div>任兼戎旅。今不劳兵革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367504_comment'></div>凶竖伏辜。臣不可终以无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367504_comment'></div>苟安非望。自奸臣逆命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367504_comment'></div>于今六年。愧无寸能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367504_comment'></div>苟求禄位。分符佩印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367504_comment'></div>不知惭羞。戮辱及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367504_comment'></div>死将不悔。陛下忍而从者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367504_comment'></div>其可胜言。臣才弱识下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367504_comment'></div>非智无谋。循涯顾分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367504_comment'></div>实自知耻。臣老母多病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367504_comment'></div>又无弟兄。漂流殊乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367504_comment'></div>孤弱相养。伏愿陛下矜臣愚钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367504_comment'></div>不合齿于朝列。念臣老母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367504_comment'></div>令臣得以奉养。则圣朝无辱官之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367504_comment'></div>山泽有纯孝之臣。不任悃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367504_comment'></div>谨遣某官奉表以闻。谨言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367504_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1367504_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　结在来瑱幕府，有诗。作品：《与党评事》<div id='poem_6060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与党评事</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6060")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6060_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6060'>大理评党晔，好閒自退，元子爱之，作诗赠焉。</div><div id='poem_preface_6060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6060'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6060'>自顾无功劳，一岁官再迁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6060'>跼身<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_6060", 6060, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>班次</span>中，常窃愧耻焉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6060'>加以久荒浪，惛愚性颇全。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6060'>未知在冠冕，不合无拘牵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6060'>勤强所不及，于人或未然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6060'>岂忘惠君子，恕之识见偏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6060'>且欲因我心，顺为理化先。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6060'>彼云万物情，有愿随所便。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6060'>爱君得自遂，令我空<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_6060", 6060, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>渊禅</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6060'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_6060_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年7月</a>　自号漫郎作《漫记》七篇。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
荆州（江陵）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e7bd6bcaeae4471a89c4c361835d8a23_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e7bd6bcaeae4471a89c4c361835d8a23");'><span id='e7bd6bcaeae4471a89c4c361835d8a23_link'
