href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年9月</a>　在荆州任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年</a>　在荆州任上，与党晔交往，有诗。作品：《与侍御》<div id='poem_6061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与党侍御</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6061")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6061_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6061'>庚子中，元子次山为监御史，党茂宗罢大理评事，次山爱其高尚，曾作诗一篇与之。及次山未辞殿中，茂宗已受监察，采茂宗尝相诮戏之意，又作诗与之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6061'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6061'>众坐吾独欢，或问欢为谁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6061'>高人党茂宗，复来官宪司。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6061'>昔吾顺元和，与世行自遗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6061'>茂宗正作吏，日有趋走疲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6061'>及吾污冠冕，茂宗方矫时。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6061'>诮吾顺让者，乃是干进资。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6061'>今将问茂宗，茂宗欲何辞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6061'>若云吾无心，此来复何为。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6061'>若云吾有羞，于此还见嗤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6061'>谁言万类心，闲之不可窥。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6061'>吾欲喻茂宗，茂宗宜听之。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6061'>长辕有修辙，驭者令尔驰。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6061'>山谷安可怨，筋力当自悲。<div id='poem_sentence_12_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_6061'>嗟嗟党茂宗，可为识者规。<div id='poem_sentence_13_6061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_6061'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_6061_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年</a>　在荆州任上，与韦洪州交往，有文。作品：《与韦洪州书》<div id='poem_1367526' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367526' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367526?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与韦洪州书</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367526")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367526_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367526'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367526'>某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367526_comment'></div>荆南节度判官水部员外郎兼殿中侍御史元结顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367526_comment'></div>某闻古之贤达居权位也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367526_comment'></div>令当世颂其德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367526_comment'></div>后世师其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367526_comment'></div>何以言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367526_comment'></div>在分君子小人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367526_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1367526", 1367526, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>察视</span>邪正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367526_comment'></div>使无冤滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367526_comment'></div>而无愤痛耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367526_comment'></div>某不能远取古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367526_comment'></div>请以端公贤公中丞为喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367526_comment'></div>前者获接端公馀论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367526_comment'></div>某尝议及中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367526_comment'></div>某以为赏中丞之功未当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367526_comment'></div>论中丞之冤至滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367526_comment'></div>端公不知情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367526_comment'></div>至泣涕交流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367526_comment'></div>岂不为有冤滥未申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367526_comment'></div>而生此愤痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367526_comment'></div>某与端公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367526_comment'></div>颇为亲故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367526_comment'></div>官又差肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367526_comment'></div>曾不垂问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367526_comment'></div>便即责使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367526_comment'></div>冤滥者岂独中丞而已乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367526_comment'></div>愤痛者岂独端公而已乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367526_comment'></div>所以至遣使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367526_comment'></div>试以自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367526_comment'></div>端公前牒则请不交兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367526_comment'></div>端公后牒则请速交兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367526_comment'></div>如此岂端公自察辨误耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367526_comment'></div>有小人惑乱端公耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367526_comment'></div>端公又云荆南将士侵暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367526_comment'></div>端公岂能保荆南将士必侵暴乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367526_comment'></div>岂能保淮西将士必不侵暴乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367526_comment'></div>端公少垂察问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367526_comment'></div>某又闻泗上邻家之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367526_comment'></div>请说以自喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367526_comment'></div>昔泗上有邻家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367526_comment'></div>有朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367526_comment'></div>游者斗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367526_comment'></div>游东家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367526_comment'></div>则曰公之友贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367526_comment'></div>能益主人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367526_comment'></div>西家之友愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367526_comment'></div>能损主人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367526_comment'></div>游西家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367526_comment'></div>则曰公之友智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367526_comment'></div>能誉主人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367526_comment'></div>东家之友狡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367526_comment'></div>能毁主人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367526_comment'></div>见其友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367526_comment'></div>亦如斗主人之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367526_comment'></div>于是邻家之友相恶将相害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367526_comment'></div>邻家之翁怒将相绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367526_comment'></div>里有正信之士为辨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367526_comment'></div>然后邻家通欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367526_comment'></div>邻友相善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367526_comment'></div>荆南与江西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367526_comment'></div>犹邻家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367526_comment'></div>某其友乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367526_comment'></div>游者方相斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367526_comment'></div>谁为正信之士一为辨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367526_comment'></div>某敢以此书献端公閤下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1367526_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367494")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367494_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367494'>天宝十四载。安禄山陷洛阳。明年。陷长安。天子幸蜀。太子即位于灵武。明年。皇帝移军凤翔。其年复两京。上皇还京师。于戏。前代帝王有盛德大业者。必见于歌颂。若今歌颂大业。刻之金石。非老于文学。其谁宜为。颂曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367494_comment'></div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1367494_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1367494'>何千万年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1367494_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年</a>　在荆州任上，与吕諲交往，有文。作品：《与吕相公书》<div id='poem_1367527' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367527' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367527?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与吕相公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367527")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367527_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367527'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367527'>某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367527_comment'></div>某官某再拜相公閤下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367527_comment'></div>某尝见时人不能自守性分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367527_comment'></div>俛仰于倾夺之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367527_comment'></div>低徊于名利之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367527_comment'></div>至有伤污毁辱之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367527_comment'></div>灭身亡家之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367527_comment'></div>则欲剧为之箴于身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367527_comment'></div>岂愿踰性分取祸辱而忘自箴者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367527_comment'></div>某性荒浪无拘限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367527_comment'></div>每不能节酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367527_comment'></div>与人相见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367527_comment'></div>适在一室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367527_comment'></div>不能无欢于醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367527_comment'></div>醉欢之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367527_comment'></div>不能无过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367527_comment'></div>少不学为吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367527_comment'></div>长又著书论自适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367527_comment'></div>昔天下太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367527_comment'></div>不敢绝世业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367527_comment'></div>亦欲求文学之官职员散冗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367527_comment'></div>为子孙计耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367527_comment'></div>自兵兴以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367527_comment'></div>此望亦绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367527_comment'></div>何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367527_comment'></div>某一身奉亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367527_comment'></div>奔走万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367527_comment'></div>所望饮啄承欢膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367527_comment'></div>今则辱在官以逾其性分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367527_comment'></div>触祸辱机兆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367527_comment'></div>日未无之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367527_comment'></div>某又三世单贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367527_comment'></div>年过四十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367527_comment'></div>弱子无母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367527_comment'></div>年未十岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367527_comment'></div>孤生嫁娶者一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367527_comment'></div>相公视某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367527_comment'></div>敢以身徇名利者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367527_comment'></div>有如某者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367527_comment'></div>以身徇名利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367527_comment'></div>齿于奴隶尚可羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367527_comment'></div>而况士君子也欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367527_comment'></div>某甚愚钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367527_comment'></div>又无功劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367527_comment'></div>自布衣历官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367527_comment'></div>不十月官至尚书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367527_comment'></div>向三岁官未削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367527_comment'></div>人多相荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367527_comment'></div>某实自忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367527_comment'></div>相公忍令某渐至畏惧而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367527_comment'></div>甚令必受祸辱而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367527_comment'></div>某前所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367527_comment'></div>相公似未见信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367527_comment'></div>故藉纸笔烦渎门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367527_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1367527_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年</a>　吕諲病剧江陵，结为之作《谢病表》作品：《为吕荆南谢病表》<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367512'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367512_comment'></div>臣自去秋<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1367512", id='poem_sentence_3_1367512_comment'></div>庶事不理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367512_comment'></div>某月日附某官口奏请替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367512_comment'></div>某月日又进状陈情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367512_comment'></div>未蒙允许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367512_comment'></div>伏增忧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367512_comment'></div>在臣病废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367512_comment'></div>岂敢偷安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367512_comment'></div>伏望天恩。<div id='poem_sentence_28_1367512_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年</a>　吕諲死，结代諲知荆南节度观察使事八月，境内晏然。作品：《吕公表》<div id='poem_1367616' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367616' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367616?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕公表</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367616_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367616'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367616'>上元二年。置南都于荆州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367616_comment'></div>为江陵府。使旧相东平吕公为江陵尹兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367616_comment'></div>分峡中湖南及武陵澧阳巴陵凡一十七州为荆南节度观察使。公理荆南三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367616_comment'></div>年五十一。薨于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367616_comment'></div>呜呼。使公年寿之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1367616", 1367616, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>不将</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367616_comment'></div>天其未厌兵革。不爱苍生欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367616_comment'></div>公明不尽人之私。惠不取人之爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367616_comment'></div>威不致人之惧。令不求人之犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367616_comment'></div>正不形人之僻。直不指人之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367616_comment'></div>故名不异俗。迹不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1367616", 1367616, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>矫时</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367616_comment'></div>内含<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1367616", 1367616, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>端明</span>。外与常规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367616_comment'></div>其大雅君子全于终始者邪。公所以进退其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367616_comment'></div>人不知其道。公所以再在台衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367616_comment'></div>人不知其德。颂元化者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367616_comment'></div>谁与颂乎。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367616_comment'></div>公将用于人。而不见其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367616_comment'></div>人将得于公。而公忘其所得乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367616_comment'></div>结等迹参<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1367616", id='poem_sentence_18_1367616_comment'></div>故刻金石。留于此邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367616_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1367616_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年</a>　吕諲死，结代諲知荆南节度观察使事。作品：《请节度使表》<div id='poem_1367505' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367505' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367505?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请节度使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367505'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367505'>臣某言。臣自以愚弱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1367505", 1367505, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>无堪</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367505_comment'></div>远迹江湖。全身之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367505_comment'></div>无所冀望。陛下过听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367505_comment'></div>徵臣顾问。今臣起家数月之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367505_comment'></div>官忝台省。尔来三岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367505_comment'></div>无益效用。愧耻之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367505_comment'></div>在臣无踰。臣窃以荆南是国家安危之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367505_comment'></div>伏愿陛下不轻易任人。陛下若独任武臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367505_comment'></div>则州县不理。若独任文吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367505_comment'></div>则戎事多阙。自兵兴以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367505_comment'></div>今八年矣。使战争未息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367505_comment'></div>百姓劳弊。多因任使不当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367505_comment'></div>致使败亡。伏惟陛下审择重臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367505_comment'></div>即日镇抚。全陛下上游之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367505_comment'></div>救愚臣不逮之急。谨遣某官奉表以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367505_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1367505_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年</a>　吕諲侄季重贫无所依，结作状以举之。作品：《举吕著作状》<div id='poem_1367513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举吕著作状</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1367513'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367513'>故荆南节度观察使江陵尹兼御史大夫吕諲侄男季重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367513_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367513'>右见任秘书省著作郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367513_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367513'>以前件状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367513_comment'></div>吕某立身无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367513_comment'></div>历官清俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367513_comment'></div>身殁之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367513_comment'></div>家无馀财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367513_comment'></div>长男幼小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367513_comment'></div>未了家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367513_comment'></div>前件侄质性纯厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367513_comment'></div>识理通敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367513_comment'></div>仁孝之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367513_comment'></div>不惭古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367513_comment'></div>自其疾甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367513_comment'></div>不视事向五六十日。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367513_comment'></div>处之无猜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367513_comment'></div>以臣所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367513_comment'></div>季重不独为贤子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367513_comment'></div>今时谷踊贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367513_comment'></div>道路多虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367513_comment'></div>漂流异乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367513_comment'></div>无以自给。<div class='inline' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年4月</a>　在荆州任上，有乞免官归养表。作品：《乞免官归养表》<div id='poem_1367506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免官归养表</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367506")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367506'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367506'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367506_comment'></div>臣以为才不称任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367506_comment'></div>位过其量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367506_comment'></div>不自知分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367506_comment'></div>祸辱皆及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367506_comment'></div>臣才不如人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367506_comment'></div>量识褊僻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367506_comment'></div>踰越秩次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367506_comment'></div>忝辱衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367506_comment'></div>人亦有惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367506_comment'></div>臣自知愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367506_comment'></div>臣少以愚弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367506_comment'></div>不愿为吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367506_comment'></div>书学自业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367506_comment'></div>老于儒家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367506_comment'></div>今迹在军中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367506_comment'></div>日预戎事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367506_comment'></div>此过臣才分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367506_comment'></div>近于祸辱者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367506_comment'></div>臣常恐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1367506", 1367506, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>荒浪</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367506_comment'></div>失于礼法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367506_comment'></div>自逸山泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367506_comment'></div>预于生类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367506_comment'></div>今秽污台省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367506_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1367506", 1367506, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>紊乱</span>时宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367506_comment'></div>此过臣才分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367506_comment'></div>近于祸辱者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367506_comment'></div>伏惟陛下察臣才分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367506_comment'></div>不令乱官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367506_comment'></div>则贪冒苟进之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367506_comment'></div>自臣知耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367506_comment'></div>陛下若官不失人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367506_comment'></div>则天下自理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367506_comment'></div>故曰天下理乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367506_comment'></div>系之官人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367506_comment'></div>臣以为官人之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367506_comment'></div>无敢易者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367506_comment'></div>陛下焉可易于臣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367506_comment'></div>臣无兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367506_comment'></div>老母久病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367506_comment'></div>所愿免官奉养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367506_comment'></div>生死愿足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367506_comment'></div>上不敢污陛下朝列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367506_comment'></div>是臣之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367506_comment'></div>下不欲贻老母忧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367506_comment'></div>是臣之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367506_comment'></div>愿全忠孝于今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367506_comment'></div>免祸辱于将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367506_comment'></div>伏惟陛下许臣免官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367506_comment'></div>许臣奉养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367506_comment'></div>在臣庆幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367506_comment'></div>无以比喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367506_comment'></div>谨遣某官奉表陈请以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1367506_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
九江（江州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f507e099c62446b7873fe737b13a72ef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f507e099c62446b7873fe737b13a72ef");'><span id='f507e099c62446b7873fe737b13a72ef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=761&endYear=761')">761年</a>，43岁</div><div id='f507e099c62446b7873fe737b13a72ef' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>结领荆南之兵镇于九江，有诗。作品：《与瀼溪邻里》《喻瀼溪乡旧游》<div id='poem_6062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6062' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6062?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与瀼溪邻里</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6062")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6062_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6062'>乾元元年，元子将家自全于瀼溪；上元二年，领荆南之兵镇于九江，方在军旅，与瀼溪邻里，不得如往时相见游。又知瀼溪之人，日转穷困，故作诗与之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6062_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6062'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6062'>昔年苦逆乱，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6062", 6062, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>举族</span>来南奔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6062'>日行几十里，爱君此山村。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6062'>峰谷呀回映，谁家无泉源。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6062'>修竹多夹路，扁舟皆到门。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6062'>瀼溪中曲滨，其阳有闲园。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6062'>邻里昔赠我，许之及子孙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6062'>我尝有匮乏，邻里能相分。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6062'>我尝有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_6062", 6062, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>不安</span>，邻里能相存。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6062'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_6062", 6062, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>斯人</span>转贫弱，力役非无冤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6062'>终以瀼滨讼，无令天下论。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6062'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_6062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6062'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6062)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_6118' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6118' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6118?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_6118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6118'>我心与瀼人，岂有辱与荣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6118'>瀼人异其心，应为我冠缨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6118'>昔贤恶如此，所以辞公卿。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6118'>贫穷老乡里，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_6118", 6118, onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_6118", 6118, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>饮啄</span>全此生。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（活动内容：元结与族弟源休皆为尚书郎在荆南府幕，休曾任湖南久理长沙，结将兵镇九江，自春及秋不得相见，抒怀以寄之。）</span><div id='poem_6113' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6113' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6113?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄源休</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6113")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6113_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6113'>辛丑中，元结与族弟源休皆为尚书郎，在荆南府幕，休以曾任湖南，久理长沙，结以曾游江州，将兵镇九江，自春及秋，不得相见，故抒所怀以寄之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6113_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6113'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6113'>天下未<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6113", 6113, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>偃兵</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6113", 6113, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>儒生</span>预戎事。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6113'>功劳安可问，且有忝官累。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6113'>昔常以荒浪，不敢学为吏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6113'>况当在兵家，言之岂容易。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6113'>忽然向三岭，境外为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_6113", 6113, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>偏帅</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6113'>时多尚矫诈，进退多欺贰。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6113'>纵有一直方，则上似奸智。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6113'>谁为明信者，能辨此劳畏。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6113'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_6113_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>结领荆南之兵镇于九江，送别韩方源，有诗。作品：《别韩方源》<div id='poem_1367535' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367535' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367535?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别韩方源序</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367535")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367535_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367535'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367535'>昔元次山与韩方源别于商馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367535_comment'></div>约不终岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367535_comment'></div>复相见于此山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367535_comment'></div>忽八年于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367535_comment'></div>始复相见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367535_comment'></div>悲欢之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367535_comment'></div>言可极邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367535_comment'></div>次山与方源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367535_comment'></div>昔年俱颐于山谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367535_comment'></div>有终焉之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367535_comment'></div>今方源得如其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367535_comment'></div>次山污在冠冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367535_comment'></div>次山一顾方源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367535_comment'></div>再三惭羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367535_comment'></div>时复饮酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367535_comment'></div>求其安我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367535_comment'></div>今方源欲安家肥阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367535_comment'></div>次山方理兵九江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367535_comment'></div>相醉相辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367535_comment'></div>不必如昔年之约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367535_comment'></div>此情岂易然者邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367535_comment'></div>乙未之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367535_comment'></div>次山有元子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367535_comment'></div>乙未之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367535_comment'></div>次山有猗玗子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367535_comment'></div>戊戌中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367535_comment'></div>次山有浪说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367535_comment'></div>悉赠方源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367535_comment'></div>庶方源见次山之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1367535_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>结领荆南之兵镇于九江，有文。作品：《左黄州表》<div id='poem_1367614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左黄州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（761年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367614")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367614'>乾元已亥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367614_comment'></div>赞善大夫左振出为黄州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367614_comment'></div>下车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367614_comment'></div>黄人歌曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367614_comment'></div>我欲逃乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367614_comment'></div>我欲去坟墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367614_comment'></div>左公今既来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367614_comment'></div>谁忍弃之去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367614_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367614_comment'></div>天下兵兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367614_comment'></div>今七年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367614_comment'></div>淮河之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367614_comment'></div>千里荒草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367614_comment'></div>自关已东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367614_comment'></div>海滨之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367614_comment'></div>屯兵百万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367614_comment'></div>不胜征税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367614_comment'></div>岂独黄人能使其人忍不去者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367614_comment'></div>谁曰不可颂乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367614_comment'></div>后一岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367614_comment'></div>黄人又歌曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367614_comment'></div>吾乡有鬼巫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367614_comment'></div>惑人人不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367614_comment'></div>天子正<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1367614", 1367614, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>尊信</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367614_comment'></div>左公能杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367614_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367614_comment'></div>近年以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367614_comment'></div>以阴阳变怪将鬼神之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367614_comment'></div>罔上惑下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367614_comment'></div>得尊重于当时者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367614_comment'></div>日见斯人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367614_comment'></div>黄之巫女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367614_comment'></div>亦以妖妄得蒙恩泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367614_comment'></div>朝廷不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367614_comment'></div>州县惟其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367614_comment'></div>公忿而杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367614_comment'></div>则彼可诛戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367614_comment'></div>岂独巫女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367614_comment'></div>如左公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367614_comment'></div>谁曰不可颂乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367614_comment'></div>三拜迁侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367614_comment'></div>判金州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367614_comment'></div>将去黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367614_comment'></div>人多去思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367614_comment'></div>故为黄人作表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367614_comment'></div>如左氏世系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367614_comment'></div>左公历官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367614_comment'></div>及黄之门生故吏与巫女事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367614_comment'></div>则南阳左公能悉记之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1367614_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
鄂州（武昌）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f9b95548242a4e8bb32a6e2b5e0b9ec8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f9b95548242a4e8bb32a6e2b5e0b9ec8");'><span id='f9b95548242a4e8bb32a6e2b5e0b9ec8_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年</a>　在鄂州，放情山水，以耕钓自娱，有文。作品：《自释》<div id='poem_1367529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367529?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自释书</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1367529'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367529'>河南元氏望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367529_comment'></div>结元子名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367529_comment'></div>次山结字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367529_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>世业</span>载国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367529_comment'></div>世系在家牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367529_comment'></div>少居商馀山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367529_comment'></div>著元子十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367529_comment'></div>故以元子为称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367529_comment'></div>天下兵兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367529_comment'></div>逃乱入猗玗洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367529_comment'></div>始称猗玗子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367529_comment'></div>后家瀼滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367529_comment'></div>乃自称浪士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367529_comment'></div>及有官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367529_comment'></div>人以为浪者亦漫为官乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367529_comment'></div>呼为漫郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367529_comment'></div>既客樊上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367529_comment'></div>漫遂显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367529_comment'></div>樊左右皆渔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367529_comment'></div>少长相戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367529_comment'></div>更曰聱叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367529_comment'></div>彼诮以聱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367529_comment'></div>为其不相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>从听</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367529_comment'></div>不相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>钩加</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367529_comment'></div>带笭箵而尽船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367529_comment'></div>独<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>聱牙</span>而挥车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367529_comment'></div>酒徒得此又曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367529_comment'></div>公之漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367529_comment'></div>其犹聱乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367529_comment'></div>公守著作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367529_comment'></div>不带笭箵乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367529_comment'></div>又<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>漫浪</span>于人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367529_comment'></div>得非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>聱牙</span>乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367529_comment'></div>公漫久矣。<div class='inline' class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>从听</span>于时俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367529_comment'></div>不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>钩加</span>于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367529_comment'></div>谁是聱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367529_comment'></div>吾欲从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367529_comment'></div>彼聱叟不惭带乎笭箵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367529_comment'></div>吾又安能薄乎著作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367529_comment'></div>彼聱叟不羞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>聱牙</span>于邻里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367529_comment'></div>吾又安能惭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>漫浪</span>于人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367529_comment'></div>取而醉人议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367529_comment'></div>当以漫叟为称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367529_comment'></div>直荒浪其情性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367529_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1367529", 1367529, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>诞漫</span>其所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367529_comment'></div>使人知无所存有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367529_comment'></div>无所将待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367529_comment'></div>乃为语曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367529_comment'></div>能带笭箵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367529_comment'></div>全独而保生。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6101'>偶得凶丑降，功劳愧方寸。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6101'>尔来将四岁，惭耻言可尽。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6101'>请取冤者辞，为吾忝官引。<div id='poem_sentence_12_6101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_6101'>冤辞何者苦，万邑馀灰烬。<div id='poem_sentence_13_6101_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_6101'>冤辞何者悲，生人尽锋刃。<div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6048'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6048'>将牛何处去，耕彼故城东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6048'>相伴有田父，相欢惟牧童。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6048'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_6048_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6136' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6136' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6136?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span id='poem_content_6136'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6136'>将牛何处去，耕彼西阳城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6136'>叔闲修农具，直者伴我耕<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6136'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_6136_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_6136'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_6136_0'>⑴ 叔闲，漫叟韦氏甥。直者，漫叟长子也</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_6136_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_6137' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6137' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6137?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>将船何处去</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6137_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6137'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6137'>将船何处去，钓彼大回中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6137'>叔静能鼓桡，正者随弱翁<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6137'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_6137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_6137'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_6137_0'>⑴ 叔静，漫翁李氏甥。正者，漫翁次子也</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_6137_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_6049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6049?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>将船何处去</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6049_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6049'>壬寅中，漫叟得免职事，漫家樊上，修耕钓以自资，作〈漫歌八曲〉与县大夫孟士源，欲士源唱而和之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6049'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6049'>将船何处去，送客小回南。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6049'>有时逢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_6049", 6049, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>恶客</span>，还家亦少酣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6049'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_6049_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年</a>　在鄂州，放情山水，以耕钓自娱，有文。作品：《漫论》《抔樽铭》《抔湖铭》《退谷铭》<div id='poem_1367549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>漫论</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367549")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367549_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367549'>乾元已亥至宝应壬寅岁。时人相诮议曰。元次山尝漫有所为。且漫聚兵。又漫辞官。漫闻议云云。因作漫论。论曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367549'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367549'>世有规检大夫持规之徒。来问叟曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367549_comment'></div>公漫然何为。对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367549_comment'></div>漫为公也。漫何以然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367549_comment'></div>对曰漫然。规者怒曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367549_comment'></div>人以漫指公者。是他家恶公之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367549_comment'></div>何得翻不恶漫。而称漫为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367549_comment'></div>漫何<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1367549", 1367549, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>检括</span>。漫何操持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367549_comment'></div>漫何是非。漫不足准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367549_comment'></div>漫不足规。漫无所用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367549_comment'></div>漫无所施。漫焉何效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367549_comment'></div>漫焉何师。公发已白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367549_comment'></div>无终惑之。叟俛首而谢曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367549_comment'></div>吾不意公之说漫至于此。意如所说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367549_comment'></div>漫焉足耻。吾当于漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367549_comment'></div>终身不羞。著书作论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367549_comment'></div>当为漫流。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367549_comment'></div>九流百氏。有定限邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367549_comment'></div>吾自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1367549", 1367549, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>分张</span>。独为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1367549", 1367549, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>漫家</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367549_comment'></div>规检之徒。则奈我何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367549_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1367549_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367565' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367565' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367565?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抔樽铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367565")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367565_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367565'>郎亭西郛有丛石。石临樊水。漫叟构石颠以为亭。石有窊颠者。因修之以藏酒。士源爱之。命为抔樽。乃为士源作抔樽铭。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367565_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367565'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367565'>窊颠之石，在吾亭上。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367565'>天全其器，实有殊状。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367565'>如窦而底，似倾几欹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367565'>非曲非方，不准不规。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367565'>孟公高贤，命曰抔樽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367565'>漫叟作铭，当欲何言。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367565'>时俗浇狡，日益伪薄。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367565'>谁能抔饮，共守淳朴。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367565_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367565'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1367565_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367567' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367567' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367567?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抔湖铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367567")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367567_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367567'>抔湖东抵抔樽。西侵退谷。北汇樊水。南涯郎亭。有菱有荷。有菰有蒲。方一二里。能浮水与。漫叟自抔亭游退谷。必泛此湖。以湖在抔樽之下。遂命曰抔湖。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367567_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367567'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367567'>谁游江海，能厌其大。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367567'>谁泛抔湖，能厌其小。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367567'>故曰人不厌者，君子之道。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367567'>于戏君子，人不厌之。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367567'>死虽千岁，其行可师。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367567'>可厌之类，不独为害。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367567'>死虽万代，独堪污秽。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367567'>或问作铭，意尽此欤。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367567'>吾欲为人厌者，勿泛抔湖。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367567_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367567'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1367567_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>退谷铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367566")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367566_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367566'>抔湖西南是退谷。谷中有泉。或激或悬。为窦为渊。满谷生寿木。又多寿藤萦之。始入谷口。令人忘返。时士源以漫叟退修耕钓。爱游此谷。遂命曰退谷。元子作铭。以显士源之意。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367566'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367566'>谁命退谷，孟公士源。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367566'>孟公之意，漫叟知焉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367566'>公畏漫叟，心进迹退。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367566'>公惧漫叟，名显身晦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367566'>公恐漫叟，辞小受大。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367566'>于戏退谷，独为吾规。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367566'>干进之客，不羞游之。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367566'>何人作铭，铭之谷口。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367566'>荒浪者欤，退谷漫叟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367566'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1367566_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年</a>　冬在鄂州，放情山水，会孟士源有诗。作品：《招孟武昌》<div id='poem_6102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>招孟武昌</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6102")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6102_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6102'>漫叟作〈退谷铭〉，指曰：「干进之客，不能游之。」作〈杯湖铭〉，指曰：「为人厌者，勿泛杯湖。」孟士源尝黜官，无情干进，在武昌不为人厌，可游退谷，可泛杯湖，故作诗招之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6102'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6102'>风霜枯万物，退谷如春时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6102'>穷冬涸江海，杯湖澄清漪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6102'>湖尽到谷口，单船近阶墀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6102'>湖中更何好，坐见大江水。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6102'>欹石为水涯，半山在湖里。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6102'>谷口更何好，绝壑流寒泉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6102'>松桂荫茅舍，白云生坐边。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6102'>武昌不干进，武昌人不厌。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6102'>退谷正可游，杯湖任来泛。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6102'>湖上有水鸟，见人不飞鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6102'>谷口有山兽，往往随人行。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6102'>莫将车马来，令我鸟兽惊。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6102'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_6102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6102'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6102)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年</a>　冬在鄂州，放情山水，雪中怀孟士源，有诗。作品：《雪中怀孟武昌》<div id='poem_6115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6115?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪中怀孟武昌</a><span class='authorDate'>（762年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6115")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6115'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6115'>冬来三度雪，农者欢岁稔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6115'>我麦根已濡，各得在仓廪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6115'>天寒未能起，孺子惊人寝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6115'>云有山客来，篮中见冬蕈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6115'>烧柴为温酒，煮鳜为作沈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6115'>客亦爱杯尊，思君共杯饮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6115'>所嗟山路閒，时节寒又甚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6115'>不能苦相邀，兴尽还就枕。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6115'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_6115_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　新春大雪，孟士源以诗问之，结作诗相酬。作品：《酬孟武昌苦雪》<div id='poem_6126' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6126' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6126?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬孟武昌苦雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6126")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6126'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6126'>积雪闲山路，有人到庭前。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6126'>云是孟武昌，令献苦雪篇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6126'>长吟未及终，不觉为凄然。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6126'>古之贤达者，与世竟何异。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6126'>不能救<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_6126", 6126, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>时患</span>，讽谕<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作论）</span>以全意。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6126'>知公惜春物，岂非爱时和。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6126'>知公苦阴雪，伤彼灾患多。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6126'>奸凶正驱驰，不合问君子。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6126'>林莺与野兽，无乃怨于此。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6126'>兵兴向九岁，稼穑谁能忧。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6126'>何时不发卒，何日不杀牛。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6126'>耕者日已少，耕牛日已希。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6126'>皇天复何忍，更又恐毙之。<div id='poem_sentence_12_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_6126'>自经危乱来，触物堪伤叹。<div id='poem_sentence_13_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_6126'>见君问我意，只益胸中乱。<div id='poem_sentence_14_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_6126'>山禽饥不飞，山木冻皆折。<div id='poem_sentence_15_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_6126'>悬泉化为冰，寒水近不热。<div id='poem_sentence_16_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_6126'>出门望天地，天地皆昏昏。<div id='poem_sentence_17_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_6126'>时见双峰下，雪中生白云。<div id='poem_sentence_18_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_6126'></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_6126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　结浪游吴中，王去西蜀，对酒欲别，有诗。作品：《别王佐卿》<div id='poem_1367536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别王佐卿序</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367536")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367536_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367536'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367536'>癸卯岁。京兆王契佐卿年四十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367536_comment'></div>河南元结次山年四十五。时次山顷日浪游吴中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367536_comment'></div>佐卿顷日去西蜀。对酒欲别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367536_comment'></div>此情易邪。在少年时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367536_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1367536", 1367536, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>握手</span>笑别。虽远不恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367536_comment'></div>以天下无事。志气犹壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367536_comment'></div>今与佐卿年近五十。又逢战争未息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367536_comment'></div>相去万里。欲强笑别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367536_comment'></div>其可得乎。与佐卿去者有清河崔异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367536_comment'></div>与次山住者有彭城刘湾。相醉相留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367536_comment'></div>几日江畔。主人鄂州刺史韦延安令四座作诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367536_comment'></div>命余为序。以送远云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367536_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1367536_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　岳州刺史夏侯公殁于私家，有文。作品：《夏侯岳州表》<div id='poem_1367618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏侯岳州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367618")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367618'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367618'>癸卯岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367618_comment'></div>岳州刺史夏侯公没于私家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367618_comment'></div>门人弟子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367618_comment'></div>爱思不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367618_comment'></div>愿旌遗德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367618_comment'></div>将显来世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367618_comment'></div>会予诏许优闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367618_comment'></div>家于樊上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367618_comment'></div>故为公作表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367618_comment'></div>庚子中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367618_comment'></div>公镇岳州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367618_comment'></div>予时为尚书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367618_comment'></div>在荆南幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367618_comment'></div>尝因廉问到公之州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367618_comment'></div>其时天下兵兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367618_comment'></div>已六七年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367618_comment'></div>人疲州小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367618_comment'></div>比太平时力役百倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367618_comment'></div>公能清正恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367618_comment'></div>静以理之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367618_comment'></div>故其人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1367618", 1367618, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>安和</span>而服悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367618_comment'></div>为当时法则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367618_comment'></div>及公罢归州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367618_comment'></div>公家与吾相邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367618_comment'></div>见公在州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367618_comment'></div>与山野童孺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367618_comment'></div>与当道辞色均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367618_comment'></div>若语是非得丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367618_comment'></div>语夭寿哀乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367618_comment'></div>恋意澹然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367618_comment'></div>吾是以知道胜于内者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367618_comment'></div>物莫能挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367618_comment'></div>德充于外者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367618_comment'></div>事不能诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367618_comment'></div>公之所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367618_comment'></div>其独有乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367618_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367618_comment'></div>公既寿而贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367618_comment'></div>保家<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1367618", 1367618, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>全归</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367618_comment'></div>于今之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367618_comment'></div>谁不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1367618", 1367618, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>荣羡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367618_comment'></div>至于公之世嗣与公官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367618_comment'></div>则本县大夫李公状著之矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1367618_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　在鄂州，夏有诗酬贾德方。作品：《漫酬贾沔州》<div id='poem_6132' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6132' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6132?labeling=true' target='_blank'>漫酬贾沔州</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6132")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6132_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6132'>贾德方与漫叟者，惧漫叟不能甘穷独，惧漫叟又须为官，故作诗相喻其指曰：「劝尔莫作官，作官不益身。」因德方之意，遂漫酬之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6132_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6132'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6132'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6132", 6132, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>往年</span>壮心在，尝欲济<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6132", 6132, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>时难</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6132'>奉诏举州兵，令得诛暴叛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6132'>上将屡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_6132", 6132, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>颠覆</span>，偏师尝救乱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6132'>未曾弛戈甲，终日领<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_6132", 6132, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>簿案</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6132'>出入四五年，忧劳忘昏旦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6132'>无谋静凶丑，自觉愚且愞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6132'>岂欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_6132", 6132, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>皂枥</span>中，争食麧<span class='inlineComment2'>（下汲切）</span>与藖<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6132'>去年辞职事，所惧贻忧患。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6132'>天子许安亲，官又得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_6132", 6132, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>闲散</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6132'>自家樊水上，性情尤荒慢。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6132'>云山与水木，似不憎吾漫。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6132'>以兹忘时世，日益无畏惮。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6132'>漫醉人不嗔，漫眠人不唤。<div id='poem_sentence_12_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_6132'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_6132", 6132, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>漫游</span>无远近，漫乐无早晏。<div id='poem_sentence_13_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_6132'>漫中漫亦忘，名利谁能算。<div id='poem_sentence_14_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_6132'>闻君劝我意，为君一长叹。<div id='poem_sentence_15_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_6132'>人谁年八十，我已过其半。<div id='poem_sentence_16_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_6132'>家中孤弱子，长子未及冠。<div id='poem_sentence_17_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_6132'>且为儿童主，种药老溪涧。<div id='poem_sentence_18_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_6132'></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_6132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_6132'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_6132_1'>⑴ 下辨切。麧，糠中可食者，牛马食馀草节曰藖</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_6132_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　在鄂州，有文。作品：《广宴亭记》<div id='poem_1367544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广宴亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367544")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367544'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367544'>樊水东尽其南。乃樊山北鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367544_comment'></div>津吏欲于鲜上以为候舍。漫叟家于樊上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367544_comment'></div>不醉则闲。乃相其地形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367544_comment'></div>验之图记。实吴故宴游之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367544_comment'></div>县大夫马公登之。叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367544_comment'></div>谢公赠伏武昌诗云。樊山开广宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367544_comment'></div>非此地邪。吾欲因而修之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367544_comment'></div>命曰广宴亭。何如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367544_comment'></div>漫叟颂之曰。古人将修废遗尤异之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367544_comment'></div>为君子之道。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367544_comment'></div>天下有废遗尤异之事如此亭者。谁能修而旌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367544_comment'></div>天将厌悔往乎。使公方壮而有是心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367544_comment'></div>吾当裁蓄简札。待为之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367544_comment'></div>故作广宴亭记。以先意云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367544_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1367544_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　在鄂州，登殊亭有文。作品：《殊亭记》<div id='poem_1367542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367542?labeling=true' target='_blank'>殊亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367542")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367542_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367542'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367542'>癸卯中。扶风马向兼理武昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367542_comment'></div>以明信严断惠正为理。故政不待时而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367542_comment'></div>于戏。若明而不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367542_comment'></div>严而不断。惠而不正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367542_comment'></div>虽欲理身。终不自理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367542_comment'></div>况于人哉。公能令人理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367542_comment'></div>使身多暇。招我畏暑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367542_comment'></div>且为凉亭。亭临大江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367542_comment'></div>复在山上。佳木相荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367542_comment'></div>常多清风。巡回极望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367542_comment'></div>目不厌远。吾见公才殊政殊迹殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367542_comment'></div>为此亭又殊。因命之曰殊亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367542_comment'></div>斲石刻记。立于亭侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367542_comment'></div>庶几来者。无所憾焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367542_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1367542_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　在鄂州，登殊亭作诗。作品：《登殊亭作》<div id='poem_6124' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6124' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6124?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登殊亭作</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6124")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6124_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6124'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6124'>时节方大暑，试来登殊亭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6124'>凭轩未及息，忽若秋气生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6124'>主人既多闲，有酒共我倾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6124'>坐中不相异，岂恨醉与醒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6124'>漫歌无人听，浪语无人惊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6124'>时复一回望，心目出四溟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6124'>谁能守缨佩，日与灾患并。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6124_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6124_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　在鄂州樊上，有诗文。作品：《樊上漫作》<div id='poem_6139' id='poem_sentence_0_6139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6139'>去郭五六里，扁舟到门前。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6117?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喻常吾直<span class='inlineComment2'>（时为摄官）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6117")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6117_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6117'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6117'>山泽多饥人，闾里多坏屋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6117'>战争且未息，徵敛何时足。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6117'>不能救人患，不合食天粟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6117'>何况假一官，而苟求其禄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6117'>近年更长吏，数月未为速。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6117'>来者罢而官，岂得不为辱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6117'>劝为辞府主，从我游退谷。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6117'>谷中有寒泉，为尔洗尘服。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6117_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6117'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_6117_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6116' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6116' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6116?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喻旧部曲</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_6116'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6116'>漫游樊水阴，忽见旧部曲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6116'>尚言军中好，犹望有所属。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6116'>故令争者心，至死终不足。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6116'>与之一杯酒，喻使烧戎服。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6116'>兵兴向十年，所见堪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_6116", 6116, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>叹哭</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6116_comment'></div></div><div
