target='_blank'>惠公禅居表</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367617")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367617_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367617'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367617'>溯樊水二百馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367617_comment'></div>有涌溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367617_comment'></div>入溪八九里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367617_comment'></div>有蛇山之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367617_comment'></div>是惠公禅居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367617_comment'></div>禅师以无情待人之有情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367617_comment'></div>以有为全已之无欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367617_comment'></div>各因其性分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367617_comment'></div>莫不与善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367617_comment'></div>知人困穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367617_comment'></div>喻使耕织。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367617_comment'></div>因人灾患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367617_comment'></div>劝守仁信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367617_comment'></div>故闾里相化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367617_comment'></div>耻为弋钓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367617_comment'></div>日勤种植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367617_comment'></div>不五六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367617_comment'></div>沮泽有沟塍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367617_comment'></div>荒皋有阡陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367617_comment'></div>桑果竹园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367617_comment'></div>如伊洛间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367617_comment'></div>所以爱禅师者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367617_comment'></div>无全行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367617_comment'></div>无全道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367617_comment'></div>岂能及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367617_comment'></div>乡人欲增修塔庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367617_comment'></div>托禅师以求福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367617_comment'></div>禅师亦随人之意而制造焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367617_comment'></div>直门临溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367617_comment'></div>广堂背山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367617_comment'></div>庭列双台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367617_comment'></div>修廓夏寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367617_comment'></div>松竹苍苍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367617_comment'></div>周流清泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367617_comment'></div>岑岭复抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367617_comment'></div>众山回旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367617_comment'></div>斯亦旷绝之殊境矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367617_comment'></div>吾以所疑咨于禅师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367617_comment'></div>禅师曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367617_comment'></div>我恐人忘善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367617_comment'></div>以事诱人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367617_comment'></div>及人将善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367617_comment'></div>固不以事为累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367617_comment'></div>吾以所惑咨于禅师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367617_comment'></div>禅师曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367617_comment'></div>公若以惑相问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367617_comment'></div>我亦惑于问焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367617_comment'></div>公若无惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367617_comment'></div>我亦何对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367617_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367617_comment'></div>吾漫浪者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367617_comment'></div>焉能尽禅师之意乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367617_comment'></div>县大夫孟彦深王文渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367617_comment'></div>识名显当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367617_comment'></div>必能尽禅师之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367617_comment'></div>故命之作赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367617_comment'></div>赞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367617_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1367617'>圣者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1367617", 1367617, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>忘迹</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367617_comment'></div>达人化心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367617_comment'></div>惠公之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367617_comment'></div>无得而寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367617_comment'></div>如山出云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367617_comment'></div>如水涵月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1367617_comment'></div>惠公得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1367617_comment'></div>演用不竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1367617_comment'></div>无情之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1367617_comment'></div>可洽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1367617", 1367617, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>群黎</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1367617_comment'></div>将引天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1367617_comment'></div>同于涌溪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1367617_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　在鄂州，有文。作品：《化虎论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（系年作品：当为宝应元年及广德元年间家樊上时所作。）</span><div id='poem_1367550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>化虎论</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367550")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367550_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367550'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367550'>都昌县大夫张粲君英将之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367550_comment'></div>与其友贾德方元次山别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367550_comment'></div>且曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367550_comment'></div>吾邑多山泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367550_comment'></div>可致麋鹿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367550_comment'></div>为二贤羞宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367550_comment'></div>何如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367550_comment'></div>及到官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367550_comment'></div>书与二友曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367550_comment'></div>待我化行旬月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367550_comment'></div>使虎为鹿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367550_comment'></div>豹为麇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367550_comment'></div>枭为鹧鸪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367550_comment'></div>虾蟆为兔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367550_comment'></div>将以丰江外庖厨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367550_comment'></div>岂独与德方次山之羞宾客也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367550_comment'></div>德方对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367550_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367550_comment'></div>兵兴岁久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367550_comment'></div>战争日甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367550_comment'></div>生人怨痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367550_comment'></div>何时休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367550_comment'></div>君英之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367550_comment'></div>岂及虎豹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367550_comment'></div>将恐虎窟公城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367550_comment'></div>豹游公庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367550_comment'></div>枭集公楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367550_comment'></div>群蛙匝公而鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367550_comment'></div>敢以不然之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367550_comment'></div>反化君英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367550_comment'></div>次山异德方报君英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367550_comment'></div>化虎之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367550_comment'></div>岂直望化虎哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367550_comment'></div>次山请商之君英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367550_comment'></div>所谓待吾化虎然后羞吾属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367550_comment'></div>其意盖欲待朝廷化小人为君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367550_comment'></div>化谄媚为公直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367550_comment'></div>化奸邪为忠信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367550_comment'></div>化进竞为退让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367550_comment'></div>化刑法为典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367550_comment'></div>化仁义为道德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367550_comment'></div>使天下之人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367550_comment'></div>皆涵纯朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367550_comment'></div>岂止化虎而羞我哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367550_comment'></div>德方未量君英欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367550_comment'></div>次山故编所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367550_comment'></div>为化虎之论。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1367550_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年12月</a>　十二月于鄂州启程赴任。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
道县（道州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='115f567b7dbd43b8982114018e0478e0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("115f567b7dbd43b8982114018e0478e0");'><span id='115f567b7dbd43b8982114018e0478e0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=765')">764-765年</a>，46-47岁</div><div id='115f567b7dbd43b8982114018e0478e0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年5月22日</a>　到道州，行古人之政,有文。作品：《谢上表》<div id='poem_1367509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367509?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（764年5月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367509")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367509_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367509'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367509'>臣某言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367509_comment'></div>去年九月敕授道州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367509_comment'></div>属西戎侵轶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367509_comment'></div>至十二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367509_comment'></div>臣始于鄂州授敕牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367509_comment'></div>即日赴任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367509_comment'></div>臣州先被西原贼屠陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367509_comment'></div>节度使已差官摄刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367509_comment'></div>兼又闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367509_comment'></div>臣在道路待恩命者三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367509_comment'></div>臣以五月二十二日到州上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367509_comment'></div>耆老见臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367509_comment'></div>俯伏而泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367509_comment'></div>官吏见臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367509_comment'></div>已无菜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367509_comment'></div>城池井邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367509_comment'></div>但生荒草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367509_comment'></div>登高极望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367509_comment'></div>不见人烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367509_comment'></div>岭南数州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367509_comment'></div>与臣接近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367509_comment'></div>馀寇蚁聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367509_comment'></div>尚未归降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367509_comment'></div>臣见招辑流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367509_comment'></div>率劝贫弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367509_comment'></div>保守城邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367509_comment'></div>畬种山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367509_comment'></div>冀望秋后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367509_comment'></div>少可全活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367509_comment'></div>臣愚以为今日刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367509_comment'></div>若无武略以制暴乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367509_comment'></div>若无文才以救疲弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367509_comment'></div>若不清廉以身率下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367509_comment'></div>若不变通以救时须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367509_comment'></div>一州之人不叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367509_comment'></div>则乱将作矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367509_comment'></div>岂止一州者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367509_comment'></div>臣料今日州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367509_comment'></div>堪征税者无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367509_comment'></div>已破败者实多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367509_comment'></div>百姓恋坟墓者盖少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367509_comment'></div>思流亡者乃众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367509_comment'></div>则刺史宜精选谨择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367509_comment'></div>以委任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367509_comment'></div>固不可拘限官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367509_comment'></div>得之货贿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367509_comment'></div>出之权门者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367509_comment'></div>凡授刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367509_comment'></div>特望陛下一年问其流亡归复几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367509_comment'></div>田畴垦辟几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367509_comment'></div>二年问畜养比初年几倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367509_comment'></div>可税比初年几倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367509_comment'></div>三年计其功过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367509_comment'></div>必行赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367509_comment'></div>则人皆不敢冀望侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367509_comment'></div>苟有所求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367509_comment'></div>臣实孱弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367509_comment'></div>辱陛下符节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367509_comment'></div>陛下必当谨择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367509_comment'></div>臣固宜废归山野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367509_comment'></div>供给井税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367509_comment'></div>臣不任恳之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367509_comment'></div>谨遣某官奉表陈谢以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1367509_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>　到官未五十日诸使征求，符牒二百余封，结以应命则州县乱，违命又必获罪戾，作诗抒其宁待罪以安民，毋邀功而贼民之意。作品：《舂陵行》<div id='poem_6114' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6114' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6114?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舂陵行</a><span class='authorDate'>（764年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6114")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6114_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6114'>癸卯岁，漫叟道州刺史，道州旧四万馀户，经贼已来，不满四千，大半不胜赋税，到官未五十日，承诸使徵求符牒二百馀封，皆曰：「失其限者罪至贬削。」于戏！若悉应其命，则州县破乱，刺史欲焉逃罪，若不应命，又即获罪戾，必不免也。吾将守官，静以安人，待罪而已。此州是舂陵故地，作〈舂陵行〉以达下情。</div><div id='poem_preface_6114_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_6114'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1068, "poem_allusion_6114")'>采诗</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_6114_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6114'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6114'>军国多所需，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6114", 6114, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>切责</span>在有司。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6114'>有司临郡县，刑法竞欲施。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6114'>供给岂不忧，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_6114", 6114, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>徵敛</span>又可悲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6114'>州小经<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_6114", 6114, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>乱亡</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_6114", 6114, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>遗人</span>实困疲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6114'>大乡无十家，大族命<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_6114", 6114, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>单羸</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6114'>朝餐是草根，暮食仍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_6114", 6114, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>木皮</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6114'>出言气欲绝，意速行步迟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6114'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_6114", 6114, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>追呼</span>尚不忍，况乃鞭扑之。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6114'>郭亭传急符，来往迹相追。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6114'>更无宽大恩，但有迫促期。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6114'>欲令鬻儿女，言发恐乱随。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6114'>悉使索其家，而又无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_6114", 6114, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>生资</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6114'>听彼道路言，怨伤谁复知。<div id='poem_sentence_12_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_6114'>去冬山贼来，杀夺几无遗。<div id='poem_sentence_13_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_6114'>所愿见王官，抚养以惠慈。<div id='poem_sentence_14_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_6114'>奈何重<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_6114", 6114, id='poem_sentence_16_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_6114'>州县忽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_6114", 6114, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>乱亡</span>，得罪复是谁。<div id='poem_sentence_17_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_6114'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_6114", 6114, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>逋缓</span>违诏令，蒙责固其宜。<div id='poem_sentence_18_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_6114'>前贤重守分，恶以祸福移。<div id='poem_sentence_19_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_6114'>亦云贵守官，不爱能适时。<div id='poem_sentence_20_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_6114'>顾惟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_6114", 6114, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>孱弱</span>者，正直当不亏。<div id='poem_sentence_21_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_6114'>何人采国风，吾欲献此辞。<div id='poem_sentence_22_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_6114'></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_6114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6114'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6114)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>　西原民攻永州，破邵，不犯道州，有诗。作品：《贼退示官吏》<div id='poem_6109' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6109' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6109?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贼退示官吏</a><span class='authorDate'>（764年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6109")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6109_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6109'>癸卯岁，西原贼入道州，焚烧杀掠（杀掠），几尽而去。明年，贼又攻永破邵，不犯此州边鄙而退，岂力能制敌欤？盖蒙其伤怜而已。诸使何为苦徵敛，故作诗一篇以示官吏。</div><div id='poem_preface_6109_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6109'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6109'>昔岁逢太平，山林二十年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6109'>泉源在庭户，洞壑当门前。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6109'>井税有常期，日晏犹得眠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6109'>忽然遭世变，数岁亲戎旃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6109'>今来典斯郡，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_6109", 6109, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>山夷</span>又纷然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6109'>城小贼不屠，人贫伤可怜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6109'>是以陷邻境，此州独见全。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6109'>使臣将王命，岂不如贼焉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6109'>今彼徵敛者，迫之如火煎。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6109'>谁能绝人命，以作时世贤。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6109'>思欲委符节，引竿自刺船。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6109'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_6109", 6109, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>将家</span>就鱼麦，归老江湖边。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6109'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_6109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6109'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6109)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>　进《免科率状》，请免百姓所负租税等十三万贯，代宗许之。<div id='poem_1367514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏免科率状</a><span class='authorDate'>（764年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367514")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367514'>当州准敕及租庸等使徵率钱物都计一十三万六千三百八十八贯八百文一十三万二千四百八十贯九百文岭南西原贼未破州已前三千九百七贯九百文贼退后徵率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367514_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367514'>以前件如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367514_comment'></div>臣自到州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367514_comment'></div>见租庸等诸使文牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367514_comment'></div>令徵前件钱物送纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367514_comment'></div>臣当州被西原贼屠陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367514_comment'></div>贼停留一月馀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367514_comment'></div>焚烧粮储屋宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367514_comment'></div>俘掠百姓男女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367514_comment'></div>驱杀牛马老少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367514_comment'></div>一州几尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367514_comment'></div>贼散后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367514_comment'></div>百姓归复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367514_comment'></div>十不存一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367514_comment'></div>资产皆无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367514_comment'></div>人心嗷嗷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367514_comment'></div>未有安者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367514_comment'></div>若依诸使期限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367514_comment'></div>臣恐坐见乱亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367514_comment'></div>今来未敢徵率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367514_comment'></div>伏待进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367514_comment'></div>又岭南诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367514_comment'></div>寇盗未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367514_comment'></div>臣州是岭北界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367514_comment'></div>守捉处多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367514_comment'></div>若臣州不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367514_comment'></div>则湖南皆乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367514_comment'></div>伏望天恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367514_comment'></div>自州未破以前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367514_comment'></div>百姓久负租税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367514_comment'></div>及租庸等使所有徵率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367514_comment'></div>和市杂物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367514_comment'></div>一切放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367514_comment'></div>自州破以后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367514_comment'></div>除正租正庸及准格式合进奉徵纳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367514_comment'></div>请据见在户徵送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367514_comment'></div>其馀科率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367514_comment'></div>并请放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367514_comment'></div>容其见在百姓产业稍成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367514_comment'></div>逃亡归复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367514_comment'></div>似可存活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367514_comment'></div>即请依常例<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1367514", 1367514, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>处分</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367514_comment'></div>伏愿陛下以臣所奏下议有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367514_comment'></div>苟若臣所见愚僻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367514_comment'></div>不合时政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367514_comment'></div>干乱纪度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367514_comment'></div>事涉虚妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367514_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1367514", 1367514, ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年</a>　在道州刺史任上，有文。作品：《贺赦表》《县令箴》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：疑《县令箴》为广德二年及永泰元年间道州刺史任内作。）</span><div id='poem_1367552' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367552' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367552?labeling=true' target='_blank'>县令箴</a><span class='authorDate'>（764年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1367552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367552'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367552'>古今所贵，有土之官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367552'>当其选授，何尝不难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367552'>为其动静，是人祸福。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367552'>为其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1367552", 1367552, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>嘘噏</span>，作人寒燠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367552'>烦则人怨，猛则人惧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367552'>勿以赏罚，因其喜怒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367552'>太宽则慢，岂能行令。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367552'>太简则疏，难与为政。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367552'>既明且断，直焉无情。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367552'>清而且惠，果然必行。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367552'>或曰关由上官，事不自我。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367552_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367552'>辞让而去，有何不可。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　结游九嶷山，宿无为观，有诗。作品：《宿无为观》<div id='poem_6111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　以虞舜葬苍梧，在其封内，因立舜祠于州西之山南，结为之刻石立表。作品：《舜祠表》<div id='poem_1367619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舜祠表</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_1367619_comment'></div>以虞舜葬于苍梧九疑之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367619_comment'></div>在我封内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367619_comment'></div>是故申明前诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367619_comment'></div>立祠于州西之山南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367619_comment'></div>已而刻石为表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367619_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367619_comment'></div>孔氏作虞书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367619_comment'></div>明大舜德及生人之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367619_comment'></div>则大舜于生人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367619_comment'></div>宜以类乎天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367619_comment'></div>生人奉大舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367619_comment'></div>宜万世而不厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367619_comment'></div>考大舜南巡之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367619_comment'></div>时已一百一十二岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367619_comment'></div>自中国至苍梧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367619_comment'></div>亦几有万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367619_comment'></div>苍梧山谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367619_comment'></div>深险可惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367619_comment'></div>帝竟入而不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367619_comment'></div>至今山下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367619_comment'></div>不知帝居之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367619_comment'></div>帝葬之陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367619_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367619_comment'></div>在有虞氏之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367619_comment'></div>人民可夺其君耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367619_comment'></div>人民于大舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367619_comment'></div>能忘而不思耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367619_comment'></div>何为来而不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367619_comment'></div>何故死于其山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367619_comment'></div>吾实惑而作表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367619_comment'></div>来者游于此邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367619_comment'></div>登乎九疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367619_comment'></div>谁能不惑也欤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1367619_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　王及将之容州耿慎惑幕，结作序送之。作品：《送王及之容州序》<div id='poem_1367533' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367533' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367533?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王及之容州序</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367533")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367533_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367533'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367533'>乾元初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367533_comment'></div>漫叟浪家于瀼溪之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367533_comment'></div>以耕钓自全而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367533_comment'></div>九江之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367533_comment'></div>未相喜爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367533_comment'></div>其意似惧叟衣食之不足耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367533_comment'></div>叟亦不促促而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367533_comment'></div>有王及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367533_comment'></div>异夫乡人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367533_comment'></div>以文学相求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367533_comment'></div>不以羁旅见惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367533_comment'></div>以相安为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367533_comment'></div>不以可否自择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367533_comment'></div>及于叟也如是之多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367533_comment'></div>叟在舂陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367533_comment'></div>及能相从游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367533_comment'></div>岁馀而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367533_comment'></div>将行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367533_comment'></div>规之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367533_comment'></div>叟爱及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367533_comment'></div>无惑叟言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367533_comment'></div>及方壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367533_comment'></div>可强艺业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367533_comment'></div>勿以游方为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367533_comment'></div>人生若不能师表朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367533_comment'></div>即当老死山谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367533_comment'></div>彼区区于财货之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367533_comment'></div>局局于权势之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367533_comment'></div>纵得钟鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367533_comment'></div>亦胡颜受纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367533_comment'></div>行矣自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367533_comment'></div>耿容州欢于叟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367533_comment'></div>及到容州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367533_comment'></div>为叟谢主人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367533_comment'></div>闻幕府野次久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367533_comment'></div>正宜收择谋夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367533_comment'></div>引信才士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367533_comment'></div>有如及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367533_comment'></div>能收引乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367533_comment'></div>二三子赋送远之什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367533_comment'></div>以系此云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1367533_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='495a04f590c04793aafa7efe01f7483f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("495a04f590c04793aafa7efe01f7483f");'><span id='495a04f590c04793aafa7efe01f7483f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=767')">766-767年</a>，48-49岁</div><div id='495a04f590c04793aafa7efe01f7483f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　春结复临道州，有谢表。作品：《再谢上表》<div id='poem_1367510' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367510' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367510?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367510")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367510_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367510'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367510'>臣某言。某伏奉某月日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367510_comment'></div>再授臣道州刺史。以某月日到州上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367510_comment'></div>臣前日在官。虽百姓不至流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367510_comment'></div>而归复者十无一二。虽寇盗不犯边鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367510_comment'></div>而不能兵救邻州。虽赋敛仅能供给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367510_comment'></div>而有司不无罪状。虽人吏似从教令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367510_comment'></div>而风俗未能移易。臣又多病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367510_comment'></div>不无假故。水旱灾沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367510_comment'></div>每岁不免。疾疫死伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367510_comment'></div>臣州尤甚。以臣自讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367510_comment'></div>合抵刑宪。圣朝宽贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367510_comment'></div>犹宜夺官。陛下过听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367510_comment'></div>重有授任。伏恐守廉让者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367510_comment'></div>以臣为苟安禄位。抱公直者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367510_comment'></div>以臣为内怀私僻。有材识者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367510_comment'></div>辱臣于台隶之下。用刑法者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367510_comment'></div>罪臣于程式之中。臣所以不敢即日辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367510_comment'></div>待陛下按验虚实。然后归罪有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367510_comment'></div>今四方兵革未宁。赋敛未息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367510_comment'></div>百姓流亡转甚。官吏侵剋日多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367510_comment'></div>实不合使凶庸<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1367510", 1367510, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>贪猥</span>之徒。凡弱下愚之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367510_comment'></div>以货贿权势。而为州县长官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367510_comment'></div>伏望陛下特加察问。举其功过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367510_comment'></div>必行赏罚。以安苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367510_comment'></div>谁不自私。臣实不敢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367510_comment'></div>所言狂直。朝夕待罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367510_comment'></div>不任恳之至。谨遣某官奉表陈谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367510_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1367510_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年3月15日</a>　既遵旧制于州西立舜庙讫，进《舜庙状》，乞免近庙一二家，令岁时拂洒，五月，诏蠲近庙两户充扫除。作品：《论舜庙状》<div id='poem_1367516' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367516' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367516?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论舜庙状</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年3月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367516")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367516_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367516'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367516'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367516_comment'></div>谨按地图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367516_comment'></div>舜陵在九疑之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367516_comment'></div>舜庙在太阳之溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367516_comment'></div>舜陵古老已失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367516_comment'></div>太阳溪今不知处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367516_comment'></div>秦汉已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367516_comment'></div>置庙山下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367516_comment'></div>年代寖远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367516_comment'></div>祠宇不存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367516_comment'></div>每有诏书令州县致祭奠酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367516_comment'></div>荒野恭命而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367516_comment'></div>岂有盛德大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367516_comment'></div>百王师表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367516_comment'></div>殁于荒裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367516_comment'></div>陵庙皆无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367516_comment'></div>臣谨遵旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367516_comment'></div>于州西山上已立庙讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367516_comment'></div>特乞天恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367516_comment'></div>许蠲免近庙一两家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367516_comment'></div>令岁时拂洒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367516_comment'></div>示为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1367516", 1367516, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>恒式</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367516_comment'></div>岂独表圣人至德及于万代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367516_comment'></div>实欲彰陛下元泽及于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367516_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1367516_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　近三年因西原民侵陷，道州民疲苦不堪，结进《奏免科率状》，敕依。<div id='poem_1367514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏免科率状</a><span class='authorDate'>（764年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367514")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367514'>当州准敕及租庸等使徵率钱物都计一十三万六千三百八十八贯八百文一十三万二千四百八十贯九百文岭南西原贼未破州已前三千九百七贯九百文贼退后徵率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367514_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367514'>以前件如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367514_comment'></div>臣自到州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367514_comment'></div>见租庸等诸使文牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367514_comment'></div>令徵前件钱物送纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367514_comment'></div>臣当州被西原贼屠陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367514_comment'></div>贼停留一月馀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367514_comment'></div>焚烧粮储屋宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367514_comment'></div>俘掠百姓男女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367514_comment'></div>驱杀牛马老少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367514_comment'></div>一州几尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367514_comment'></div>贼散后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367514_comment'></div>百姓归复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367514_comment'></div>十不存一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367514_comment'></div>资产皆无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367514_comment'></div>人心嗷嗷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367514_comment'></div>未有安者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367514_comment'></div>若依诸使期限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367514_comment'></div>臣恐坐见乱亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367514_comment'></div>今来未敢徵率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367514_comment'></div>伏待进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367514_comment'></div>又岭南诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367514_comment'></div>寇盗未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367514_comment'></div>臣州是岭北界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367514_comment'></div>守捉处多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367514_comment'></div>若臣州不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367514_comment'></div>则湖南皆乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367514_comment'></div>伏望天恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367514_comment'></div>自州未破以前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367514_comment'></div>百姓久负租税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367514_comment'></div>及租庸等使所有徵率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367514_comment'></div>和市杂物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367514_comment'></div>一切放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367514_comment'></div>自州破以后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367514_comment'></div>除正租正庸及准格式合进奉徵纳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367514_comment'></div>请据见在户徵送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367514_comment'></div>其馀科率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367514_comment'></div>并请放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367514_comment'></div>容其见在百姓产业稍成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367514_comment'></div>逃亡归复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367514_comment'></div>似可存活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367514_comment'></div>即请依常例<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1367514", 1367514, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>处分</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367514_comment'></div>伏愿陛下以臣所奏下议有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367514_comment'></div>苟若臣所见愚僻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367514_comment'></div>不合时政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367514_comment'></div>干乱纪度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367514_comment'></div>事涉虚妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367514_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_47_1367514", 1367514, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>忝官</span>尸禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367514_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1367514", 1367514, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>欺上罔下</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367514_comment'></div>是臣之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367514_comment'></div>合正典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367514_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1367514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　结爱处士张季秀介直高尚，有文。作品：《举处士张季秀状》<div id='poem_1367517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举处士张季秀状</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367517")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367517'>臣州僻在岭隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367517_comment'></div>其实边裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367517_comment'></div>土风贪于货贿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367517_comment'></div>旧俗多习吏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367517_comment'></div>独季秀能介直自全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367517_comment'></div>退守廉让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367517_comment'></div>文学为业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367517_comment'></div>不求人知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367517_comment'></div>寒馁切身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367517_comment'></div>弥更守分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367517_comment'></div>贵其所尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367517_comment'></div>愿老山林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367517_comment'></div>臣切以兵兴已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367517_comment'></div>人皆趋竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367517_comment'></div>苟利分寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367517_comment'></div>不愧其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367517_comment'></div>则如季秀者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367517_comment'></div>不可不加褎异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367517_comment'></div>臣特望天恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367517_comment'></div>令州县取其稳便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367517_comment'></div>与造草舍十数间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367517_comment'></div>给水田一两顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367517_comment'></div>免其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1367517", 1367517, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>当户</span>徭役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367517_comment'></div>令得保遂其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367517_comment'></div>此实圣朝旌退让之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367517_comment'></div>亦为士庶识廉耻之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367517_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1367517_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　处士张季秀卒，有文。作品：《张处士表》<div id='poem_1367621' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367621' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367621?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张处士表</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367621")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367621_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367621'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367621'>永泰丙午中。处士张秀卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367621_comment'></div>于戏。吾尝验古人将老死岩谷远迹时世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367621_comment'></div>不必其心皆好山林。若非介直方正与时世不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367621_comment'></div>必识高行独与时世不合。不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367621_comment'></div>则刚褊傲逸与时世不合。彼若遭逢不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367621_comment'></div>则身不足以为祸。将家族以随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367621_comment'></div>至于伤污毁辱。何足说者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367621_comment'></div>故使之矫然绝世。逃其不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367621_comment'></div>直为逸民。竟为退士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367621_comment'></div>枕石饮水。终身而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367621_comment'></div>当时之君。欲以禄位招之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367621_comment'></div>有土之官。欲以厚礼处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367621_comment'></div>彼惊惧抗绝而去。时之见能如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367621_comment'></div>所以尤高尚焉。呜呼处士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367621_comment'></div>与时不合者耶。而未能矫然绝世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367621_comment'></div>遭以礼法相检不见容。悲夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367621_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1367621_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　在道州刺史任上，有文。作品：《菊圃记》<div id='poem_1367541' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367541' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367541?labeling=true' target='_blank'>菊圃记</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367541")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367541_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367541'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367541'>舂陵俗不种菊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367541_comment'></div>前时自远致之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367541_comment'></div>植于前庭墙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367541_comment'></div>及再来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367541_comment'></div>菊已无矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367541_comment'></div>徘徊旧圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367541_comment'></div>嗟叹久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367541_comment'></div>谁不知菊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367541_comment'></div>方华可赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367541_comment'></div>在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1367541", 1367541, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>药品</span>是良药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367541_comment'></div>为蔬菜是佳蔬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367541_comment'></div>纵须地趋走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367541_comment'></div>犹宜徙植修养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367541_comment'></div>而忍蹂践至尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367541_comment'></div>不爱惜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367541_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367541_comment'></div>贤人君子自植其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367541_comment'></div>不可不慎择所处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367541_comment'></div>一旦遭人不爱重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367541_comment'></div>如此菊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367541_comment'></div>悲伤奈何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367541_comment'></div>于是更为之圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367541_comment'></div>重畦植之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367541_comment'></div>其地近<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1367541", 1367541, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>宴息</span>之堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367541_comment'></div>吏人不此奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367541_comment'></div>近登望之亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367541_comment'></div>旌旄不此行列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367541_comment'></div>纵参歌妓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367541_comment'></div>菊非可恶之草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367541_comment'></div>使有酒徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367541_comment'></div>菊为助兴之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367541_comment'></div>为之作记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367541_comment'></div>以托后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367541_comment'></div>并录药经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367541_comment'></div>列于记后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1367541_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　夏巡属县至州南江华，游县大夫瞿令问所筑县南山石之亭，命之寒亭，作《寒亭记》，刻于亭背。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：《菊圃记》约作于此期。）</span><div id='poem_1367543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367543?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寒亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367543")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367543_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367543'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367543'>永泰丙午中。巡属县至江华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367543_comment'></div>县大夫瞿令问咨曰。县南水石相映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367543_comment'></div>望之可爱。相传不可登临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367543_comment'></div>俾求之。得洞穴而入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367543_comment'></div>栈险以通之。始得搆茅亭于石上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367543_comment'></div>及亭成也。以阶槛凭空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367543_comment'></div>下临长江。轩楹云端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367543_comment'></div>上齐绝巅。若旦暮景风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367543_comment'></div>烟霭异色。苍苍石⿰<span class='inlineComment2'>（石庸）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367543_comment'></div>含映水木。欲名斯亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367543_comment'></div>状类不得。敢请名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367543_comment'></div>表示来世。于是休于亭上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367543_comment'></div>为商之曰。今大暑登之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367543_comment'></div>疑天时将寒。炎蒸之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367543_comment'></div>清凉可安。合命之曰寒亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367543_comment'></div>乃为寒亭作记。刻之亭背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367543_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1367543_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　结与瞿令问游县东南六七里之阳华岩，作《阳华岩铭》，瞿刻之岩下。<div id='poem_1367557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>阳华岩铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367557")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367557_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367557'>道州江华县东南六七里。有回山。南面峻秀。下有大岩。岩当阳端。故以阳华命之。吾游处山林。几三十年。所见泉石。如阳华殊异而可家者未也。故作铭称之。县大夫瞿令问。艺兼篆籀。俾依石经。刻之岩下。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367557'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367557'>九疑万峰，不如阳华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367557'>阳华<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1367557", 1367557, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>崭巉</span>，其下可家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367557'>洞开为岩，岩当阳端。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367557'>岩高气清，洞深泉寒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367557'>阳华旋回，岑巅如辟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367557'>沟塍松竹，辉映水石。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367557'>尤宜逸民，亦宜退士。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367557'>吾欲投节，穷老于此。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367557'>惧人讥我，以官矫时。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　巡属江华，有诗。作品：《招陶别驾家阳华》<div id='poem_6103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6112?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿洄溪翁宅</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript:
