id='poem_content_6112'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6112'>长松万株绕茅舍，怪石寒泉近岩下。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6112'>老翁八十犹能行，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_6112", 6112, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>将领</span>儿孙行拾稼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6112'>吾羡老翁居处幽，吾爱老翁无所求。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6112'>时俗是非何足道，得似老翁吾即休。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6112'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_6112_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6104?labeling=true' target='_blank'>说洄溪招退者<span class='inlineComment2'>（在州南江华县）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6104")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6104_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_6104'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3340, "poem_allusion_6104")'>葛仙翁</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_6104_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6104'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6104'>长松亭亭满四山，山间<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6104", 6104, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>乳窦</span>流清泉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6104'>洄溪正在此山里，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_6104", 6104, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>乳水</span>松膏常灌田。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6104'>松膏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_6104", 6104, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>乳水</span>田肥良，稻苗如蒲米粒长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6104'>糜色如珈玉液酒，酒熟犹闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_6104", 6104, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>松节</span>香。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6104'>溪边老翁年几许，长男头白孙嫁女。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6104'>问言只食松田米，无药无方向人语。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6104'>浯溪石下多泉源，盛暑大寒冬大温。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6104'>屠苏宜在水中石，洄溪一曲自当门。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6104'>吾今欲作洄溪翁，谁能住我舍西东。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6104'>勿惮山深与地僻，罗浮尚有<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3340, "poem_sentence_9_6104")'>葛仙翁</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6104'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_6104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6104'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6104)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　在道州刺史任上，有文。作品：《问进士五篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：原注云：“永泰二年道州问。”）</span>《九嶷图记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：九嶷图记末云：“时永泰丙午中也”）</span>《窊樽铭》<div id='poem_1367497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>问进士<span class='inlineComment2'>（永泰二年通州问）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367497")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367497'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367497'>问。天下兴兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367497_comment'></div>今十二年矣。杀伤劳辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367497_comment'></div>人似未厌。控强兵据要害者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367497_comment'></div>外以奉王命为辞。内实理车甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367497_comment'></div>招宾客。树<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1367497", 1367497, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>爪牙</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367497_comment'></div>国家亦因其所利。大者王而相之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367497_comment'></div>亚者公侯。尚不满望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367497_comment'></div>今欲散其士卒。使归乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367497_comment'></div>收其器械。纳之王府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367497_comment'></div>随其才分。与之禄位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367497_comment'></div>欲临之以威武。则力未能制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367497_comment'></div>欲责之以辞让。则其心未喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367497_comment'></div>若舍而不问。则未睹太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367497_comment'></div>秀才通明古今。才识<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1367497", 1367497, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>杰异</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367497_comment'></div>天下之兵须解。苍生须致仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367497_comment'></div>其策安出。子其昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367497_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1367497_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367498?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367498'>问。往年天下太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367498_comment'></div>仕者非累资序。积劳考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367498_comment'></div>二十许年。不离一尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367498_comment'></div>至于入廊庙。总枢辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367498_comment'></div>则当时名声籍甚者得至焉。今商贾贱类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367498_comment'></div>台隶下品。数月之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367498_comment'></div>大者上污卿监。小者下辱州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367498_comment'></div>至于廊庙。不无杂人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367498_comment'></div>如专经以求进。主文而望达者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367498_comment'></div>若不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1367498", 1367498, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>困顿</span>于林野。则必悽惶于道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367498_comment'></div>今日国家行何道得九流鉴清。作何法得侥倖路绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367498_comment'></div>施何令使人自知耻。设何教使贤愚自分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367498_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1367498_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367499?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367499'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367499'>问。开元天宝之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367499_comment'></div>耕者益力。四海之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367499_comment'></div>高山绝壑。耒耜亦满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367499_comment'></div>人家粮储。皆及数岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367499_comment'></div>太仓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1367499", 1367499, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>委积</span>。陈腐不可校量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367499_comment'></div>忽遇凶年。谷犹耗尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367499_comment'></div>当今三河膏壤。淮泗沃野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367499_comment'></div>皆荆棘已老。则耕可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367499_comment'></div>太仓空虚。雀鼠犹饿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367499_comment'></div>至于百姓。朝暮不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367499_comment'></div>而诸道聚兵。百有馀万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367499_comment'></div>遭岁不稔。将何为谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367499_comment'></div>今欲劝人耕种。则丧亡之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367499_comment'></div>人自贫苦。寒馁不救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367499_comment'></div>岂有生资。今欲罢兵息戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367499_comment'></div>则又寇盗犹在。尚须<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1367499", 1367499, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>防遏</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367499_comment'></div>使国家用何策得人安俗阜。不战无兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367499_comment'></div>用何谋使纵遇凶年。亦无灾患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367499_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1367499_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367500?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367500'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367500'>问。往年粟一斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367500_comment'></div>估钱四百犹贵。近年粟一斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367500_comment'></div>估钱五百尚贱。往年帛一匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367500_comment'></div>估钱五百犹贵。近年帛一匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367500_comment'></div>估钱二千尚贱。今耕夫未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367500_comment'></div>织妇犹在。何故往年耕织。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367500_comment'></div>计时量力。劳苦忘倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367500_comment'></div>求免寒馁。何故今日甘心寒馁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367500_comment'></div>惰游而已。于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367500_comment'></div>曩时粟帛至贱。衣食至易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367500_comment'></div>今日粟帛至贵。衣食至难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367500_comment'></div>而人心勤惰如此。其何故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367500_comment'></div>试一商之。欲闻其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367500_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1367500_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367501?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367501'>问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367501_comment'></div>古人识贵精通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367501_comment'></div>学重兼博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367501_comment'></div>不有激发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367501_comment'></div>何以相求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367501_comment'></div>三礼何篇可删。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367501_comment'></div>三传何者可废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367501_comment'></div>墨氏非乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367501_comment'></div>其礼何以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367501_comment'></div>儒家委命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367501_comment'></div>此言当乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367501_comment'></div>彼天女天孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367501_comment'></div>不知何物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367501_comment'></div>彼日兄月姊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367501_comment'></div>弟妹是谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367501_comment'></div>驵侩与伧奴宁分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367501_comment'></div>一纯将二精何说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367501_comment'></div>孤竹之君何姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367501_comment'></div>新城老妇何名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367501_comment'></div>棘竹出自何方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367501_comment'></div>毒铜产于何国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367501_comment'></div>何乡无水可饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367501_comment'></div>何地卧冰而温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367501_comment'></div>何人恩信过于田横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367501_comment'></div>何人壮勇等于关羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367501_comment'></div>何人凿坯而遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367501_comment'></div>何人终日扫门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367501_comment'></div>无浅近之不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367501_comment'></div>悉说。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1367501_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九疑山图记</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367545")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367545_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367545'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367545'>九疑山方二千馀里。四州各近一隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367545_comment'></div>世称九峰相似。望而疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367545_comment'></div>谓之九疑。亦云舜望九峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367545_comment'></div>疑禹而悲。从臣有作九疑之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367545_comment'></div>因谓之疑。九峰殊极高大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367545_comment'></div>远望皆可见也。彼如嵩华之峻峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367545_comment'></div>衡岱之方广。在九峰之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367545_comment'></div>磊磊然如布棋石者。可以百数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367545_comment'></div>中峰之下。水无鱼鳖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367545_comment'></div>林无鸟兽。时闻声如蝉蝇之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367545_comment'></div>听之亦无。往往见大谷长川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367545_comment'></div>平由深渊。杉松百围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367545_comment'></div>桧栝并茂。青莎白沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367545_comment'></div>洞穴丹崖。寒泉飞流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367545_comment'></div>异竹杂华。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1367545", 1367545, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>回映</span>之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367545_comment'></div>似藏人家。实有九水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367545_comment'></div>出于山中。四水南流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367545_comment'></div>灌于南海。五水北注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367545_comment'></div>合为洞庭。若度其高卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367545_comment'></div>比洞庭南海之岸。直上可二三百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367545_comment'></div>不知海内之山。如九疑者几焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367545_comment'></div>或曰。若然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367545_comment'></div>兹山何不列于五岳。对曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367545_comment'></div>五帝之前。封疆尚隘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367545_comment'></div>衡山作岳。已出荒服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367545_comment'></div>今九疑之南。万里臣妾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367545_comment'></div>国门东望。不见涯际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367545_comment'></div>西行几万里。未尽边陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367545_comment'></div>当合以九疑为南岳。以昆崙为西岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367545_comment'></div>衡华之辈。听逸者占为山居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367545_comment'></div>封君表作苑囿耳。但苦当世议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367545_comment'></div>拘限常情。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1367545", 1367545, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>牵引</span>古制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367545_comment'></div>不能有所改创也。如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367545_comment'></div>故图画九峰。略载山谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367545_comment'></div>传于好事。以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1367545", 1367545, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>旌异</span>之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367545_comment'></div>如山中之往迹。峰洞之名称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367545_comment'></div>为人所传说者。并随方题记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367545_comment'></div>庶几观者易知。时永泰丙午年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367545_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1367545_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367575' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367575' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367575?labeling=true' target='_blank'>窊樽铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367575")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367575_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367575'>道州城东有左湖。湖东二十步有小石山。山颠有窊石。可以为樽。乃为亭樽上。刻石为志。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367575_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367575'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367575'>井石何状，如兽之踆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367575'>其背䫜窊，可以为樽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367575'>空而临之，长岑深壑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367575'>广亭之内，如见山岳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367575'>满而临之，曲浦回渊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367575'>长瓢之下，江湖在焉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367575'>彼成全器，谁为之力。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367575'>天地开凿，日月<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1367575", 1367575, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>抆拭</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367575'>寒暑琢磨，风雨润色。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367575'>此器大朴，尤宜直纯。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367575'>勒铭亭下，以告后人。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367575_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367575'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1367575_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　在道州刺史任上，有诗。作品：《窊樽诗》（巉巉小山石）<div id='poem_6108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>窊尊诗<span class='inlineComment2'>（在道州）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6108")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6108_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_6108'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(125, "poem_allusion_6108")'>蓬瀛</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5025, "poem_allusion_6108")'>陶渊明</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_6108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6108'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6108'>巉巉小山石，数峰对<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作戴）</span>窊亭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6108'>窊石堪为樽，状类不可名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6108'>巡回数尺间，如见小<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(125, "poem_sentence_2_6108")'>蓬瀛</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6108'>尊中酒初涨，始有岛屿生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6108'>岂无日观峰，直下临沧溟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6108'>爱之不觉醉，醉卧还自醒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6108'>醒醉在尊畔，始为吾性情。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6108'>若以形胜论，坐隅临郡城。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6108'>平湖近阶砌，近山复青青。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6108'>异木几十株，林条冒檐楹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6108'>盘根满石上，皆作龙蛇形。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6108'>酒堂贮酿器，户牖皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_6108", 6108, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>罂瓶</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6108'>此尊可常满，谁是<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5025, "poem_sentence_12_6108")'>陶渊明</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_6108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_6108'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_6108_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　在道州刺史任上，有文送谭山人归云阳。作品：《送谭山人归云阳序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：当是由江华返道州后所作。）</span><div id='poem_1367534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367534?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送谭山人归云阳序</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367534")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367534_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367534'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367534'>吾于九疑之下。赏爱泉石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367534_comment'></div>今几三年。能扁舟数千里来游者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367534_comment'></div>独云阳谭子。谭子文学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367534_comment'></div>隐名山野。隐身云阳之阿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367534_comment'></div>世如君何。牧犊爱云阳之宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367534_comment'></div>峻公不出南岳三十年。今得云阳一峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367534_comment'></div>谭子又在焉。彼真可家之者邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367534_comment'></div>子去为吾谋于牧犊。近峻公有泉石老树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367534_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1367534", 1367534, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>寿藤</span>萦垂。水可灌田一区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367534_comment'></div>火可烧种菽粟。近泉可为十数间茅舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367534_comment'></div>所诣才通小船。吾则往而家矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367534_comment'></div>此邦舜祠之奇怪。阳华之殊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367534_comment'></div>潓泉之胜绝。见峻公与牧犊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367534_comment'></div>当一一说之。松竹满庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367534_comment'></div>水石满堂。石鱼负樽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367534_comment'></div>凫舫运觞。醉送谭子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367534_comment'></div>归于云阳。漫叟元次山序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367534_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1367534_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　冬结自道州诣长沙，计兵事，至零陵，游郭中，得岩与洞，命曰朝阳岩，作《朝阳岩铭》<div id='poem_1367576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367576?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝阳岩铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367576")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367576_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367576'>永泰丙午中。自舂陵诣都使计兵。至零陵。爱其郭中有水石之异。泊舟寻之。得岩与洞。此邦之形胜也。自古荒之。而无名称。以其东向。遂以朝阳命之焉。前刺史独孤愐为吾剪辟榛莽。后摄刺史窦泌为吾创制茅阁。于是朝阳水石。始有胜绝之名。已而刻铭岩下。将示来世。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367576_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367576'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367576'>于戏朝阳，怪异难状。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367576'>苍苍半山，如在水上。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367576'>朝阳水石，可谓幽奇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367576'>岩下洞口，洞中泉垂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367576'>彼高岩绝崖，深洞寒泉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367576'>纵僻在幽远，尤宜往焉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367576'>况郡城井邑，岩洞相对。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367576'>无人修赏，竞使芜秽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367576'>刻石岩下，问我何为。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367576'>欲零陵水石，世人有知。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367576_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367576'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1367576_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　结自道州诣长沙，计兵事，至零陵，游郭中，得岩与洞，命曰朝阳岩，作《朝阳岩下歌》<div id='poem_6119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6119?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝阳岩下歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6119")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6119_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6119'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6119'>朝阳岩下湘水深，朝阳洞口寒泉清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6119'>零陵城郭夹湘岸，岩洞幽奇带郡城。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6119'>荒芜自古人不见，零陵徒有先贤传。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6119'>水石为娱安可羡，长歌一曲留相劝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6119'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_6119_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年2月</a>　以军事诣长沙，二月还州，泛湘江，过零陵，逢春水，舟行不进，有诗。作品：《杂曲歌辞 欸乃曲五首》<div id='poem_6043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杂曲歌辞<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>欸乃曲<span class='inlineComment2'>（欸乃，棹船声也。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（767年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6043")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6043_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6043'>大历丁未中，漫叟结为道州刺史，以军事诣都使。还州，逢春水，舟行不进，作〈欸乃〉五首（作〈欸乃〉五章），令舟子唱之，盖以取适于道路云（盖以取适于道路耳）。</div><div id='poem_preface_6043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6043'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6043'>偏<span class='inlineComment2'>（集作偶）</span>存名迹在人间，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6043", 6043, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>顺俗</span>与时未安闲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6043'>来谒大官兼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_6043", 6043, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>问政</span>，扁舟却入九疑山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_6046' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6046?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>欸乃曲<span class='inlineComment2'>（欸乃，棹船声也。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（767年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6046_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6046'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6046'>零陵郡北湘水东，浯溪形胜满湘中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6046_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6046'>溪口石颠堪自逸，谁能相伴作渔翁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6046_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6046'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_6046_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6047' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6047' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6047?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>欸乃曲<span class='inlineComment2'>（欸乃，棹船声也。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（767年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6047_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6047'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6047'>下泷船似入深渊，上泷船似欲升天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6047_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6047'>泷南始到九疑郡，应绝高人乘兴船。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6047_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6047'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_6047_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6047'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6047)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年2月</a>　宿丹崖翁唐节宅，有诗。作品：《宿丹崖翁宅》<div id='poem_6110' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6110' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6110?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿丹崖翁宅</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6110")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6110_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6110'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6110'>扁舟欲到泷口湍，春水湍泷上水难。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6110'>投竿来泊丹崖下，得与崖翁尽一欢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6110'>丹崖之亭当石颠，破竹半山引寒泉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6110'>泉流掩映在木杪，有若白鸟飞林间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6110'>往往随风作雾雨，湿人巾履满庭前。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6110'>丹崖翁，爱丹崖，弃官几年崖下家。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6110'>儿孙棹船抱酒瓮，醉里长歌挥钓车。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6110'>吾将求退与翁游，学翁歌醉在鱼舟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6110'>官吏随人往未得，却望丹崖惭复羞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_6110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6110'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6110)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a>　宿丹崖翁唐节宅，有文。作品：《丹崖翁宅铭》<div id='poem_1367556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367556?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丹崖翁宅铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367556")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367556_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367556'>零陵泷下三十里。得丹崖翁宅。有唐节督者。曾为泷水令。去官家于崖下。自称丹崖翁。丹崖湘中水石之异者。翁湘中得道之逸者。爱其水石。为之作铭。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367556_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367556'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367556'>泷水未尽，泷山犹峻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367556'>忽见渊洄，丹崖千仞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367556'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1367556", 1367556, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>磳磳</span>丹崖，其下谁家。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367556'>门前断船，篱上钓车。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367556'>不知几峰，为其四墉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367556'>竹幽石磴，飞泉户中。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367556'>怪石临渊，䂩䂩石巅。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367556'>何得石巅，翁独醉眠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367556'>吾欲与翁，东西茅宇。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367556'>饮啄终老，翁亦悦许。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367556'>世俗常事，阻人心情。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367556'>徘徊崖下，遂刻此铭。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1367556_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1367556'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1367556_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a>　在道州刺史任上，有文。作品：《右溪记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：永泰、大历间结在道州任内作。）</span>《刺史厅壁记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：永泰、大历间结在道州任内作。）</span>《七泉铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：永泰、大历间结在道州任内作。）</span>《五如石铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：永泰、大历间结在道州任内作。）</span>《别崔曼序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：永泰、大历间结在道州任内作。）</span><div id='poem_1367540' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367540' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367540?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右溪记</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367540")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367540_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367540'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367540'>道州城西百馀步有小溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367540_comment'></div>南流数十步合营溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367540_comment'></div>水抵两岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367540_comment'></div>悉皆怪石欹嵌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367540_comment'></div>盘缺不可名状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367540_comment'></div>清流触石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367540_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1367540", 1367540, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>洄悬</span>激注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367540_comment'></div>佳木异竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367540_comment'></div>垂阴相荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367540_comment'></div>此溪若在山野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367540_comment'></div>则宜逸民退士之所游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367540_comment'></div>处在人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367540_comment'></div>则可为都邑之胜境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367540_comment'></div>静者之林亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367540_comment'></div>而置州已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367540_comment'></div>无人赏爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367540_comment'></div>徘徊溪上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367540_comment'></div>为之怅然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367540_comment'></div>乃疏凿芜秽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367540_comment'></div>俾为亭宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367540_comment'></div>植松与桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367540_comment'></div>兼之香草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367540_comment'></div>以裨形胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367540_comment'></div>为溪在州右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367540_comment'></div>遂命之曰右溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367540_comment'></div>刻铭石上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367540_comment'></div>彰示来者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1367540_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367538' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367538' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367538?labeling=true' target='_blank'>道州刺史厅壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367538")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367538'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367538'>天下太平。方千里之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367538_comment'></div>生植齿类。刺史能存亡休戚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367538_comment'></div>天下兵兴。方千里之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367538_comment'></div>能保黎庶。能攘患难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367538_comment'></div>在刺史耳。凡刺史若无文武才略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367538_comment'></div>若不清廉肃下。若不明惠公直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367538_comment'></div>则一州生类。皆受其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367538_comment'></div>于戏。自至此州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367538_comment'></div>见井邑邱墟。生人几尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367538_comment'></div>试问其故。不觉涕下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367538_comment'></div>前辈刺史。或有贪猥惛弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367538_comment'></div>不分是非。但以衣服饮食为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367538_comment'></div>数年之间。苍生蒙以私欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367538_comment'></div>侵夺兼之。公家驱迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367538_comment'></div>非奸恶强富。殆无存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367538_comment'></div>问之耆老。前后刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367538_comment'></div>能恤养贫弱。专守法令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367538_comment'></div>有徐公履道李公廙而已。遍问诸公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367538_comment'></div>善或不及徐李二公。恶有不堪说者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367538_comment'></div>故为此记。与刺史作戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367538_comment'></div>自置州以来。诸公改授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367538_comment'></div>迁黜年月。则旧记存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367538_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1367538_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367555' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367555?labeling=true' target='_blank'>五如石铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367555")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367555_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367555'>涍泉之阳。得怪石焉。左右前后。及登石颠。均有如似。故命之曰五如石。石皆有窦。窦中涌泉。泉诡异于七泉。故命为七胜泉。石有双目。一目命为洞井。井与泉通。一目命为洞樽。樽可䝻酒。石尾有穴。有如砻者。又如泷者。泉可渟澄。匝石而流。入砻中。出而为泷。于戏。彼能异于此。安可不称显之。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367555'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367555'>五如之石，何以为名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367555'>请悉状之，谁为我听。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367555'>左如旋龙，低首回顾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367555'>右如惊鸿，张翅不去。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367555'>前如饮虎，饮而蹲焉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367555'>后如怒龟，出洞登山。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367555'>若坐于颠，石则如船。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367555'>乘彼灵槎，在汉之间。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367555'>洞井如凿，渊然泉涌。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367555'>澄澜涵石，波起如动。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1367555'>不旌尤异，焉用为文。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1367555'>刻铭石上，于千万春。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1367555_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1367555'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1367555_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367537' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367537' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367537?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别崔曼序</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367537")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367537_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367537'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367537'>漫叟年将五十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367537_comment'></div>与时不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367537_comment'></div>垂三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367537_comment'></div>爱恶之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367537_comment'></div>纷纷人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367537_comment'></div>博陵崔曼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367537_comment'></div>惑叟所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367537_comment'></div>游而辨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367537_comment'></div>数月未去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367537_comment'></div>会潭州都督张正言荐曼为蜀邑长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367537_comment'></div>将行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367537_comment'></div>叟谓曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367537_comment'></div>叟异时乃山林一病民耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367537_comment'></div>宜不相罔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367537_comment'></div>行矣勿惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367537_comment'></div>吾子有才业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367537_comment'></div>且明辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367537_comment'></div>又方年少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367537_comment'></div>必能树勋庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367537_comment'></div>垂名声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367537_comment'></div>若求先达贤异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367537_comment'></div>能相抆拭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367537_comment'></div>正在张公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367537_comment'></div>张公往年在西域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367537_comment'></div>主人能用其一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367537_comment'></div>遂开境千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367537_comment'></div>威振绝域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367537_comment'></div>宠荣当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367537_comment'></div>公往在淮南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367537_comment'></div>逡巡指麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367537_comment'></div>万夫风从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367537_comment'></div>遭逢猜疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367537_comment'></div>弛而不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367537_comment'></div>今海内兵革未息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367537_comment'></div>张公必为时用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367537_comment'></div>吾子勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367537_comment'></div>所相规者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367537_comment'></div>宜缓步富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367537_comment'></div>从容谋画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367537_comment'></div>少节酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367537_comment'></div>平气槩耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1367537_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_6120'>小溪在城下，形胜堪赏爱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6120'>尤宜春水满，水石更殊怪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6120'>长山势回合，井邑相萦带。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6120'>石林绕舜祠，西南正相对。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6120'>阶庭无争讼，郊境罢守卫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6120_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6120'>时时溪上来，劝引<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_6120", 6120, id='poem_sentence_1_6121'>每到潓泉上，情性可安舒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6121_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6121'>草堂在<span class='link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a>　在道州刺史任上，游石鱼湖，有诗。作品：《石鱼湖上作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：永泰、大历间结在道州任内作。）</span>《石鱼湖上醉歌》<span target='_blank'>石鱼湖上作</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6068")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6068_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6068'>潓泉南上有独石在水中，状如游鱼，鱼凹处，修之可以贝居（案：姜鱼切。）酒。水涯四匝，多攲石相连，石上堪人坐。水能浮小舫载酒，又能绕石鱼洄流，乃命湖曰石鱼湖。镌铭于湖上，显示来者，又作诗以歌之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6068'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6068'>吾爱石鱼湖，石鱼在湖里。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6068'>鱼背有酒樽，绕鱼是湖水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6068'>儿童作小舫，载酒胜一杯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6068'>座中令酒舫，空去复满来。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6068'>湖岸多欹石，石下流寒泉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6068'>醉中一盥漱，快意无比焉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6068'>金玉吾不须，轩冕吾不爱。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6068'>且欲坐湖畔，石鱼长相对。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6068'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_6068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6068'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6068)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_6069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6069?labeling=true' target='_blank'>石鱼湖上醉歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6069")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6069_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6069'>漫叟以公田米酿酒，因休暇则载酒于湖上，时取一醉。欢醉中，据湖岸，引臂向鱼取酒，使舫载之。遍饮坐者，意疑倚巴丘酌于君山之上，诸子环洞庭而坐，酒舫泛泛然触波涛而往来者，乃作歌以长之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6069_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6069'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6069'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_6069", 6069, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>石鱼湖</span>，似洞庭，夏水欲满君山青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6069'>山为樽，水为沼，酒徒历历坐洲岛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6069'>长风连日作大浪，不能废人运酒舫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6106_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6063?labeling=true' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a>　在道州刺史任上，有诗。作品：《潓阳亭作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：永泰、大历间结在道州任内作。）</span>《夜宴石鱼湖上作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：永泰、大历间结在道州任内作。）</span><div id='poem_6140' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6140' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6140?labeling=true' id='poem_preface_6140'>初得潓泉，则为亭于泉上，因开檐霤，又得石渠，泉渠相宜，亭更加好，以亭在泉北，故命之曰潓阳亭。</div><div id='poem_preface_6140_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6140'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6140'>问吾常宴息，泉上何处好。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6140'>独有潓阳亭，令人可终老。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6140'>前轩临潓泉，凭几漱清流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6140'>外物自相扰，渊渊还复休。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6140'>有时出东户，更欲檐下坐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6140'>非我意不行，石渠能留我。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6140'>峰石若鳞次，欹垂复旋回。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6140'>为我引潓泉，泠泠檐下来。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6140'>天寒宜泉温，泉寒宜天暑。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6140'>谁到潓阳亭，其心肯思去。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6140_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6140'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_6140_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_6100' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6100?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夜宴石鱼湖作</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6100")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6100'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6100'>风霜虽惨然，出游熙天正<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作晴）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6100'>登临日暮归，置酒湖上亭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6100'>高烛照泉深，光华溢轩楹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6100'>如见海底日，曈曈始欲生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6100'>夜寒闭窗户，石溜何清泠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6100'>若在深洞中，半崖闻水声。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6100'>醉人疑舫影，呼指递相惊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6100'>何故有双鱼，随吾酒舫行。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6100'>醉昏能诞语，劝醉能忘情。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6100'>坐无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_6100", 6100, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>拘忌</span>人，勿限醉与醒。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6100'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_6100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6100'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6100)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a>　在道州刺史任上，有文。作品：《浯溪铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：疑大历元年、二年间作。）</span>《峿台铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：6月15日刻石，在祁阳。铭或为本年春间道经祁阳时所作。）</span><div id='poem_1367558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367558?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浯溪铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367558")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367558_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367558'>浯溪在湘水之南。北汇于湘。爱其胜异。遂家溪畔。溪世无名称者也。为自爱之。故命浯溪。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367558'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367558'>湘水一曲，渊洄傍山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367558'>山开石门，溪流潺潺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367558'>山开如何，巉巉双石。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367558'>临渊断崖，夹溪绝壁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367558'>水实殊怪，石又尤异。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367558'>吾欲求退，将老兹地。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367558'>溪古地荒，芜没已久。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1367558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1367558'>命曰浯溪，旌吾独有。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1367558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1367558'>人谁知之，铭在溪口。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1367558_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1367558'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1367558_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1367560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>峿台铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367560")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367560_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367560'>浯溪东北二十馀丈。得怪石焉。周行三百馀步。从未申至丑寅。厓壁斗绝。左属回鲜。前有磴道。高八九十尺。下当洄潭。其势碅磳。半出水底。苍然泛泛。若在波上。石巅胜异之处。悉为亭堂。小峰歁窦。宜间松竹。掩映轩户。毕皆幽奇。于戏。古人有蓄愤闷与病于时俗者。力不能筑高台以瞻眺。则必山巅海畔。伸颈歌吟。以自畅达。今取兹石。将为峿台。盖非愁怨。乃所好也。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367560'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367560'>湘渊清深，峿台峭𡺿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367560'>登临长望，无远不尽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367560'>谁厌朝市，羁牵局促。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367560'>借君此台，一纵心目。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367560'>阳厓砻琢，如瑾如珉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367560'>作铭刻之，彰示后人。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367560_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367560'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1367560_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年</a>　冬次第近作合于旧编凡二百三首曰《文编》作品：《文编序》<div id='poem_1367530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367530?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文编序</a><span class='authorDate'>（767年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367530")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367530_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367530'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367530'>天宝十二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367530_comment'></div>漫叟以进士获荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367530_comment'></div>名在礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367530_comment'></div>会有司考校旧文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367530_comment'></div>作文编纳于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367530_comment'></div>当时叟方年少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367530_comment'></div>在显名迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367530_comment'></div>切耻时人谄邪以取进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367530_comment'></div>奸乱以致身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367530_comment'></div>径欲填陷阱于方正之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367530_comment'></div>推时人于礼让之庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367530_comment'></div>不能得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367530_comment'></div>故优游于林壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367530_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1367530", 1367530, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>怏恨</span>于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367530_comment'></div>是以所为之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367530_comment'></div>可戒可劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367530_comment'></div>可安可顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367530_comment'></div>侍郎杨公见文编叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367530_comment'></div>以上第污元子耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367530_comment'></div>有司得元子是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367530_comment'></div>叟少师友仲行公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367530_comment'></div>公闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367530_comment'></div>谕叟曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367530_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367530_comment'></div>吾尝恐直道绝而不续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367530_comment'></div>不虞杨公于子相续如缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367530_comment'></div>明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367530_comment'></div>有司于都堂策问群士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367530_comment'></div>叟竟在上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367530_comment'></div>尔来十五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367530_comment'></div>更经丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367530_comment'></div>所望全活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367530_comment'></div>岂欲迹参戎旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367530_comment'></div>苟在冠冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367530_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1367530", 1367530, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>触践</span>危机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367530_comment'></div>以为荣利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367530_comment'></div>盖辞谢不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367530_comment'></div>未能逃命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367530_comment'></div>故所为之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367530_comment'></div>多退让者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367530_comment'></div>多激发者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367530_comment'></div>多嗟恨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367530_comment'></div>多伤闵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367530_comment'></div>其意必欲劝之忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367530_comment'></div>诱以仁惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367530_comment'></div>急于公直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367530_comment'></div>守其节分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1367530_comment'></div>如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1367530_comment'></div>非救时劝俗之所须者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1367530_comment'></div>叟在此州今五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1367530_comment'></div>地偏事简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1367530_comment'></div>得以文史自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1367530_comment'></div>乃<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1367530", 1367530, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>次第</span>近作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1367530_comment'></div>合于旧编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1367530_comment'></div>凡二百三首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1367530_comment'></div>分为十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1367530_comment'></div>复命曰文编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1367530_comment'></div>示门人子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1367530_comment'></div>可传之于筐箧耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1367530_comment'></div>叟之命称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1367530_comment'></div>则著于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1367530", 1367530, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>自释</span>云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1367530_comment'></div>不录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1367530_comment'></div>时大历二年丁未中冬也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1367530_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
