-----title
衡阳（衡州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bf0ea1ad7c7040c6a34303c8b542b300_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bf0ea1ad7c7040c6a34303c8b542b300");'><span id='bf0ea1ad7c7040c6a34303c8b542b300_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=766')">765-766年</a>，47-48岁</div><div id='bf0ea1ad7c7040c6a34303c8b542b300' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　夏结罢守道州，赴衡阳，遇故友刘湾。作品：《刘侍御月夜宴会》<div id='poem_6070' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6070' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6070?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘侍御月夜宴会</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6070")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6070_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6070'>兵兴已来，十一年矣，获与同志欢醉达旦，咏歌取适，无一二焉。乙巳岁，彭城刘灵源在衡阳，逢故人或有在者，日昔相会（曰昔相会），第欢远游，始与诸公待月而笑语，竟与诸公爱月而欢醉，咏歌夜久，赋诗言怀。于戏！文章道丧盖久矣！时之作者，烦杂过多，歌儿舞女，且相喜爱，系之风雅，谁道是邪。诸公尝欲变时俗之淫靡，为后生之规范，今夕岂不能道达情性，成一时之美乎？</div><div id='poem_preface_6070_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6070'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6070'>我从苍梧来，将耕旧山田。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6070'>踟蹰为故人，且复停归船。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6070'>日夕得相从，转觉和乐全。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6070'>愚爱凉风来，明月正满天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6070'>河汉望不见，几星犹粲然。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6070'>中夜兴欲酣，改坐临清川。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6070'>未醉恐天旦，更歌促繁弦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6070'>欢娱不可逢，请君莫言旋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6070_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6070'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_6070_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　孟士源镇湖南将二岁，是夏建茅阁，结为作诗。作品：《题孟中丞茅阁诗》<div id='poem_6141' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6141' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6141?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题孟中丞茅阁</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6141")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6141_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6141'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6141'>小山为郡城，随水能萦纡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6141'>亭亭最高处，今是西南隅。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6141'>杉大老犹在，苍苍数十株。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6141'>垂阴满城上，枝叶何扶疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6141'>乃知四海中，遗事谁谓无。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6141'>及观茅阁成，始觉形胜殊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6141'>凭轩望熊湘，云榭连苍梧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6141'>天下正炎热，此然冰雪俱。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6141'>客有在中坐，颂歌复何如。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6141'>公欲举<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_6141", 6141, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>遗材</span>，如此佳木欤。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6141'>公方庇苍生，又如斯阁乎。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6141'>请达谣颂声，愿公且踟蹰。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6141_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6141'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_6141_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　孟士源镇湖南将二岁，是夏建茅阁，有文。作品：《茅阁记》<div id='poem_1367539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>茅阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367539")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367539_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367539'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367539'>己已中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367539_comment'></div>平昌孟公镇湖南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367539_comment'></div>将二岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367539_comment'></div>以威惠理戎旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367539_comment'></div>以简易肃州县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367539_comment'></div>刑政之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367539_comment'></div>则无挠人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367539_comment'></div>故居方多闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367539_comment'></div>时与宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367539_comment'></div>尝欲因高引望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367539_comment'></div>以抒远怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367539_comment'></div>偶爱古木数株。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367539_comment'></div>垂覆城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367539_comment'></div>遂作茅阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367539_comment'></div>荫其清阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367539_comment'></div>长风寥寥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367539_comment'></div>入我轩槛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367539_comment'></div>扇和爽气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367539_comment'></div>满于阁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367539_comment'></div>世传衡阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367539_comment'></div>暑湿郁蒸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367539_comment'></div>休息于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367539_comment'></div>何为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367539_comment'></div>今天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367539_comment'></div>正苦大热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367539_comment'></div>谁似茅阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367539_comment'></div>荫而庥之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367539_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367539_comment'></div>贤人君子为苍生之庥荫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367539_comment'></div>不如是邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367539_comment'></div>诸公咏歌以美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367539_comment'></div>俾茅阁之什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367539_comment'></div>得系嗣于风雅者矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1367539_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　潭州刺史崔灌去官，结为之作表。作品：《崔潭州表》<div id='poem_1367620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>崔潭州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367620")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367620'>乙已岁。潭州刺史崔瓘去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367620_comment'></div>州人衡州司功参军郑浰为乡人某等请余为崔公作表。公前在澧州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367620_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1367620", 1367620, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>谣颂</span>之声。达于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367620_comment'></div>褒异之诏。与人为程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367620_comment'></div>及领此州在今日。能使孤寡老弱无悲忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367620_comment'></div>单贫困穷安其乡。富豪强家无利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367620_comment'></div>贾人就食之类。各得其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367620_comment'></div>职役供给。不匮人而当于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367620_comment'></div>若非清廉而信。正直而仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367620_comment'></div>则不能。至于观察御史中丞孟公奏课又第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367620_comment'></div>会国家以犬戎为虞。未即徵拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367620_comment'></div>使苍生正暍而去其庥荫。使苍生正渴而敝其清源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367620_comment'></div>时艰道远。州人等不得诣阙冤诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367620_comment'></div>且欲刻石立表。以彰盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367620_comment'></div>呜呼。刺史有土官也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367620_comment'></div>千里之内。品形之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367620_comment'></div>不亦多乎。岂可令凶竖暴类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367620_comment'></div>贪夫奸党。以货权家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367620_comment'></div>而至此官。如崔公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367620_comment'></div>岂独真刺史耶。郑浰之为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367620_comment'></div>岂苟媚其君而私于州里耶。盖惧清廉正直之道溺于时俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367620_comment'></div>君子遗爱之心不显来世。故采其意而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367620_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1367620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　户部员外郎何倡裕收赋到江湖，赠结皮弁，结作书谢焉。作品：《与何员外书》<div id='poem_1367528' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367528' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367528?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与何员外书</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367528")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367528_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367528'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367528'>月日。次山白何夫子执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367528_comment'></div>皮弁时俗废之久矣。非好古君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367528_comment'></div>谁能存之。忽蒙见赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367528_comment'></div>惊喜无喻。次山漫浪者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367528_comment'></div>苦不爱便事之服时世之巾。昔年在山野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367528_comment'></div>曾作愚巾凡裘。异于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1367528", 1367528, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>制度</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367528_comment'></div>凡裘领缁界缁缘缁带。其馀皆褐带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367528_comment'></div>联后缝中。腰前系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367528_comment'></div>愚巾顶方带方垂方。缁葛为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367528_comment'></div>元丝为缕。次山自衣带巾裘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367528_comment'></div>虽不为时人大恶。亦尝辱其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1367528", 1367528, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>嗤诮</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367528_comment'></div>方欲杂古人衣带以自免辱。赠及皮弁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367528_comment'></div>与凡裘正相宜。若风霜惨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367528_comment'></div>出行林野。次山则戴皮弁衣凡裘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367528_comment'></div>若大暑蒸湿。出见宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367528_comment'></div>次山则戴愚巾衣野服。野服大抵缁褐布葛为之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367528_comment'></div>腰担为裳。短襟为衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367528_comment'></div>裳下及履。衣垂及膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367528_comment'></div>不审夫子异时归休。适在山野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367528_comment'></div>能衣戴此者不乎。若以为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367528_comment'></div>当各造一副送往。元次山白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367528_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1367528_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　结与户部员外郎何倡裕醉欢将别有诗。作品：《别何员外》<div id='poem_6071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别何员外</a><span class='authorDate'>（765年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6071")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6071'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6071'>谁能守清躅，谁能嗣世儒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6071'>吾见何君饶，为人有是夫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6071'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_6071", 6071, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>黜官</span>二十年，未曾暂崎岖。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6071'>终不病贫贱，寥寥无所拘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6071'>忽然逢知己，数月领官符。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6071'>犹是尚书郎，收赋来江湖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6071'>人皆悉苍生，随意极所须。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6071'>比盗无兵甲，似偷又不如。<div id='poem_sentence_7_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_6071'>公能独宽大，使之力自输。<div id='poem_sentence_8_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_6071'>吾欲探时谣，为公伏奏书。<div id='poem_sentence_9_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_6071'>但恐抵忌讳，未知肯听无。<div id='poem_sentence_10_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_6071'>不然且相送，醉欢于坐隅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_6071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_6071'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_6071_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　校书郎孟云卿将赴南海，结作诗以送之。作品：《送孟校书往南海》<div id='poem_6105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_6105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/6105?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送孟校书往南海<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序。一作别孟校书。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_6105")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_6105_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_6105'>平昌孟云卿，与元次山同州里，以词学相友。几二十年，次山今罢守舂陵，云卿始典校芸阁。于戏！材业次山不如云卿，词赋次山不如云卿，通和次山不如云卿，在次山又诩然求进者也。谁言时命，吾欲听之，次山今且未老，云卿少次山六七岁。云卿声名满天下，知己在朝廷，及次山之年，云卿何事不可至。勿随长风，乘兴蹈海，勿爱罗浮，往而不归。南海幕府，有乐安任鸿，与次山最旧，请任公为次山一白府主，趣资装云卿使北归，慎勿令徘徊海上，诸公第作歌送之。</div><div id='poem_preface_6105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_6105'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_6105'>吾闻近南海，乃是魑魅乡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_6105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_6105'>忽见孟夫子，欢然游此方。<div id='poem_sentence_1_6105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_6105'>忽喜海风来，海帆又欲张。<div id='poem_sentence_2_6105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_6105'>漂漂随所去，不念归路长。<div id='poem_sentence_3_6105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_6105'>君有失母儿，爱之似<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_6105", 6105, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>阿阳</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_6105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_6105'>始解随人行，不欲离君傍。<div id='poem_sentence_5_6105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_6105'>相劝早旋归，此言慎勿忘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_6105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_6105'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_6105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_6105'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(6105)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>

梧州

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年4月</a>　结以老母身病不堪远行，乞停所授，有文。作品：《让容州表》<div id='poem_1367507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让容州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（768年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367507")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367507'>臣结言。臣伏奉今月二十二日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367507_comment'></div>授臣使持节都督容州诸军事守容州刺史御史中丞充本管经略守捉使。四月十六日敕到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367507_comment'></div>二十一日发付本道行营。臣实愚弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367507_comment'></div>谬当寄任。奉诏之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367507_comment'></div>不辞忧惧。臣结中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367507_comment'></div>臣闻孝于家者忠于国。以事君者无所隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367507_comment'></div>臣有至切。不敢不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367507_comment'></div>臣实一身。奉养老母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367507_comment'></div>医药饮食。非臣不喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367507_comment'></div>臣暂违离。则忧悸成疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367507_comment'></div>臣又多病。近日加剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367507_comment'></div>前在道州。黾勉六岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367507_comment'></div>实无政理。多是假名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367507_comment'></div>频请停官。使司不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367507_comment'></div>今臣所属之州。陷贼岁久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367507_comment'></div>颓城古木。远在炎荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367507_comment'></div>管内诸州。多未<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1367507", 1367507, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>宾伏</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367507_comment'></div>行营野次。向十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367507_comment'></div>在臣一身。为国展效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367507_comment'></div>死当不避。敢惮艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367507_comment'></div>但以老母念臣。疾疹日久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367507_comment'></div>时方大暑。南逾火山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367507_comment'></div>举家漂泊。寄在湖上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367507_comment'></div>单车将命。赴于贼庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367507_comment'></div>臣将就路。老母悲泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367507_comment'></div>闻者悽怆。臣心可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367507_comment'></div>臣欲扶持版舆。南之合浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367507_comment'></div>则老母气力。艰于远行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367507_comment'></div>臣欲奋不顾家。则母子之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367507_comment'></div>禽畜犹有。臣欲久辞老母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367507_comment'></div>则又污辱名教。臣欲便不之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367507_comment'></div>又恐稽违诏命。在臣肝肠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367507_comment'></div>如煎如灼。昔徐庶心乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367507_comment'></div>先主不逼。令伯陈情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367507_comment'></div>晋武允许。君臣国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367507_comment'></div>万代为规。伏惟陛下以孝理万姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367507_comment'></div>慈育生类。在臣情志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367507_comment'></div>实堪矜悯。臣每读前史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367507_comment'></div>见吴起游宦。噬臂不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367507_comment'></div>温峤奉使。绝裾而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367507_comment'></div>常恨不逢斯人。使之殊死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367507_comment'></div>臣所以冒犯圣旨。乞停今授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367507_comment'></div>待罪私门。长得奉养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367507_comment'></div>供给井税。臣之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1367507", 1367507, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>恳愿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367507_comment'></div>尘黩天威。不胜惶恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367507_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1367507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年4月</a>　结理容州，实寄理于梧州，单车入于夷庭，亲自抚喻，六旬而收复八州。作品：《冰井铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：《寰宇记》载：冰泉在城，一郡人民皆饮此水，唐大历三年容州经略使元结撰《冰泉铭》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年闰8月9日</a>　林云刻结《（广吾）庼铭》，在祁阳。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：《（广吾）庼铭》文或于大历三年前作。）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f26f2af1e97f40e0b29925c63a71f555_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f26f2af1e97f40e0b29925c63a71f555");'><span id='f26f2af1e97f40e0b29925c63a71f555_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=771')">769-771年</a>，51-53岁</div><div id='f26f2af1e97f40e0b29925c63a71f555' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年4月13日</a>　结寄住永州。敕命起复结守金吾卫将军、员外置司正员、兼御史中丞使持节都督容州诸军事兼容州刺史充本管经略守捉使，赐紫金鱼袋。结丁母优作《再让容州表》，许之。<div id='poem_1367508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367508?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再让容州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（769年4月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367508")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1367508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367508'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367508'>草土臣结言。伏奉四月十三日敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1367508_comment'></div>以臣前在容州。殊有理政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1367508_comment'></div>使司乞留。以遂人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1367508_comment'></div>起复臣守金吾卫将军员外置同正员兼御史中丞使持节都督容州诸军事兼容州刺史充本管经略守捉使。赐紫金鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1367508_comment'></div>忽奉恩诏。心魂惊悸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1367508_comment'></div>哀慕悲感。不任忧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1367508_comment'></div>臣某中谢。臣闻苟伤礼法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1367508_comment'></div>妄蒙寄任。古人所畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1367508_comment'></div>臣敢不惧。国家近年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1367508_comment'></div>切恶薄俗。文官忧免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1367508_comment'></div>许终丧制。臣素非战士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1367508_comment'></div>曾忝台省。墨缞戎旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1367508_comment'></div>实伤礼法。且容府陷没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1367508_comment'></div>十二三年。管内诸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1367508_comment'></div>多在贼境。臣前行营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1367508_comment'></div>日月甚浅。宣布圣泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1367508_comment'></div>远人未知。有何政能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1367508_comment'></div>得在人口。使司过听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1367508_comment'></div>误有请留。遂令朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1367508_comment'></div>隳紊法禁。至使愚弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1367508_comment'></div>秽污礼教。臣实不敢践古人可畏之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1367508_comment'></div>辱圣朝委任之命。敢以死请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1367508_comment'></div>乞追恩诏。前者陛下授臣容州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1367508_comment'></div>臣正任道州刺史。臣身病母老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1367508_comment'></div>不敢辞谢。实为道州地安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1367508_comment'></div>数年禄养。容州破陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1367508_comment'></div>不宜辞避。臣以为安食其禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1367508_comment'></div>蹈危不免。此乃人臣之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1367508_comment'></div>其时臣便奉表陈乞。以母老地远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1367508_comment'></div>请解职任。陛下察臣恳至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1367508_comment'></div>追臣入朝。臣以为不贻忧叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1367508_comment'></div>荣及膝下。人子之分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1367508_comment'></div>不图恩敕未到。臣丁酷罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1367508_comment'></div>哀号冤怨。无所迨及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1367508_comment'></div>今陛下又夺臣情。礼授容州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1367508_comment'></div>臣遂行则亡母旅榇。归葬无日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1367508_comment'></div>几筵漂寄。奠祀无主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1367508_comment'></div>捧读诏书。不胜悲惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1367508_comment'></div>臣旧患风疾。近转增剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1367508_comment'></div>荒忽迷忘。不自知觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1367508_comment'></div>馀生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1367508", 1367508, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>残喘</span>。朝夕殒灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1367508_comment'></div>岂堪金革。能伏叛人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1367508_comment'></div>特乞圣慈。允臣所请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1367508_comment'></div>收臣新授官诰。令臣终丧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1367508_comment'></div>免生死羞愧。是臣恳愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1367508_comment'></div>臣今寄住永州。请刺史王庭璬为臣进表陈乞以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1367508_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1367508_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年</a>　结大历四年至大历七年正月前家居丁母优。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年</a>　号其居曰“漫郎宅”。结有《右堂铭》刻石祁阳浯溪。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：《右堂铭》未见，疑已逸。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年6月</a>　号其居曰“漫郎宅”。结上元中所撰《中兴颂》刻石祁阳浯溪石崖上，俗谓《摩崖碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年6月</a>　号其居曰“漫郎宅”。结有《中堂铭》刻石在祁阳。<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品系年：《中堂明》今逸。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年6月</a>　号其居曰“漫郎宅”。结有《东崖铭》刻石在祁阳，不记年月，疑家浯溪时所作。<div id='poem_1367561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东崖铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367561")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367561_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367561'>峿台西面。㩻㪁高迥。在亭为东崖。下可行坐八九人。其为形胜与石门石屏。亦犹宫羽之相资也。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367561'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367561'>峿台苍苍，西崖云端。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367561'>亭午崖下，清阴更寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367561'>可容枕席，何事不安。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367561_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367561'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1367561_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年6月</a>　号其居曰“漫郎宅”。结有《寒泉铭》刻石在祁阳，不记年月，疑家浯溪时所作。<div id='poem_1367562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1367562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1367562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寒泉铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(12931, "唐", "元结", "poem_title_1367562")'>元结</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1367562_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1367562'>湘江西峰。直平阳江口。有寒泉出于石穴。峰上有老木。寿藤垂阴泉上。近泉堪戙维大舟。惜其蒙蔽。不可得见。踟蹰行循。其水本无名称也。为其当暑大寒。故命曰寒泉。铭曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1367562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1367562'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1367562'>于戏寒泉，瀛瀛江湄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1367562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1367562'>堪救<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1367562", 1367562, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>渴暍</span>，人不之知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1367562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1367562'>当时大暑，江流若汤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1367562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1367562'>寒泉一掬，能清心肠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1367562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1367562'>谁谓仁惠，不在兹水。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1367562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1367562'>舟楫尚存，为利未已。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1367562_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1367562'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1367562_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
